Zheng,T. Zhou,X. Zhou,Y. Zhou,V. Zhovkovska,L. Z. Zhu,X. Zhu,X. Zhu,Y. Zhu,V. Zhukov,J. Zhuo,D. Zuliani*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用LHCb探测器在质心能量13 TeV的质子-质子对撞中，首次测量了前向快度区关联Z玻色子与瞬发J/ψ粒子的产生截面，发现其远超单部分子散射（single-parton scattering）预期，表明多部分子相互作用（multiparton interactions）主导该过程，并提取出有效截面σ_eff = 16.6 ± 4.7 mb，为质子横向空间结构提供了直接实验约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 关联Z玻色子与J/ψ的产生过程对多部分子相互作用敏感，但此前缺乏前向快度区（forward rapidity region）的实验数据，尤其是在同时具有小Bjorken-x和电弱硬尺度（由Z玻色子质量设定）的运动学区域中，质子横向空间结构尚未得到直接约束。

Method: 利用LHCb探测器在2016至2018年采集的质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度5.1 fb⁻¹），在质心能量√s = 13 TeV的前向快度区测量关联Z玻色子与瞬发J/ψ的产生；将测量结果与单部分子散射（single-parton scattering）预期进行比较，并在标准双部分子散射（double-parton scattering）框架下提取有效截面σ_eff。

Result: 测量得到的赝截面（fiducial cross-section）为5.5 ± 1.5 pb，显著高于单部分子散射预期值0.10 ± 0.08 pb；在双部分子散射解释下得到有效截面σ_eff = 16.6 ± 4.7 mb。

Conclusion: 该结果表明多部分子相互作用（multiparton interactions）在前向快度区主导关联Z+J/ψ过程，所提取的σ_eff为质子横向空间结构在同时包含小Bjorken-x和电弱硬尺度的运动学区域中提供了直接的实验约束。

Abstract: This letter reports a study of associated $Z$ boson and prompt $J/ψ$ production in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV with the LHCb detector in the forward rapidity region, using a data sample taken during 2016 to 2018 corresponding to an integrated luminosity of $5.1 \mathrm{fb}^{-1}$. The measured fiducial cross-section is $5.5 \pm 1.5$ pb, significantly exceeding the single-parton scattering expectation of $0.10 \pm 0.08$ pb, indicating that multiparton interactions dominate this process in the explored phase space. Interpreted within the standard double-parton scattering framework, the data yields an effective cross-section $σ_{\mathrm{eff}} = 16.6 \pm 4.7$ mb. This provides a direct experimental constraint on the transverse spatial structure of the proton in a kinematic regime characterized simultaneously by small Bjorken-$x$ and an electroweak hard scale set by the $Z$ boson mass.

*Lucas Russell*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确测量希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）的物理性质是检验标准模型（Standard Model, SM）以及探索新物理的关键途径。

Method: 基于LHC上ATLAS和CMS探测器记录的$\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV及$\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV质子-质子对撞数据，通过$H\to\gamma\gamma$和$H\to WW^*$等衰变道进行事例重建与统计推断。

Result: CMS合作组给出了$H\to\gamma\gamma$道中的希格斯玻色子质量与宽度测量结果，以及$H\to WW^*$末态中的宽度测量结果。ATLAS合作组报告了对希格斯-矢量玻色子耦合的电荷宇称（charge-parity, CP）性质的联合测量。此外，CMS合作组报告了对希格斯-τ轻子汤川耦合（Yukawa coupling）CP结构的最新分析。

Conclusion: 两项实验在多个衰变道中均取得了改进的测量结果，为精确检验希格斯玻色子的标准模型预言提供了最新的实验约束。

Abstract: Recent measurements of Higgs boson properties using proton-proton collision data recorded at $\sqrt{s}=13$ TeV and $\sqrt{s}=13.6$ TeV with the ATLAS and CMS detectors at the LHC are presented. CMS results on the Higgs boson mass and width in the $H\toγγ$ channel are reported, together with a measurement of the Higgs boson width in the $H\to WW^*$ final state. A combined measurement of the charge-parity (CP) nature of the Higgs-vector boson couplings by the ATLAS collaboration, as well as improved results in individual channels by both experiments are summarised. Finally, the latest CMS analysis of the CP structure of the Higgs-tau lepton Yukawa coupling is reported.

### [3] [Mountain Muography for China Jinping Underground Laboratory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06029)
*Xinshun Zhang,Shaomin Chen,Wei Dou,Haoyang Fu,Lei Guo,Ziyi Guo,XiangPan Ji,Jianmin Li,Jinjing Li,Bo Liang,Ye Liang,Qian Liu,Wentai Luo,Ming Qi,Wenhui Shao,Haozhe Sun,Jian Tang,Yuyi Wang,Zhe Wang,Changxu Wei,Jun Weng,Yiyang Wu,Benda Xu,Chuang Xu,Tong Xu,Tao Xue,Haoyan Yang,Yuzi Yang,Aiqiang Zhang,Bin Zhang,Yang Zhang,Zhicai Zhang,Lin Zhao,Yangheng Zheng*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了在中国锦屏地下实验室（CJPL）——世界最深和最大的地下设施之一——首次开展的深层μ子成像（muography）实验。通过利用锦屏中微子实验的一吨级原型探测器，在约2400米深处对3公里横向范围内的上覆岩层密度结构进行了非侵入式成像，重建的方向不透明度图与卫星地形模型高度吻合。该工作验证了在千米级上覆岩层极端深度下开展μ子成像的可行性，并为锦屏二期（CJPL-II）八个实验厅的总μ子通量提供了预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深层地下实验室（如CJPL）为暗物质、中微子等低本底物理实验提供了理想环境，但上覆岩层的精确密度结构对于评估宇宙线μ子背景至关重要。此前在如此极端深度（约2400米）下的大尺度μ子成像尚未开展。因此，需验证深层μ子成像（muography）的可行性，并建立一种非侵入性的地质密度探测方法，以支撑未来实验的物理设计。

Method: 利用锦屏中微子实验的一吨级原型探测器（直径1.3米，近各向同性接收度，角分辨率约4.5°），在CJPL中检测宇宙线μ子。通过将预测的地表μ子通量分布与地下测量数据进行关联，重建了方向不透明度图（directional opacity map），进而约束上覆岩层的密度结构。

Result: 重建的方向不透明度图与卫星导出的地形模型（satellite-derived terrain models）具有极好的一致性，验证了该成像方法在极端深度下的有效性。基于验证后的上覆岩层模型，进一步预测了CJPL-II全部八个实验厅的总μ子通量。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在千米级上覆岩层的极端深度下进行μ子成像的可行性，并建立了一套稳健的方法论。该成果不仅可用于未来地球物理学应用，也为锦屏全规模中微子实验等大型设施的物理方案提供了关键的μ子背景输入。

Abstract: The China Jinping Underground Laboratory (CJPL), located $\sim 2,400$~m beneath Jinping Mountain, is one of the world's deepest and largest ($\sim 300{,}000~\mathrm{m}^3$) underground facilities, hosting dark matter, nuclear astrophysics, and neutrino experiments. We report the first muon radiography (muography) conducted at this extraordinary depth. Cosmic muons detected by a one-ton prototype developed for the Jinping Neutrino Experiment were used to perform non-invasive subsurface density mapping over a 3~km lateral range. The 1.3~m diameter detector provides nearly isotropic acceptance and an angular resolution of $\sim 4.5^\circ$. By correlating the predicted surface muon flux distributions with the underground measurements, we reconstruct a directional opacity map that constrains the density structure of the overburden and shows excellent agreement with satellite-derived terrain models. This work demonstrates the feasibility of muography at extreme depths with kilometer-scale overburden and establishes a robust methodology for future geophysical applications and large-scale facilities, such as the full Jinping Neutrino Experiment. Based on this validated overburden model, we further predict the total muon fluxes for the eight experimental halls in CJPL-II, providing essential input for their physics programs.

TL;DR: 本文报告了在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA第四次观测运行期间，对LIGO探测器数据中窄带频谱伪影（narrow spectral artifacts）的识别、表征与缓解工作。研究更新并部署了关键软件工具以支持数据监测与调查，成功识别并缓解了多个窄带噪声源。减少含非天体物理伪影的频率带数量，对于最大化窄带持续性引力波（narrowband persistent gravitational waves）的探测潜力至关重要。

Method: 针对第四次LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA观测运行，更新了关键软件工具并部署了新工具，以支持噪声调查与实时数据监测。研究团队利用这些工具对LIGO数据中的窄带伪影进行了系统性的识别与表征。

Conclusion: 最小化含有非天体物理伪影的频率带数量，对于最大化发现新型引力波信号（gravitational-wave signals）的潜力至关重要。

Abstract: We present efforts to identify, characterize, and mitigate narrow spectral artifacts in LIGO detector data during the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run. Narrow spectral artifacts in gravitational-wave detectors are non-astrophysical noise sources that can degrade searches for narrowband persistent gravitational waves. Identifying and, where possible, mitigating these noise sources is one of the core efforts of the LIGO Detector Characterization group. Key software tools have been updated and new tools deployed for the fourth LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA observing run to facilitate investigations and data monitoring. We discuss these tool upgrades, and present several identified narrowband artifacts that have been successfully investigated and mitigated in LIGO data. Regardless of whether artifacts are mitigated or not, narrowband persistent gravitational-wave searches require information on which frequency bands contain non-astrophysical artifacts. Minimizing the number of bands containing non-astrophysical artifacts is essential to maximize the potential for discovery of a new class of gravitational-wave signals.

### [5] [Sensitivity Limits and Operational Threshold Calibration for DINOv2-based Gravitational-Wave Glitch Characterization: A Strain-Domain Mock Data Challenge on LIGO O4a](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06237)
*Luca Cirfeta*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本论文通过一项模拟数据挑战（Mock Data Challenge, MDC）系统地表征了 gravi-signal-ml 流水线（Cirfeta 2026）在无监督引力波毛刺（glitch）探测中的灵敏度极限。研究发现，在统计严格的运行阈值下，该流水线对所有八种注入形态在测试信噪比（SNR）范围内召回率（Recall）均为 0，根本原因在于 DINOv2 [CLS] 令牌的全局平均池化（global average pooling）稀释了仅占据频谱图小块区域（<5%）的信号。该结果表明 Cirfeta (2026) 的零结果应被条件性地重新解释：它确认了无新型宏观结构，但无法排除局域化微观结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作（Cirfeta 2026）在应用基于视觉 Transformer（Vision Transformer, ViT）的无监督流水线 gravi-signal-ml 进行引力波毛刺探测时报告了零结果，但其灵敏度极限及失效原因尚未被系统地表征。本研究旨在通过受控注入实验定量评估该流水线的探测能力边界，并识别导致探测失败的根本机制。

Method: 本研究构建了包含八种形态族的应变域（strain-domain）合成注入数据集，将其嵌入公开 LIGO O4a L1 数据；采用 session 自适应动态阈值（tau_dyn = mu_bg - 2.5 * sigma_bg）和统计严格运行阈值（tau_op = 0.874，校准于经验 5x10^-5 分位数）两种阈值方案评估流水线性能；并对完整的 O4a 嵌入分布（N = 188,142 段）进行了非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）表征，使用广义极值分布（Generalized Extreme Value, GEV）对左尾进行建模。

Result: 在 session 自适应动态阈值下，流水线对视觉各向异性形态（Butterfly, ZSweep）在匹配滤波信噪比（matched-filter SNR）≥70 时达到 Recall = 1.0，但假阳性率（False Positive Rate, FPR）未受控。在统计严格运行阈值下，所有八种形态在所有测试 SNR 水平（包括 SNR 高达 430 的窄带和脉冲瞬变）的 Recall 均为 0。完整 O4a 嵌入分布呈现极端非高斯性（偏度 skewness = -4.12，超额峰度 excess kurtosis = 15.38，Shapiro-Wilk p 值接近 0）。

Conclusion: 本研究的核心结论是：gravi-signal-ml 流水线的探测盲区源于 DINOv2 [CLS] 令牌的全局平均池化对局域化信号的稀释效应；Cirfeta (2026) 的零结果应被条件性地重新解释为仅能排除新型宏观结构，而不能排除局域化微观结构。这些发现为下一代基于 ViT 的流水线提供了定量路线图，建议采用分块级评分（patch-level scoring）和多尺度窗口化（multi-scale windowing）策略。

Abstract: We present a Mock Data Challenge (MDC) to characterize the sensitivity limits of the gravi-signal-ml pipeline (Cirfeta 2026) for unsupervised gravitational-wave glitch detection. Strain-domain synthetic injections of eight morphological families into public LIGO O4a L1 data reveal two threshold-dependent sensitivity regimes. With a session-adaptive dynamic threshold (tau_dyn = mu_bg - 2.5 * sigma_bg), the pipeline recovers visually anisotropic morphologies (Butterfly, ZSweep) at matched-filter SNR >= 70, reaching Recall = 1.0, though the False Positive Rate (FPR) remains uncontrolled across sessions. Characterization of the full O4a embedding distribution (N = 188,142 segments) reveals extreme non-Gaussianity (skewness = -4.12, excess kurtosis = 15.38, Shapiro-Wilk p-value near 0), with the left tail best modeled by a Generalized Extreme Value (GEV) distribution. Under a statistically rigorous operational threshold (tau_op = 0.874) calibrated at the empirical 5x10^-5 quantile (FPR < 0.01%), the MDC yields Recall = 0 for all eight morphologies at all tested SNR levels, including narrowband structures (HarmonicComb, NarrowChirp) and impulsive transients (AsymBlip) at SNR up to 430. We trace this insensitivity to the global average pooling of the DINOv2 [CLS] token, which dilutes signals occupying a small fraction (<5%) of the spectrogram's 37x37 patch grid. The null result of Cirfeta (2026) is conditionally reinterpreted: it confirms the absence of novel macro-structures but cannot exclude localized micro-structures. These findings provide a quantitative roadmap for next-generation ViT-based pipelines using patch-level scoring and multi-scale windowing.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [6] [High-Dimensional Theory of LoRA Fine-Tuning in a Solvable Attention Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05899)
*O. Duranthon,F. Boncoraglio,L. Zdeborová*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对注意力模型中的低秩适配（LoRA）建立了一套高维统计理论，揭示了预训练与微调之间的相互作用。通过可解框架，在无限数据预训练与有限数据秩一LoRA微调的场景下，推导出测试误差与表示对齐（representation alignment）的精确渐近刻画，并发现预训练的影响可等效为一个有效噪声项，从而指导最优预训练策略。同时，论文指出了测试误差与表示质量之间存在失配区域，并提出了该理论在主动微调（active fine-tuning）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对LoRA的理论理解尚不充分，尤其缺乏能够刻画预训练与微调之间复杂耦合关系的高维统计理论。本文旨在为LoRA在注意力模型中的行为提供可解析的渐近理论，从而解释预训练如何影响微调效果，并为优化预训练过程提供理论指导。

Method: 本文构建了一个可解的分析框架：首先在数据充裕任务上对单头注意力层（single-head attention layer）进行预训练，随后在有限数据上通过秩一LoRA更新（rank-one LoRA update）进行微调。在高维极限（high-dimensional limit）下，利用一组有限序参量（order parameters）对两个阶段进行锐利渐近刻画，推导测试误差与表示对齐的显式预测。

Result: 分析表明，预训练对LoRA的影响可归纳为一个有效噪声项（effective noise term），据此推导出最优预训练过程的指导原则。实验还发现了测试误差与表示质量之间存在失配（mismatch）的区间，并展示了该理论在主动微调中的应用。

Conclusion: 本文为LoRA在注意力模型中的预训练-微调机制提供了严格的统计理论支撑，揭示了预训练效应的等效噪声形式，并为最优预训练策略与主动微调方法提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a high-dimensional statistical theory of low-rank adaptation (LoRA) in attention models, capturing the interplay between pre-training and fine-tuning. We introduce a solvable framework in which a single-head attention layer is first pre-trained on a data-abundant task and subsequently adapted via a rank-one LoRA update on limited data. In the high-dimensional limit, both stages admit a sharp asymptotic characterization in terms of a finite set of order parameters, yielding explicit predictions for test errors and representation alignment. Our analysis shows that the impact of pre-training on LoRA is summarized by an effective noise term, from which we derive prescriptions for the optimal pre-training procedure. We also demonstrate a regime with a mismatch between the value of the test error and representation quality, and propose an application of our theory to active fine-tuning.

</details>


### [7] [Generative Criticality in Large Language Model Temperature Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06238)
*Huajian Ruan,Jinyang Li,Xingyu Guo,Lingxiao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统计场（statistical-field）框架，将大语言模型（LLM）生成的文本中的词元嵌入（token embedding）视为一维链上的连续自旋变量（continuous spin variable）。通过定义磁化率（susceptibility）和序参量（order parameter），发现随softmax温度T的变化，系统在特征温度T_c附近出现尖锐的磁化率峰、序参量快速变化以及低于T_c时语义方向坍缩（collapse）现象，整体行为类似于连续相变（continuous phase transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏从统计力学（statistical mechanics）视角定量刻画LLM生成文本中集体统计结构的系统工具。作者旨在建立一套统计场框架，以揭示解码策略（decoding strategies）与临界现象（critical phenomena）之间的潜在联系。

Method: 将词元嵌入视为一维链上的连续自旋变量；从关联两点相关器（connected two-point correlator）定义磁化率，从系综平均嵌入场（ensemble-averaged embedding field）定义序参量；改变softmax温度T并观测这些量的行为；利用最近邻两邻点（TwoNN）方法独立估计本征维度（intrinsic dimension）。

Result: 在特征温度T_c附近观察到尖锐的磁化率峰并伴有幂律标度（power-law-like scaling）、序参量快速变化以及低于T_c时语义方向坍缩；TwoNN估算的本征维度在T_c附近达到最小值。这些结果在模型规模（Qwen3: 0.6B至32B）和提示类别（prompt categories）上保持一致。

Conclusion: 所观察到的现象类似于连续相变，但自回归生成（autoregressive generation）的非平衡（non-equilibrium）性质需要进一步研究。该框架为探测LLM输出的集体统计结构提供了定量工具，并暗示了解码策略与临界现象之间的关联。

Abstract: We propose a statistical-field framework for text generated by large language models (LLMs), treating token embeddings as continuous spin variables on a one-dimensional chain. Defining a susceptibility from the connected two-point correlator and an order parameter from the ensemble-averaged embedding field, we vary the \texttt{softmax} temperature $T$ and observe a sharp susceptibility peak near a characteristic $T_c$ with power-law-like scaling, a concurrent rapid change in the order parameter, and a collapse onto a single semantic direction below $T_c$. The intrinsic dimension estimated by the two nearest neighbor (TwoNN) method independently corroborates these findings, reaching a minimum near $T_c$. Results are robust across model scales (Qwen3: 0.6B--32B) and prompt categories. While the phenomenology closely resembles a continuous phase transition, the non-equilibrium nature of autoregressive generation warrants further investigation. Our framework provides quantitative tools for probing the collective statistical structure of LLM outputs and suggests connections between decoding strategies and critical phenomena.

</details>

# math.DS [[Back]](#toc)

### [8] [Existence of the C-type renormalisation two-cycle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06274)
*Zainab Rahman,Maria Pickett,Andrew Burbanks*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明了C型重整化二周期（C-type renormalisation two-cycle）的存在性，从而为平面非可逆映射族中C型通向混沌道路的普适性提供了理论支撑。通过在解析映射的巴拿赫空间（Banach space）中获得对相应普适状态空间缩放常数的严格界，作者将此前针对单向耦合映射的FS型结果推广至双向耦合映射，并将重整化群（renormalization group）变换的框架从不动点拓展至周期轨道，进一步确立了C型普适类源自RG变换动力学中倍周期分岔的猜想图景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非可逆二维映射族（至少含两个参数且具有折叠型临界点）展现出一种独特的临界缩放类型——C型，其参数积累导致无限多个共存的吸引周期轨道（周期为4^n或2·4^n），且伴随由特定普适常数控制的周期四倍化（period quadrupling）缩放行为。本文旨在从数学上严格证明驱动这一现象的C型重整化二周期的存在性，从而为理解该普适类提供严格基础。

Method: 研究在解析映射的巴拿赫空间（Banach space）中构建并分析重整化二周期，通过严格计算证明该二周期上的牛顿法（Newton's method）变体是一个压缩映射（contraction map），从而确立其存在性，并获得相应普适状态空间缩放常数的严格界。

Result: 成功证明了C型重整化二周期的存在性，并获得了对应的普适状态空间缩放常数的严格界。该结果将最近针对单向耦合映射（FS型）的结论推广至双向耦合映射（bidirectionally-coupled maps），并将重整化算子（renormalisation operator）的框架从不动点（fixed points）拓展到周期轨道（periodic orbits）。

Conclusion: 该证明为进一步确立关于倍周期分岔不同普适类（universality classes）的一系列悬而未决的猜想迈出了关键一步，并支持C型普适类诞生于重整化群（RG）变换自身动力学中的倍周期分岔这一理论图景。C型缩放规律已在若干有实际意义的动力系统中被观察到，尤为引人注目的是在具有生物学合理性的肾单位血压自动调节模型中。

Abstract: We prove the existence of the C-type renormalisation two-cycle, helping to establish the universality of the C-type route to chaos in families of non-invertible maps of the plane.
  Families of two-dimensional non-invertible maps, with at least two parameters and critical points of fold type, exhibit a distinct type of critical scaling, the C-type. An accumulation of parameter values leads to an infinite collection of coexisting attracting cycles of periods $4^n$ or $2\cdot 4^n$. Asymptotically, period quadrupling is accompanied by parameter-space scaling and state-space scaling governed by particular universal constants. Kuznetsov et. al. explained this phenomenon in terms of a stationary orbit of period two of the renormalisation group (RG) transformation for period-doubling.
  We prove the existence of the corresponding renormalisation two-cycle in a Banach space of analytic maps and gain rigorous bounds on the corresponding universal state space scaling constants. This result provides a further step in proving a series of outstanding conjectures concerning distinct universality classes for period-doubling. It extends the recent results for unidirectionally-coupled maps (the FS-type) to bidirectionally-coupled maps, and generalises the framework from fixed points to periodic orbits of the corresponding renormalisation operators. It also provides a further step in establishing the conjectured picture that the C-type universality class is born from the FS-type class via a period-doubling bifurcation in the dynamics of the RG transformation itself. The proof relies on rigorous computations to establish that a variant of Newton's method for the two-cycle is a contraction map.
  The C-type scaling regularity is known to occur in a number of dynamical systems of interest, perhaps most notably in biologically-plausible models of nephron blood pressure autoregulation.

</details>

### [9] [Flapping instability of elastic disks in Stokes flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06215)
*Yijiang Yu,Hugo Perrin,Michael D. Graham,Lorenzo Botto*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验和模拟发现，在低雷诺数剪切流中，自由悬浮的薄弹性圆盘会在超过临界流强时发生变形，产生周期性的拍动（flapping dynamics），该现象是一种亚临界不稳定性（subcritical instability），其关键机制在于圆盘的有限可伸展性（finite extensibility）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低雷诺数下的流固耦合（fluid-structure interactions）现象可能比以往预期更加丰富，而片状颗粒（sheet-like particles）在粘性流体中的流动动力学是新兴研究领域，亟需深入理解其基本机制。

Method: 采用实验与数值模拟相结合的方法，研究自由悬浮的薄弹性圆盘在剪切流中的动力学行为，其中圆盘平面初始平行于流动平面；通过模拟获得分岔图（bifurcation diagram），并结合线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）进行预测。

Result: 实验和模拟均表明，超过临界流强后圆盘发生变形，产生相对于水平剪切面周期性上下弯曲的拍动动力学；分岔图揭示多种振荡解，包括线性稳定性分析所预测的摆动运动（wiggling motion）；拍动行为被证明是一种亚临界不稳定性。

Conclusion: 拍动弹性的关键机制是圆盘的有限可伸展性；该发现对理解二维聚合物（2D polymers）和二维晶体材料（2D crystalline materials）等片状颗粒在粘性流体中的流动动力学具有重要启示意义。

Abstract: Fluid-structure interactions at low Reynolds number can lead to a much richer phenomenology than previously expected. Here, we study the dynamics of a freely suspended, thin elastic disk in a shear flow, where the plane of the disk is initially parallel to the flow plane. Using a combination of experiments and simulations, we demonstrate that beyond a critical flow strength the disk deforms, performing flapping dynamics, in which the disk curves up and down periodically relative to the horizontal shear plane. The bifurcation diagram obtained by simulation reveals several oscillatory solutions, including a wiggling motion that is predicted by a linear stability analysis. The flapping dynamics is shown to be a subcritical instability whose key ingredient is the finite extensibility of the disk. The behavior we observe has implications for emerging investigations on the flow dynamics of sheet-like particles, such as 2D polymers and 2D crystalline materials immersed in viscous fluids.

</details>

### [10] [Periodic discrete graphs with prescribed spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06398)
*Andrii Khrabustovskyi,Anna Muranova*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文构造了一类周期加权图（periodic weighted graph），其离散拉普拉斯算子（discrete Laplacian）的谱精确包含 n 个带隙（gaps），且可通过适当选取权重使这些带隙端点及谱上界达到预定值。该图具有刷状几何结构（brush-like geometry），并给出了权重系数的半显式公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究周期加权图上离散拉普拉斯算子的谱带隙结构，探索通过图几何与权重设计精确控制谱间隙个数及端点位置的构造方法。

Method: 采用刷状几何结构：一条无限顶点链，每个顶点额外连接 n 个悬挂顶点（pendant vertices）。权重系数的部分由显式表达式给出，部分则表示为某个显式确定多项式的根。

Result: 成功构造出一类周期加权图，其离散拉普拉斯谱恰好具有 n 个带隙；通过调整权重，可使这些带隙的端点以及谱的上界达到任意预设值。

Conclusion: 该构造表明，借助刷状图结构与半显式的权重公式，可以灵活控制周期加权图离散拉普拉斯的谱间隙数量与位置，为谱图论（spectral graph theory）中带隙设计问题提供了新的构造性结果。

Abstract: We construct a periodic weighted graph whose discrete Laplacian has a spectrum with precisely $n$ gaps. Moreover, we show that by an appropriate choice of the weights, the endpoints of these gaps, as well as the upper edge of the spectrum, attain the prescribed values. The underlying graph has a brush-like geometry: it consists of an infinite chain of vertices, each of which is connected to $n$ additional pendant vertices by extra edges. Semi-explicit formulae for the weight coefficients are provided: some of the coefficients are determined explicitly, while others are given as roots of an explicitly determined polynomial.

</details>

### [11] [Superconducting Triple Point in UTe$_2$: Thermodynamics and Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05210)
*L. A. Melnikovsky*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文报告在超导材料UTe₂的相图中，正常相与两个不同超导相之间的三条二级相变（second-order phase transition）线交汇于一个三相点（triple point），并指出这种三相点并不违反热力学约束。作者利用朗道理论（Landau theory）将相图解释为两个具有不同规范对称性（gauge symmetry）的超导序参量（superconducting order parameter）的耦合，且在空间均匀性假设下该解释具有唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示UTe₂相图中正常相与两个超导相之间存在三条二级相变线交汇于一点的特殊拓扑结构，并澄清“此类三相点在热力学上被禁止”的常见误解。

Method: 基于朗道理论（Landau theory），构建两个具有不同规范对称性（gauge symmetry）的超导序参量（superconducting order parameter）的自由能泛函，在空间均匀性（spatial uniformity）假设下解释相图结构。

Result: 发现UTe₂的相图中存在一个三相点（triple point），三条二级相变（second-order phase transition）线在此交汇；该三相点不存在热力学约束的障碍。在空间均匀性假设下，用两个不同规范对称性的超导序参量对相图的解释是唯一的。

Conclusion: UTe₂中三个相（正常相与两个超导相）之间的二级相变线可以在一个三相点共存，这并不违反热力学定律；朗道理论能够自洽地描述这一现象，并为理解多组分超导序参量（multi-component superconducting order parameter）的竞争与耦合提供框架。

Abstract: Three lines of second-order phase transitions between the normal phase and two distinct superconducting phases meet at a single point on the phase diagram of UTe$_2$. Contrary to common belief, there are no thermodynamic constraints for such triple points. The phase diagram is interpreted within Landau theory in terms of two superconducting order parameters with different gauge symmetries. Such an interpretation is unique under the assumption of spatial uniformity.

</details>


### [12] [Magnetochiral anisotropy in strained superconducting transition metal dichalcogenides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05302)
*Joaquim Telles de Miranda,Maxim Khodas,Alex Levchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文从理论上研究了二维非中心对称超导体（以过渡金属二硫化物MoS₂为代表）中非互易电荷输运现象。研究发现，在正常态下电流与磁场相对取向的响应被对称性破缺微扰压制，而在超导转变附近磁手征各向异性（magnetochiral anisotropy）显著增强。论文考虑了由序参量涨落（order-parameter fluctuations）和量子干涉过程（quantum-interference processes）对非互易电流的贡献，并将其与金兹堡-朗道自由能（Ginzburg-Landau free energy）中允许的高阶利夫希兹不变量（Lifshitz invariants）相关联，同时指出应变可引入额外的非线性电流响应矢量分量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究二维非中心对称超导体（如MoS₂）中的非互易电荷输运机制，特别是在超导转变附近磁手征各向异性增强的物理起源。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，基于金兹堡-朗道理论框架，考虑序参量涨落和量子干涉过程的贡献，并引入高阶利夫希兹不变量来描述对称性破缺效应。

Result: 正常态下非互易响应对对称性破缺微扰呈压制行为；超导转变附近磁手征各向异性显著增强；非互易电流可归因于序参量涨落和量子干涉过程，且与高阶利夫希兹不变量相关；应变可引入额外的非线性电流响应矢量分量。

Conclusion: 二维非中心对称超导体中的非互易电荷输运在超导转变附近显著增强，其物理机制可通过金兹堡-朗道理论中的高阶利夫希兹不变量理解，应变效应提供了调控该响应的新自由度。

Abstract: We present a theoretical study of nonreciprocal charge transport in two-dimensional noncentrosymmetric superconductors, focusing on transition-metal dichalcogenide MoS$_2$ as a representative example. In the normal state, the electrical response of a material to the relative orientation of the current and magnetic field is suppressed to leading order in the symmetry-breaking perturbations. In the vicinity of the superconducting transition, magnetochiral anisotropy is strongly enhanced. We consider contributions to the nonreciprocal current originating from order-parameter fluctuations and quantum-interference processes. These terms are linked to higher-order Lifshitz invariants generically allowed in the Ginzburg-Landau free energy of superconductors with broken inversion and time-reversal symmetries. We further show that strain enables additional vector components in the nonlinear current response.

### [13] [Fermiology and the Candidate Chiral Superconductor in Rhombohedral Tetralayer Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05356)
*Sandesh S. Kalantre,Ben H. Alexander,Julian May-Mann,Jonah Herzog-Arbeitman,Marisa Hocking,Qingrui Cao,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,David Goldhaber-Gordon,Andrew J. Mannix,Trithep Devakul,Yves H. Kwan,Daniel E. Parker,Aaron Sharpe*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过量子振荡测量揭示了菱方四层石墨烯中正常态在超导区附近存在比先前预期更丰富的电子结构，排除了简单连通费米口袋的季度金属态，对超导机制和手性配对可能性的探索提出了新的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性超导（chiral superconductivity）因其与拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）的紧密联系而备受关注。近期菱方多层石墨烯中发现的超导态可能具有手性，但其手性取决于正常态费米面（Fermi surface）的对称性和结构，而该正常态尚未被直接测量过。

Method: 作者在菱方四层石墨烯（rhombohedral tetralayer graphene）相图的大范围区域（包括超导区）测量了量子振荡（quantum oscillations），并结合微观建模对可能的正常态候选结构进行了比较分析。

Result: 在载流子密度远高于超导起始点的区域，作者复现了与自旋和谷极化的季度金属（quarter metal）一致的振荡信号，对应单一连通费米口袋（simply-connected Fermi pocket）。随着密度降低，系统进入一种复杂的“多频率”态（multitone state），该态持续存在于超导区域，其量子振荡谱与简单连通的季度金属不兼容。微观建模提出的完全极化环形态（fully-polarized annular）、向列态（nematic）和三口袋态（three-pocket）等次简单候选态也与测量结果不一致。

Conclusion: 菱方四层石墨烯的正常态比先前预想的更为丰富，这一发现重塑了对超导机制以及配对通道可能手性（chirality）的探索方向。

Abstract: Chiral superconductivity, in which the phase of the superconducting order parameter winds in momentum space, has long been sought for its close link to topological superconductivity. Recent work reported a superconductor in rhombohedral multilayer graphene emerging from a time-reversal symmetry broken normal state, suggesting that it could be a chiral superconductor. However, the possibility of chirality depends on the symmetry and structure of the normal-state Fermi surface, which have not been directly measured. Here we measure quantum oscillations in rhombohedral tetralayer graphene over a broad range of the phase diagram, including the superconducting region. At densities well above the onset of superconductivity, we reproduce previously-reported oscillations consistent with a spin- and valley-polarized quarter metal with a single simply-connected Fermi pocket. As the carrier density is reduced, we find a transition to a complex "multitone" state that persists through the superconducting region. This state's spectrum of quantum oscillations is incompatible with a simply-connected quarter metal. The next-simplest candidate normal states suggested by our microscopic modeling (fully-polarized annular, nematic, and three-pocket states) are inconsistent with our measurements, albeit difficult to rule out entirely. The normal state is thus seen to be richer than previously envisaged, reshaping the search for the superconducting mechanism and the possible chirality of the pairing channel.

</details>


### [14] [BCS-BEC crossover driven by small Fermi pockets of a high-Tc cuprate superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05653)
*Junhyeok Jeong,Yamato Enomoto,Yoshimitsu Kohama,Tomotaka Nakayama,Kotaro Ando,Kifu Kurokawa,Soonsang Huh,Zhuo Yang,Toshihiro Nomura,Matthew D. Watson,Timur K. Kim,Cephise Cacho,Chun Lin,Makoto Hashimoto,Donghui Lu,Shiro Sakai,Takami Tohyama,Kazuyasu Tokiwa,Takeshi Kondo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过角分辨光电子能谱（ARPES）和量子振荡（quantum oscillations）实验，在四层铜氧化物超导体Ba2Ca3Cu4O8(F,O)2的清洁内CuO2层中，发现了小费米口袋（small Fermi pocket）与大超导能隙（large superconducting gap）的共存，该共存是BCS-BEC交叉（BCS-BEC crossover）的标志性特征，并揭示了其随载流子密度增加而非减少的异常涌现行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欠掺杂铜氧化物中观测到的费米弧（Fermi arcs）究竟是来自大费米面（large Fermi surface）的片段还是小费米口袋（small Fermi pockets），这一长期争议阻碍了对该体系属于常规BCS（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer） regime还是强耦合BEC（Bose-Einstein condensation）交叉极限的分类。

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, ARPES）和量子振荡（quantum oscillations）两种实验手段，对四层铜氧化物Ba2Ca3Cu4O8(F,O)2的清洁内CuO2层进行测量。

Result: 观测到小费米口袋与大超导能隙的共存；在存在反铁磁（antiferromagnetic, AF）序的情况下，小口袋中的超导能隙异常大，使能隙-费米能之比（Delta_pocket/e_F ~ 0.6）和临界温度-费米温度之比（Tc/TF ~ 1.3）达到二维超导（two-dimensional superconductivity）的理论上限；且该BCS-BEC交叉并非随载流子密度降低，而是随其增加、在不足1%的窄掺杂范围内突然出现。

Conclusion: 这些结果为掺杂反铁磁Mott绝缘体（doped AF-Mott insulators）中的d波配对机制（d-wave pairing mechanism）提供了长期寻求的微观基础。

Abstract: Fermi arcs observed in underdoped cuprates have sparked debate over whether they represent segments of a large Fermi surface or small Fermi pockets. This ambiguity has long hindered their classification as either the conventional Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) regime or the strongly coupled Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) crossover limit. Here, using angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy and quantum oscillations, we demonstrate the coexistence of a small Fermi pocket and a large superconducting gap in the clean inner CuO2 layers of the four-layer cuprate Ba2Ca3Cu4O8(F,O)2. This coexistence constitutes a hallmark of the BCS-BEC crossover and has remained elusive for decades. Despite the presence of antiferromagnetic (AF) order, the superconducting gap in the small pocket is remarkably large, yielding a gap-to-Fermi-energy ratio (Delta_pocket/e_F ~ 0.6) and a critical-to-Fermi-temperature ratio (Tc/TF ~ 1.3) that reach the theoretical upper bound for two-dimensional superconductivity. Unexpectedly, this BCS-BEC crossover emerges not as the carrier density decreases but as it increases, abruptly within a narrow doping range of less than 1%. These results provide a long-sought microscopic foundation for the d-wave pairing mechanism in doped AF-Mott insulators.

</details>


### [15] [Strongly nonlinear regime of Josephson transmission lines revealed by two-tone spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05813)
*A. S. Averkin,A. A. Kopasov,I. E. Pologov,Aleksey N. Bolgar,Daria A. Kalacheva,Viktor B. Lubsanov,M. V. Fistul,A. Karpov*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We present experimental and theoretical studies of the off-resonant and strongly nonlinear regime of Josephson transmission lines (JTLs) with galvanically-coupled nonlinear elements. The transition from the weakly to the strongly nonlinear regime of a JTL induced by increasing the input power of the pump is probed via two-tone spectroscopy. Measurements of the phase of the transmission coefficient for a weak probe signal reveal a large increase and pronounced oscillations in the phase length variation as a function of the microwave power of the pump. Experimental observations are explained on the basis of the developed theoretical approach suitable for the description of the nonlinear response of strongly driven JTLs. Using the derived nonlinear wave equation, we show that the behavior of the phase length variation is associated with the oscillatory dependence of the Josephson inductances on the microwave power. It is demonstrated that the dissipation-induced propagation losses increase in the strongly nonlinear regime and also lead to smearing out the phase length oscillations. The developed theoretical analysis is in good agreement with experimental observations.

### [16] [Superconductivity beyond band geometry: emergence of pair quantum geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06017)
*Mehmet Akif Keskiner,Menderes Işkın*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文证明，量子几何（quantum geometry）不仅决定单粒子布洛赫态的有效质量，也通过“对量子几何（pair quantum geometry）”显著影响两体束缚态和库珀对（Cooper pair）的有效质量，从而成为超导理论中超越传统能带几何的基本要素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何已被证明通过单粒子态的几何性质调控布洛赫粒子的有效质量，但其是否以及如何影响配对态（paired states）的动力学行为尚不清楚，本文旨在将这一原理推广到两体束缚态和超导库珀对。

Method: 从一般多能带哈伯德模型（multiband Hubbard model）出发，推导出两体束缚态精确的有效质量定理及其在高斯涨落理论（Gaussian fluctuation theory）框架下、临界温度附近库珀对的对应形式；通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）处理涨落核的非厄米性，引入双正交对几何（biorthogonal pair geometry）；并在1D、2D、3D晶格模型上进行精确计算验证。

Result: 逆有效质量分解为传统的能带结构贡献和新的几何贡献——对量子几何，后者由配对流形（pairing manifold）上的量子度规（quantum metric）决定，在子格间配对非均匀时非平凡；多体情形下库珀对有效质量一般为复数，虚部反映朗道阻尼（Landau damping）；低维到三维模型中的精确计算表明，对量子几何对有效质量有定量显著贡献。

Conclusion: 对量子几何是理解超导配对动力学的一个基本新要素，其贡献超越传统能带几何，应被视为超导理论中不可或缺的组成部分。

Abstract: Quantum geometry shapes the effective mass of Bloch particles through the geometric properties of single-particle states. Here we show that this principle extends to paired states. Starting from a generic multiband Hubbard model, we derive an exact effective-mass theorem for two-body bound states and its many-body counterpart for Cooper pairs near the critical temperature within Gaussian fluctuation theory. In both cases, the inverse effective mass separates into a ``conventional'' band-structure contribution and a new geometric contribution, pair quantum geometry, governed by quantum metrics on the pairing manifold, which becomes nontrivial when pairing is non-uniform across sublattices. In the many-body setting, analytic continuation renders the fluctuation kernel non-Hermitian, producing a biorthogonal pair geometry and a generally complex Cooper-pair effective mass whose imaginary part reflects Landau damping. Exact calculations on one-, two-, and three-dimensional lattice models show that pair quantum geometry can make quantitatively significant contributions to the effective mass. These results establish pair quantum geometry as a fundamental ingredient of superconductivity beyond conventional band geometry.

### [17] [2.4 GHz Flip-flop Device within Nonequilibrium Superconducting Diode](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06152)
*Xiangyu Bi,Hongyi Li,Aoshen Yang,Yuqiang Fang,Ganyu Chen,Shichong Yang,Yicheng Shen,Qizheng Sun,Junwei Huang,Wei Jiang,Da Wang,Fuqiang Huang,Haijun Zhang,Qianghua Wang,Hongtao Yuan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本工作在范德瓦尔斯超导体2M-WS₂中实现了一种极性可控的非平衡约瑟夫森结超导二极管，展示了高达2.4 GHz的边缘触发触发器操作。通过调控超导纳米片的厚度来工程化结中的反演不对称性，获得了67%的二极管效率和超过10⁵的通断比，其输出脉冲信号的脉宽和占空比可在跨越12个数量级的宽带频率范围内调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应具有非对称临界超电流（asymmetric critical supercurrent），因其无耗散的超电流（dissipationless supercurrent）可为超导电子学提供极高的通断比（on-off ratio）和二极管效率。然而，实现高频工作（high working frequency）——实际应用的关键要求——仍是一个难以达成的挑战。

Method: 在范德瓦尔斯超导体2M-WS₂中构建非平衡约瑟夫森结（non-equilibrium Josephson junction），通过调控超导纳米片的厚度来工程化结中的反演不对称性（inversion asymmetry），从而实现极性可控的超导二极管及其边缘触发触发器（edge-triggered flip-flop）操作。

Result: 实现了高达2.4 GHz的高频操作，二极管效率达67%，通断比超过10⁵。输出脉冲信号的脉宽和占空比可在跨越12个数量级的宽带频率范围内调控。理论分析表明，结中超电流的非平衡动力学性质（non-equilibrium dynamic nature）是高频操作和极性控制的关键。

Conclusion: 该2.4 GHz非平衡约瑟夫森二极管为先进超导逻辑电路（superconducting logic circuits）和宽带电信应用（broadband telecommunication applications）提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Superconducting diode effect exhibits asymmetric critical supercurrent and has profound implications for condensed matter physics. The technical appeals of such superconducting diodes are their ultrahigh on-off ratio and diode efficiency for superconducting electronics owing to the dissipationless supercurrent therein. However, realizing superconducting diode operation at high working frequency, which is a key requirement for practical applications, remains elusive and challenging. Here, we demonstrate a polarity-controllable superconducting diode with non-equilibrium Josephson junction and its edge-triggered flip-flop operation at a high frequency up to 2.4 GHz, within a van der Waals superconductor 2M-WS$_2$. By simply tuning the thickness of superconducting 2M-WS$_2$ nanoflakes to engineer inversion asymmetry in the junction, we achieve a high diode efficiency of 67% and an on-off ratio exceeding 10$^5$. Importantly, the pulse width and duty cycle of output pulse signals in such superconducting diode flip-flop devices can be controlled in a broadband frequency range crossing 12 orders of magnitude. Theoretical analysis reveals that the non-equilibrium dynamic nature of supercurrent in these Josephson junctions enables such a high diode operating frequency and the polarity control of supercurrent. The 2.4 GHz non-equilibrium Josephson diode developed here provides a promising platform for advanced superconducting logic circuits and broadband telecommunication applications.

### [18] [Particle-Hole Ghost Interference in Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06437)
*Archisman Panigrahi,Vladislav Poliakov,Leonid Levitov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出边界辅助杂质干涉（boundary-assisted impurity interference）作为一种新型电子干涉机制，与镜子辅助的杨氏双缝干涉类似。超导体中的单个杂质靠近线缺陷、台阶边缘或相边界时，直接散射的准粒子波与边界反射波干涉，产生“鬼影”干涉图案。该效应在杂质势一阶就出现，比双杂质杨氏干涉更强，且空间调制直接反映配对态的准粒子结构，可作为超导电子序的局域探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 借鉴镜面辅助光学干涉提升杨氏双缝干涉保真度的思路，探索超导体中相应的电子类比机制——即由单个杂质与边界共同作用产生的粒子-空穴干涉（particle-hole interference），以发展更强的局域探针。

Method: 理论分析超导体中单个杂质靠近线缺陷、台阶边缘或相边界时的准粒子散射与干涉。直接散射的准粒子波与边界反射波叠加，产生融合传统$2k_F$弗里德尔振荡（Friedel oscillations）与额外双曲条纹（hyperbolic fringes）的“鬼影”干涉图案。

Result: 该效应在杂质势一阶（first order）即出现，相比近期研究的双杂质杨氏干涉（two-impurity Young's interference）参数更强；空间调制范围超过$λ_F/2$，且直接敏感于配对态的准粒子结构，包括超导序参量可能的费米面各向异性（Fermi-surface anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 边界辅助杂质干涉是一种稳健的超导电子序局域探针，其清晰信号可通过扫描隧道显微镜/扫描隧道谱（STM/STS）测量获取。

Abstract: Mirror-assisted optical interference can improve the fidelity of Young's double-slit interference. Here we discuss an electron analogue: particle-hole interference in superconductors produced by a single impurity near a line defect, terrace edge, or phase boundary. Quasiparticle waves scattered directly from the impurity interfere with waves reflected by the boundary, generating a ``ghost'' interference pattern that combines conventional $2k_F$ Friedel oscillations with additional hyperbolic fringes. Compared to the recently studied two-impurity Young's interference, this effect appears already at first order in the impurity potential and is therefore parametrically stronger. The resulting spatial modulation extends beyond $λ_F/2$ and is directly sensitive to the quasiparticle structure of the paired state, including possible Fermi-surface anisotropy of the superconducting order parameter. These findings point to boundary-assisted impurity interference as a robust local probe of superconducting electronic order, with clear signatures accessible to STM/STS measurements.

### [19] [Variational Inverse Problems for Second Order ODEs with and without Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05550)
*G. E. Prince,T. Mestdag,D. Martin de Diego*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多物理系统（无论是否带有非完整约束（nonholonomic constraints））均具有拉格朗日描述（Lagrangian description）。约束系统的拉格朗日模型由限制在速度子流形上的二阶常微分方程表示，而非约束系统则不受此限制。本文旨在解决一个更具一般性的逆问题：给定一个流形上受约束或不受约束的二阶常微分方程组，何时它能成为某个拉格朗日模型的表示？

Method: 采用几何技术（geometric techniques）对约束与非约束两类系统进行统一处理，通过流形上的微分几何框架分析二阶常微分方程组的拉格朗日可表示性条件。

Result: 约束情形的逆问题展现出比非约束情形更多的歧义性与复杂性，后者已被充分地理解。

Conclusion: 约束系统在拉格朗日逆问题中具有更高的结构复杂性，需要更深入的分析方法加以处理。

Abstract: Many physical systems with or without nonholonomic constraints have a Lagrangian description. In the first case, the Lagrangian model can be represented by second-order ODEs that are constrained to a submanifold of velocities; in the latter case the ODEs are unconstrained. In this paper, using geometric techniques, we address the more general inverse problem: ``When can a given constrained or unconstrained system of second order ODEs on a manifold be the representation of a Lagrangian model?''. We show that the constrained case has many more ambiguities and complexities than its well-understood, unconstrained counterpart.

### [20] [Second-Jet Equivariant $η$ Separations on Lens Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06403)
*Sanchita Sharma*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文利用透镜空间（lens space）的旋量狄拉克特征空间（spin Dirac eigenspace）的显式同余描述，研究三维透镜空间在圆度量（round metric）和标准坐标环面作用下的等变η不变量（equivariant η invariant）。针对平方族L(ℓ²,ℓ-1)与L(ℓ²,2ℓ-1)（ℓ≥5奇数），发现普通η值相同，但剩余圆等变η芽（residual-circle equivariant η germ）的二阶导数非零，可区分普通η不变量无法区分的空间。以L(25,4)与L(25,9)为例，归一化二阶导数为-6080。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 透镜空间是谱几何（spectral geometry）中有用的检验实例，因其旋量狄拉克特征空间具有显式的同余描述。本文旨在利用这些描述研究普通标量η不变量（ordinary scalar η invariant）之外更精细的等变η不变量，以区分普通η不变量无法区分的透镜空间。

Method: 保留每个特征空间的旋量-傅里叶特征（spin-Fourier character），而非仅使用普通标量η值。采用剩余圆等变η芽（residual-circle equivariant η germ）的分析框架，直接使用旋量-傅里叶留数（spin-Fourier residues）进行计算，微扰海森符号（perturbative Hessian signs）仅作为动机参考而非不变量本身。

Result: 对于平方族L(ℓ²,ℓ-1)与L(ℓ²,2ℓ-1)（ℓ≥5奇数），普通η值相同，剩余圆等变η芽的一阶导数因对称性为零，但二阶导数非零。以L(25,4)与L(25,9)为例，归一化二阶导数为-6080。

Conclusion: 剩余圆等变η芽可以检测到普通η不变量无法区分的差异，表明等变η不变量在透镜空间谱几何中提供了更精细的区分能力。

Abstract: Lens spaces are useful test examples in spectral geometry because their spin Dirac eigenspaces admit explicit congruence descriptions. We use these descriptions to study equivariant $η$ invariants for three-dimensional lens spaces with the round metric and the standard coordinate-torus action, retaining the spin-Fourier character of each eigenspace rather than only the ordinary scalar $η$ value. For the square family $L(\ell^2,\ell-1)$ and $L(\ell^2,2\ell-1)$, with $\ell\geq 5$ odd, we obtain a residual-circle equivariant $η$ separation: the ordinary $η$ values agree, and the first derivative of the residual $η$ germ vanishes by symmetry, but the second derivative is nonzero. For $L(25,4)$ versus $L(25,9)$, the normalized second derivative is $-6080$. Thus, the residual-circle equivariant $η$ germ detects a distinction invisible to the ordinary $η$ invariant. The calculation uses spin-Fourier residues directly; perturbative Hessian signs serve only as motivation and are not part of the invariant.

### [21] [Isospectrality and Operator Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05294)
*Pradip Kattel,Yicheng Tang,Natan Andrei*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究通过一对等谱（isospectral）费米子链——一个强相互作用、一个二次型（quadratic）——证明了两者尽管拥有完全相同的多体谱，却因非局域非线性幺正变换导致截然不同的相结构与算符动力学。算符复杂性在二次型模型中表现为封闭线性子空间内的演化，而在相互作用模型中呈现渐近Lanczos增长（$b_n\propto\sqrt n$），表明自由多体谱与相互作用算符动力学可以根本兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究通常认为可解模型（exactly solvable models）的谱结构决定了其算符复杂性（operator complexity）和相图，但尚不清楚等谱系统是否必然具有相同的算符动力学行为。作者旨在探索等谱但相互作用性质迥异的模型是否能产生不同的相结构与算符复杂度。

Method: 作者构建并严格求解了一对等谱费米子链：一个为强相互作用模型，另一个为二次型（quadratic）模型。通过非局域非线性幺正变换（nonlocal nonlinear unitary transformation）将两者映射起来，该变换保留完整的多体谱，但将局域费米子算符（local fermion operators）转化为延展的多体弦算符（extended many-body strings）。

Result: 在二次型模型中，算符在封闭的线性子空间中演化；而在相互作用模型中，算符生成越来越高的多体项，并呈现渐近Lanczos增长 $b_n\propto\sqrt n$。两个模型尽管谱完全相同，却展现了不同的相（distinct phases）和截然不同的算符复杂性（sharply different notions of operator complexity）。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，自由多体谱（free many-body spectra）与相互作用算符动力学（interacting operator dynamics）在根本上是兼容的，即等谱系统可以同时拥有自由粒子谱特征和相互作用导致的复杂算符演化行为。

Abstract: We study a pair of exactly solvable, isospectral fermion chains, one strongly interacting and one quadratic, that nevertheless display remarkably different phase structures and operator dynamics. A nonlocal nonlinear unitary transformation maps one onto the other while preserving the entire many-body spectrum and converting local fermion operators into extended many-body strings. Thus, operators that evolve within a closed linear subspace in the quadratic model become interacting operators that generate increasingly higher-body terms and exhibit asymptotic Lanczos growth $b_n\propto\sqrt n$. Despite their identical spectra, the two models realize distinct phases and sharply different notions of operator complexity. Our results demonstrate that free many-body spectra and interacting operator dynamics are fundamentally compatible.

### [22] [Multiple Quantum Hypothesis Testing: One-Shot Pairwise Bounds and Sharp Asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06246)
*Hao-Chung Cheng,Po-Chieh Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对多量子态贝叶斯判别问题，建立了无维度依赖的一次性误差上界，证明并改进了已有的多量子Chernoff界；同时在二元量子假设检验中，证明了最小误差概率可由迹调和平均量刻画，并在常数因子内与经典误差概率相匹配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Audenaert和Mosonyi (2014)提出的猜想，并改进Li (2016)的多量子Chernoff界中存在的维度依赖预因子；此外，处理此前尚未解决的无限维希尔伯特空间情形，以及完善Nussbaum和Szkoła (2009)中经典-量子误差概率的对比。

Method: 基于成对误差（pairwise errors）之和，构建了一个无维度依赖（dimension-free）的一次性（one-shot）上界，用于约束多量子态贝叶斯判别的最小误差概率；在二元情形中引入迹调和平均量（trace harmonic-mean quantity）刻画误差概率。

Result: 在多量子态情形中，该上界去除了此前界中维度相关的预因子，并在任意可分离希尔伯特空间（separable Hilbert spaces）上证明了多量子Chernoff距离（multiple quantum Chernoff distance）的可达性，给出了最优误差概率的常因子锐渐近（constant-factor sharp asymptotics）。在二元情形中，最小误差概率由迹调和平均量在通用常数（universal constants）内刻画，且最优量子误差概率与Nussbaum-Szkoła分布对应的经典误差概率相差不超过因子2。

Conclusion: 本文提出的无维度依赖上界解决了多个公开问题，统一并改进了量子多态判别与二元假设检验中的已有理论界限，同时建立了量子和经典误差概率之间的定量联系。

Abstract: We consider Bayesian discrimination among multiple quantum states and establish a dimension-free one-shot upper bound on the minimum probability of error in terms of the sum of pairwise errors. This resolves a conjecture of Audenaert and Mosonyi [J. Math. Phys. 55 (2014)] and improves the multiple quantum Chernoff bound of Li [Ann. Statist. 44 (2016)] by removing its dimension-dependent prefactor. In the asymptotic many-copy regime, our bound proves the achievability of the multiple quantum Chernoff distance for arbitrary separable Hilbert spaces, thereby settling the previously open infinite-dimensional case, and further yields constant-factor sharp asymptotics for the optimal error probability.
  In binary quantum hypothesis testing, we prove that the minimum error probability is characterized, up to universal constants, by a trace harmonic-mean quantity. Consequently, the optimal binary quantum error probability is within a factor of two of the optimal classical error probability for the associated Nussbaum-Szkoła distributions, complementing the lower bound of Nussbaum and Szkoła [Ann. Statist. 37 (2009)].

</details>


### [23] [Polymer quantum mechanics on compact configuration spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06019)
*Maxwell R. Siebersma,Basie Seibert,Samuel Shuman,David A. Craig*

TL;DR: 本文研究了“聚合物量子力学”（polymer quantum mechanics）——一种受圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）启发的量子化方案，其特点是理论位形空间采用离散拓扑结构。详细分析了该方案对经典紧致位形空间系统的量子化，以粒子在环上和盒子中为例，给出了有限图上的精确能量本征值和本征函数，并与标准薛定谔量子力学进行了对比，同时展示了连续极限下本征函数向连续对应物的趋近行为。

Method: 采用聚合物量子化（polymer quantization）方案，构建基于离散拓扑位形空间的正则表示（representation），并利用有限图（finite graph）上的聚合物态构造希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）。以粒子在环上和盒子中的系统为例，在晶格上求解精确能量本征值和本征函数，并分析其连续极限。

Result: 给出了粒子在环上（particle on a ring）和粒子在盒子中（particle in a box）在聚合物量子化框架下的精确能量本征值和本征函数，详细展示了位置表象中的本征函数在连续极限下如何趋近于标准薛定谔量子力学中的连续对应物。

Conclusion: 聚合物量子化提供了一种与标准薛定谔表示截然不同的正则对易关系（canonical commutation relations）表示；在紧致位形空间系统中，离散拓扑结构导致希尔伯特空间定义在有限图上，其能谱和本征函数与标准量子力学既有相似之处也有差异，且可在连续极限下恢复标准结果。

Abstract: "Polymer quantum mechanics" is the name given to a quantization scheme inspired by loop quantum gravity in which the configuration space of the theory is chosen to have a discrete topology. Polymer quantization yields a representation of the canonical commutation relations that is genuinely distinct from the conventional "Schrödinger" representation. In this paper, we summarize the main features of polymer quantum mechanics and investigate in detail the polymer quantization of systems with configuration spaces that are classically compact. We show explicitly how using the standard construction of polymer states leads to a Hilbert space of states defined on a finite graph of points. By way of example, we find the exact energy eigenvalues and eigenfunctions for a particle on a ring and a particle in a box defined on such lattices, and discuss similarities and differences from standard Schrödinger quantum mechanics. We also explore the continuum limit of states in these systems, and demonstrate in detail how the exact eigenfunctions in the position representation approach their continuum counterparts.

### [24] [Frustrated superradiant phases in one- and two-dimensional lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05278)
*Jongjun M. Lee,Myung-Joong Hwang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究周期晶格上耦合Dicke模型阵列中的阻挫（frustration）与对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）问题，发现阻挫驱动光子密度波有序，自发平移对称性破缺可从对称相激发谱预测，并揭示了离散对称性下涌现Nambu-Goldstone模、类准晶准周期有序以及合成磁场调控对称性破缺等新现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究了一维和二维周期晶格上耦合Dicke模型（coupled Dicke models）的大尺度阵列，通过强光-物质耦合产生超辐射相（superradiant phase），并利用相邻序参量（order parameter）竞争诱导自发平移对称性破缺（spontaneous translational symmetry breaking）。

Result: 阻挫驱动光子密度波有序（photonic density-wave ordering），对称相激发谱可预测破缺周期性；在一维链中离散对称性下临界点附近涌现Nambu-Goldstone模（emergent Nambu-Goldstone mode）并揭示了其产生机制；超辐射相中出现类准晶（quasicrystals）的准周期有序；合成磁通（synthetic magnetic flux）可有效控制平移对称性破缺的性质。

Conclusion: Dicke晶格模型构成一类全新的量子多体系统，局域与全局热力学极限的共存导致非常规对称性破缺和涌现集体行为，为量子多体物理开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Understanding how frustration and symmetry breaking shape collective behavior is a central problem in quantum many-body systems. In this work, we investigate this problem in large one- and two-dimensional arrays of coupled Dicke models on a periodic lattice, where strong light-matter coupling gives rise to a superradiant phase and competition between neighboring order parameters induces spontaneous translational symmetry breaking. Such Dicke lattice models constitute a fundamentally new class of quantum many-body systems, as they simultaneously realize the thermodynamic limit associated with the lattice size and an intrinsic thermodynamic limit arising from collective on-site interactions with quantum emitters. We show that frustration drives photonic density-wave ordering, and that the resulting broken periodicity can be predicted from the excitation spectrum of the symmetric phase, without requiring computationally prohibitive thermodynamic energy minimization. Furthermore, we demonstrate that an emergent Nambu-Goldstone mode arises near the critical point in a one-dimensional chain despite the presence of only discrete symmetry, and uncover the mechanism that enables this otherwise forbidden gapless excitation. We also find quasi-periodic ordering in the superradiant phase, reminiscent of quasicrystals, and demonstrate that synthetic magnetic flux provides a powerful knob to control the nature of translational symmetry breaking. Our results establish a new direction in quantum many-body physics where the coexistence of local and global thermodynamic limits gives rise to unconventional symmetry breaking and emergent collective behavior.

### [25] [Emergent Self-Similar Quantum Revivals in Spiral Drives](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05288)
*Xin-Chi Zhou,Liang-Hong Mo,Hongzheng Zhao,Bastien Lapierre*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现了一种新的非平衡时间序：准周期螺旋脉冲驱动的多体系统中出现的自相似量子复兴（self-similar quantum revivals），系统会在层次嵌套的时间序列中反复回到接近初始状态的状态，并基于广义自旋回波和准周期SU(2)余环（cocycles）给出了严格的解析证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多体非平衡系统中是否存在不同于传统时间晶体（time crystal）的新型时间有序结构，特别是由准周期驱动（quasiperiodic driving）诱导的自相似时间序。

Method: 解析推导了准周期螺旋脉冲驱动下多体系统的保真度（fidelity）和纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）的动力学行为；通过识别涌现动力学吸引子（emergent dynamical attractor），利用广义自旋回波过程和准周期SU(2)余环证明自相似量子复兴的起源。

Result: 保真度与纠缠熵均表现出自相似的时间结构；连续复兴之间的纠缠标度（scaling）可通过驱动参数在体积律（volume-law）与面积律（area-law）之间调节；存在可积性破缺微扰时系统最终会加热，但在此之前会出现寿命呈代数可调（algebraically tunable）的长寿命预热 regime（prethermal regime）。

Conclusion: 自相似量子复兴为非平衡量子物质（nonequilibrium quantum matter）提供了一种新范式，并在当前量子模拟器（quantum simulators）中具有可观测的现实可行性。

Abstract: We uncover a distinct form of nonequilibrium temporal order: self-similar quantum revivals in a many-body system driven by quasiperiodic spiral kicks, where the system recurrently returns close to its initial state at a hierarchically nested sequence of times. We demonstrate that both the fidelity and entanglement entropy exhibit this self-similar temporal structure. It originates from an emergent dynamical attractor, which we identify, such that all momentum modes eventually fall into the same closed orbits at self-similar times. We analytically justify this behavior and show that, for special momentum modes, this attractor arises as a consequence of a generalized spin echo process, and more generally we prove its existence using quasiperiodic SU(2) cocycles. Interestingly, the dynamics between consecutive revivals supports either volume- or area-law entanglement scaling, tunable via the driving parameters. In the presence of integrability-breaking perturbations, the system eventually heats up, but a long-lived prethermal regime with algebraically tunable lifetime occurs before heating sets in. Our results establish self-similar quantum revivals as a new paradigm for nonequilibrium quantum matter and provide a realistic route for its observation in current quantum simulators.

### [26] [Non-equilibrium thermodynamics of collapse models in the strongly non-Gaussian regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06259)
*Pedro B. Melo,Pedro V. Paraguassú,Simone Artini,Gabriele Lo Monaco,Sandro Donadi,Mauro Paternostro*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了耗散性Diósi-Penrose（dDP）模型（并推广至CSL模型）的热力学一致性，通过Wigner相空间形式及其精确伪谱模拟方法，揭示了该系统不会热化而是进入非平衡稳态（NESS），其中渐近非高斯性按耗散参数β的三次方标度，并通过Wigner熵产生确认了模型的热力学有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准客观坍缩模型（objective collapse models）为量子测量问题提供了统一框架，但预测了系统能量的非物理无限增长（heating issue）。耗散性Diósi-Penrose（dDP）模型通过引入线性摩擦机制试图解决该问题，但这种修正带来了复杂的非高斯相空间动力学，其热力学一致性尚未得到严格证明。

Method: 采用Wigner相空间形式（Wigner phase-space formalism），显著超越二次近似（quadratic approximation）的局限。为克服强耗散下微扰方法（perturbative methods）的失效，引入了一种新颖的精确伪谱模拟方法（exact pseudo-spectral simulation approach）。

Result: dDP机制下的系统不会热化（thermalize），而是进入非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady-state, NESS），其中渐近非高斯性（asymptotic non-Gaussianity）按耗散参数β的三次方标度。通过评估Wigner熵产生（Wigner entropy production），确认了模型的热力学有效性，并表明高灵敏度的信息论量需借助精确数值方法才能准确捕捉分布的关键非高斯尾部（non-Gaussian tails）。

Conclusion: 该研究严格建立了耗散性Diósi-Penrose模型（扩展至CSL模型）在弱与强非高斯区间的热力学一致性，验证了其热力学有效性，同时强调了精确数值方法对于获取非高斯尾部信息的重要性。

Abstract: Standard objective collapse models offer a unified approach to the quantum measurement problem but predict an unphysical, indefinite increase in the energy of the system. The dissipative Diósi-Penrose (dDP) model resolves this heating issue by introducing a linear friction mechanism. However, this modification induces complex, non-Gaussian phase-space dynamics. We rigorously establish the thermodynamic consistency of this friction mechanism -- extended to the CSL model -- across both weakly and strongly non-Gaussian regimes. Using the Wigner phase-space formalism, we go significantly beyond the quadratic approximation and, to bypass the failure of perturbative methods under strong dissipation, introduce a novel exact pseudo-spectral simulation approach. Our analysis reveals that the system subjected to the dDP mechanism does not thermalize, but rather settles into a non-equilibrium steady-state (NESS) where the asymptotic non-Gaussianity scales as the third power of the dissipation parameter $β$. By evaluating the Wigner entropy production, we confirm the thermodynamic validity of the model and demonstrate that highly sensitive information-theoretic quantities require exact numerical methods to accurately capture the key non-Gaussian tails of the distribution.

### [27] [Reliability of asymptotic work extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06318)
*Kaito Watanabe,Bartosz Regula,Marco Tomamichel,Ryuji Takagi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文挑战了量子热力学中关于功提取最优速率不依赖于具体操作类别的传统观点，通过分析提取速率与可靠性之间的权衡，发现保吉布斯操作（Gibbs-preserving operations）与热操作（thermal operations）在渐近性能上存在显著差异，前者在误差抑制速度上严格优于后者，从而揭示能量守恒等操作约束对量子任务精度的限制比渐近速率所暗示的更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子态功提取是量子热力学（quantum thermodynamics）的基础任务。前人研究认为，无论采用能量守恒的热操作还是公理化的保吉布斯操作，最优功提取速率均由亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）给出，似乎不受操作类别影响。本文旨在挑战这一观点，探究两种操作类别在渐近性能上的更深层次差异。

Method: 本文聚焦于功提取速率与其可靠性（reliability）之间的权衡，具体通过刻画提取误差可被抑制的最优渐近速度（optimal asymptotic speed）来展开分析。采用佩茨（Petz）与夹层（sandwiched）Rényi 相对熵（Rényi relative entropies）分别表征保吉布斯操作和热操作的可靠性。

Result: 研究表明，保吉布斯操作和热操作的可靠性分别由佩茨 Rényi 相对熵和夹层 Rényi 相对熵刻画，且前者的性能在一般情况下严格优于后者。这一发现为若干信息论散度（information-theoretic divergences）提供了新的解释。

Conclusion: 操作约束（如能量守恒）对量子任务可达精度的限制比从渐近速率中推断出的更强。因此，不应将保吉布斯操作视为物理可实现热过程的数学便利替代品。研究还质疑了现有文献中仅关注渐近速率的分析视角的充分性。

Abstract: Extracting work from quantum states is a fundamental task in quantum thermodynamics. Previous studies have primarily focused on determining the best achievable rate of work extraction, and remarkably, this characterization appeared to remain unchanged regardless of the choice of allowed processes: whether one considers the operationally motivated class of energy-conserving thermal operations, or the axiomatic class of Gibbs-preserving operations, the optimal extractable work is given by the Helmholtz free energy. Here, we challenge this perspective, showing that a more refined analysis of the asymptotic performance of work extraction reveals significant differences in the performance for the two different classes of free operations. Precisely, we focus on the trade-off between the extraction rate and its reliability, characterized by the optimal asymptotic speed at which the extraction error can be suppressed. We establish that the reliability of Gibbs-preserving operations and of thermal operations are respectively characterized by the Petz and the sandwiched Rényi relative entropies, demonstrating that the former in general strictly outperforms the latter, and providing new interpretations of several information-theoretic divergences. Our analysis reveals that operational constraints such as energy conservation impose stronger limitations on the achievable precision of quantum tasks than can be inferred from their asymptotic rates, thereby questioning the use of Gibbs-preserving operations as a mathematically convenient substitute for the physically realizable thermal processes.

</details>


### [28] [Energy-Modulated Time-Asymmetric Spontaneous Collapse: Forward-Backward Dynamics from Stochastic Ito Reversal and Bright Solitons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06452)
*Ikechukwu C. Okoro,Mike O. Osiele,Godfrey E. Akpojotor*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于立方-五次非线性薛定谔方程（cubic-quintic nonlinear Schrödinger equation, CQ-NLSE）形式，建立了一个关于对称性破缺和量子不可逆性的严格理论框架，核心在于伊藤随机场反转（stochastic Itô field reversal）导致的2/3普适不对称耦合参数，以及正反向坍缩算子比率约10^30的显著不对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于从理论上揭示由伊藤随机场反转（stochastic Itô field reversal）引发的对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）和量子不可逆性（quantum irreversibility）的内在机制，并探讨其在非线性薛定谔方程形式中的具体表现。

Method: 方法基于三个物理动机，利用伊藤微积分（Itô calculus）推导正反向非线性随机微分方程；引入一个正比于噪声强度、局域概率密度和激发能平方的能量驱动坍缩算子（energy-driven collapse operator），并在准一维吸引性锂-7原子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（BEC）中求解精确亮孤子解。

Result: 结果表明运动学时间反演（kinematic time-reversal）与伊藤随机结构根本不相容，产生了普适不对称耦合参数2/3；正反向振幅比为1.870；热图分析显示正向坍缩算子随时间单调增长，反向坍缩算子则衰减，二者比率约为10^30，与传统的对称坍缩模型形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该框架所展示的显著不对称性——尤其是正反向坍缩算子约10^30的比率——清晰地区分了这一理论与传统的对称坍缩模型，为理解量子不可逆性和对称性破缺提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We present a rigorous theoretical framework for symmetry breaking and quantum irreversibility arising from stochastic Ito field reversal within a cubic-quintic nonlinear Schrodinger equation (CQ-NLSE) formalism. Starting from three physically motivated considerations, forward and backward nonlinear stochastic differential equations are derived via the Ito calculus. Kinematic time-reversal is shown to be fundamentally incompatible with the Ito stochastic structure, yielding the universal asymmetry-coupling parameter of 2/3. An energy-driven collapse operator proportional to the product of noise strength, local probability density, and excitation energy squared is introduced, amplifying the collapse in high-density, high-excitation regions. Exactly bright soliton solutions are obtained for a quasi-one-dimensional BEC of attractive Li-7 atoms, with forward and backward amplitude ratio of 1.870. Heat map analysis of the parameter planes reveals that the forward collapse operator grows monotonically in time while the backward counterpart decays, achieving a ratio approximately 1030, sharply distinguishing this framework from conventional symmetric collapse models.

</details>

### [29] [Propagation of Regularity for Schroedinger Equations with Time Dependent Potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27321)
*Avy Soffer*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文研究了含时薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）在一般时间依赖性势场下的动力学行为，证明了对于空间局域势（localized potentials），正则性传播（propagation of regularity）在高阶索伯列夫范数（higher Sobolev norms）中一致有界，并针对解的非散射部分引入了直接在H^2(R^3)中起作用的传播估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要针对解发生散射（scatter）的情况，通过标准自举论证（bootstrap argument）证明正则性传播。然而在一般情况下，解的一部分并不散射，这对此类问题提出了新的理论挑战。因此，需要发展新的传播估计方法来处理非散射情形。

Method: 论文提出了一种直接作用于H^2(R^3)空间的传播估计（propagation estimates），而非依赖散射后的自举论证。该方法专门针对空间局域势下不散射的解部分，从而在高阶索伯列夫范数中建立一致有界性。

Result: 对于空间局域势，无论势函数的时间依赖性如何，薛定谔方程的正则性传播在高阶索伯列夫范数中均保持一致有界。该结果涵盖了解中存在非散射成分的一般情形。

Conclusion: 该工作拓展了含时薛定谔方程正则性理论的范围，通过引入新的传播估计，成功处理了非散射解部分带来的技术困难，为更一般的含时势场问题提供了分析工具。

Abstract: The dynamics of Schrödinger equation with time dependent potentials of general time dependence is considered. It is shown that for localized in space potentials, there is propagation of regularity which is uniformly bounded in higher Sobolev norms. Unlike the cases where the solution scatter, and then propagation is proved via a standard bootstrap argument, the solutions considered here have a part that does not scatter, as expected in general. For this we introduce propagation estimates that work directly in (e.g.) $H^2(\mathcal{R}^3).$

</details>

### [30] [Beyond Critical Minerals Targets: Digital Rock Physics as Infrastructure for Secure and Circular Supply Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05798)
*Hannah P. Menke,Alessio Scanziani,Maja Rücker*

TL;DR: 本文主张将数字岩石物理（Digital Rock Physics, DRP）视为关键矿产政策实施的基础设施，而非仅作为专业实验室方法，并提出一项以DRP为核心的英国-欧洲政策议程，涵盖翻译示范、跨学科培训、数字矿石护照标准、联邦式数字矿石数据库及综合反应端站，以推动关键矿产战略从目标设定走向实际落地。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 英国和欧洲正从关键矿产（critical minerals）的目标设定阶段快速转向实施阶段，但许多潜在区域资源仍面临复杂、勘探不足、历史开采或经济边缘化等问题。现有政策依赖许可证改革和项目指定，缺乏能够确定矿石、卤水、废物流及回收原料是否可经济且环保加工的竞争前测量、建模与数据基础设施。

Method: 论文提出将数字岩石物理（Digital Rock Physics, DRP）作为实施基础设施，该技术整合三维成像（three-dimensional imaging）、关联化学分析（correlative chemistry）、基于人工智能的图像分析（AI-enabled image analysis）及孔隙尺度建模（pore-scale modelling），用以连接矿物结构与反应路径，支持矿石表征、解离预测、浸出、直接锂提取、矿山废物资源化及电池回收等决策。

Result: 论文制定了一项英国-欧洲政策议程，包括：翻译示范项目（translational demonstrators）、跨学科培训（cross-disciplinary training）、数字矿石护照标准（Digital Ore Passport standard）、联邦式数字矿石数据库（federated Digital Ore Database）以及综合地质-反应端站（integrated geo-reactive end stations）。

Conclusion: 如果将DRP作为共享实施基础设施加以对待，它能够帮助将关键矿产战略转化为保障供应安全、提高资源效率、促进循环性及实现更环保开发的实际路径。

Abstract: The United Kingdom and Europe are moving rapidly from critical minerals target-setting to implementation. The EU Critical Raw Materials Act and the UK's Vision 2035 create ambitious benchmarks for domestic extraction, processing, recycling, circularity, and supply-chain resilience, but many prospective regional resources remain complex, under-explored, historically worked, or economically marginal. This paper argues that implementation will depend not only on permitting reform and project designation, but also on pre-competitive measurement, modelling, and data infrastructure capable of determining which ores, brines, waste streams, and recycling feedstocks can be processed viably and with lower environmental impact. Digital Rock Physics (DRP) should therefore be understood as enabling infrastructure for resource policy rather than as a specialist laboratory method alone. By combining three-dimensional imaging, correlative chemistry, AI-enabled image analysis, and pore-scale modelling, DRP can connect mineral texture and reactive pathways to decisions about ore characterisation, liberation prediction, leaching, Direct Lithium Extraction, mine-waste valorisation, and battery recycling. The paper sets out a UK-European policy agenda built around translational demonstrators, cross-disciplinary training, a Digital Ore Passport standard, a federated Digital Ore Database, and integrated geo-reactive end stations. Treated as shared implementation infrastructure, DRP could help turn critical minerals strategies into practical routes for supply security, resource efficiency, circularity, and more environmentally responsible development.

</details>

### [31] [Early psychosis shows deviations in scaling behaviour within a critical regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06290)
*Irem Topal,Paola Moreno Ancalmo,Guillermo Montana Valverde,Philipp Homan,Wolfram Hinzen*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本研究结合现象学重整化群（PRG）、功率谱密度（PSD）和去趋势波动分析（DFA），发现早期精神病患者的大规模脑活动仍保持尺度不变（scale-invariant）组织，但其标度指数（scaling exponents）发生系统性偏移，提示疾病状态并非简单的临界性丧失，而是集体动力学的重组织。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有证据表明大脑大规模活动存在近临界动力学，且精神疾病中临界性相关指标出现改变，但这些发现分散于不同的观测变量和模态之间，尚不清楚不同的标度测量是否捕捉到大规模脑动力学的同一类变化。

Method: 采用静息态功能磁共振成像（resting-state fMRI）数据，结合现象学重整化群（phenomenological renormalization group, PRG）框架、功率谱密度（power spectral density, PSD）和去趋势波动分析（detrended fluctuation analysis, DFA），对早期精神病患者和健康对照者的大脑活动进行跨尺度的集体动力学表征。

Result: 健康对照组的静息态活动表现出非平凡的标度行为，符合临界类组织。早期精神病患者保留了同样的尺度不变组织的整体现象学，但多个观测变量上的标度指数出现系统性偏移。

Conclusion: 早期精神病并非简单的临界动力学丧失，而是在保留的标度体制内发生集体动力学的重组织。结合粗粒化（coarse-graining）方法与时间标度分析，为研究精神疾病中的大规模脑动力学提供了一个原则性框架。

Abstract: Accumulating evidence suggests that large-scale brain activity exhibits scale-invariant dynamics consistent with operation in a near-critical regime. Such dynamics have been associated with long-range correlations, efficient information processing, and the emergence of collective organization. While altered criticality-related measures have been reported in psychiatric disorders, previous findings remain fragmented across observables and modalities, making it unclear whether different scaling measures capture a common alteration of large-scale brain dynamics. Here, we investigated scaling properties in resting-state fMRI data from individuals with early psychosis and healthy controls. We combined a phenomenological renormalization group (PRG) framework with power spectral density (PSD) and detrended fluctuation analysis (DFA) to characterize collective dynamics across scales. In healthy controls, resting-state activity exhibited non-trivial scaling behavior consistent with critical-like organization. Early psychosis participants showed the same overall phenomenology of scale-invariant organization, but with systematic shifts in scaling exponents across multiple observables. These findings indicate that early psychosis is not characterized by a simple loss of critical-like dynamics, but rather by a reorganization of collective dynamics within a preserved scaling regime. More broadly, our results suggest that combining coarse-graining approaches with temporal scaling analyses provides a principled framework for studying large-scale brain dynamics in psychiatric disorders.

### [32] [Magnetic-field driven hybridization of heavy- and light-hole Rydberg excitons in GaAs quantum wells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05267)
*David de la Fuente Pico,Johannes Bürger,Antonio Gianfrate,Jesper Levinsen,Meera M. Parish,Daniele Sanvitto,Dario Ballarini,Francesca Maria Marchetti*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过理论建模与实验测量相结合，研究了法拉第几何下宽GaAs量子阱中基态和激发Rydberg激子态在磁场中的行为。基于Luttinger哈密顿量的多带激子模型统一处理了库仑相互作用、磁约束和能带混合，理论预测与高达9 T的偏振分辨磁反射测量结果高度吻合，表明价带混合对激发激子态的磁场依赖性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宽GaAs量子阱中Rydberg激子（Rydberg exciton）在磁场下的行为尚未被系统理解，特别是价带混合（valence-band mixing）对激发态激子性质的影响缺乏定量描述。本文旨在建立一个能够统一处理库仑相互作用、磁约束和能带混合的理论框架，并与实验对照验证。

Method: 采用基于Luttinger哈密顿量（Luttinger Hamiltonian）的多带激子模型，该模型捕捉了量子阱限制和磁场共同诱导的重空穴（heavy-hole）与轻空穴（light-hole）态之间的价带混合。发展了一种高效数值方法，在同等地位上处理库仑相互作用、磁约束和能带混合，系统表征激子能量、振子强度（oscillator strength）和轨道组成。

Result: 能带混合随磁场增强而增大，且对更高激发态更为显著——这些态在更低磁场下即出现混合并强烈改变其性质。对20 nm宽GaAs/Al$_{0.4}$Ga$_{0.6}$As量子阱进行最高9 T的偏振分辨磁反射（magneto-reflectance）测量，基态和前四个Rydberg激子的抗磁位移（diamagnetic shift）和塞曼分裂（Zeeman splitting）的理论预测与实验达到极好一致。

Conclusion: 价带混合在决定激发激子态的磁场依赖性中起关键作用，必须将其恰当地纳入模型才能对宽GaAs量子阱中的磁激子（magneto-exciton）进行定量描述。

Abstract: We present a combined theoretical and experimental study of ground and excited Rydberg exciton states in wide GaAs quantum wells exposed to a magnetic field in the Faraday geometry. We employ a multiband exciton model based on the Luttinger Hamiltonian, which captures valence-band mixing between heavy- and light-hole states induced by both the quantum well confinement and the magnetic field, and we develop an efficient numerical approach to solve for both ground- and excited-state excitons. The method treats Coulomb interactions, magnetic confinement, and band mixing on an equal footing, enabling a systematic characterization of exciton energies, oscillator strengths, and orbital composition. We show that band hybridization increases with magnetic field and is significantly more pronounced for higher excited states, where it sets in at lower fields and strongly modifies their properties. The theoretical predictions are validated by polarization-resolved magneto-reflectance measurements up to 9 T on GaAs/Al$_{0.4}$Ga$_{0.6}$As quantum wells of 20 nm width. We find excellent agreement for both the diamagnetic shift and Zeeman splitting of the ground state and the first four Rydberg excitons. Our results demonstrate that valence-band mixing plays a crucial role in determining the magnetic-field dependence of excited exciton states and must be properly included for a quantitative description of magneto-excitons in wide GaAs quantum wells.

### [33] [A nanoscale magnetic spectrum analyzer based on qubit dressed states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05426)
*Jan Rueschkamp,Shantam Ravan,Daniel Fernandez,Nazar Delegan,F. Joseph Heremans,David D. Awschalom,Ronald L. Walsworth,Nikola Maksimovic,Amir Yacoby*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过在动态解耦序列中引入微波缀饰场（microwave dressing field），克服了氮-空位（NV）中心量子传感器在带宽上的限制，成功实现了对纳米尺度自旋波动力学的宽带检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度上的磁场涨落现象广泛存在于电子与自旋动力学、量子多体系统及分子化学等领域，但现有传感器难以同时满足宽带（broad spectral bandwidth）、高灵敏度（high sensitivity）和纳米级空间分辨率（nanoscale spatial resolution）的要求。NV中心虽具备灵敏度和纳米级传感体积，但其带宽受限于量子控制序列的实际执行速度。

Method: 在动态解耦（dynamical decoupling）序列中，将NV量子比特（qubit）暴露于微波缀饰场下，该场既能放大目标信号，又能将任意频率的信号通过频率混频（frequency-mixing）方式搬移到动态解耦协议的检测带内。

Result: 利用该方法，NV中心成功在宽频率范围内检测到钇铁石榴石（yttrium-iron-garnet, YIG）薄膜中的相干及噪声纳米尺度自旋波动力学（spin wave dynamics）。

Conclusion: 该技术可推广至其他量子比特平台（qubit platforms），为跨物理与化学体系的纳米尺度光谱学（nanoscale spectroscopy）提供了一种通用框架。

Abstract: Magnetic field fluctuations on nanometer length scales manifest in a diverse range of phenomena -- electron and spin dynamics in materials and devices, quantum many-body systems, and molecular chemistry. Measuring these phenomena requires sensors with a challenging combination of broad spectral bandwidth, high sensitivity, and nanoscale spatial resolution. Nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers, atom-like quantum sensors in diamond, possess the requisite sensitivity and nanoscale sensing volume, but are typically limited in bandwidth by the practical speed of the applied quantum control sequence. Here, we overcome this limitation by exposing the NV qubit to a microwave dressing field during a dynamical decoupling sequence, which both amplifies and frequency-mixes target signals at arbitrary frequencies into the detection band of the dynamical decoupling protocol. We demonstrate this approach by using NV centers to detect both coherent and noisy nanoscale spin wave dynamics in a magnetic yttrium-iron-garnet (YIG) thin film over a broad frequency range. Our technique generalizes to other qubit platforms, providing a versatile framework for nanoscale spectroscopy across diverse physical and chemical systems.

</details>


### [34] [Realistic quantum device data synthesized by consumer AI and how to identify it](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05472)
*S. M. Frolov,O. V. Kravchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文探讨了生成式AI（generative AI）在模拟量子电子器件实验数据方面的能力，证明使用ChatGPT即可生成与其实现象（如量子比特控制、马约拉纳费米子等）高度相似的合成数据，并指出AI无需依赖专业数据集，仅需物理方程和实验信号基本特征即可构建逼真数据集。为防范合成数据被误当作真实实验数据，建议共享大量原始数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在文本和图像领域的伦理问题已引起广泛关注，但其对数值数据的分析、处理和合成能力相对较少被讨论。本文的核心动机是探究AI是否能够合成实验数据，使得领域专家认为这些数据具有科学意义，且与同行评审论文图表中的数据相当。

Method: 聚焦于量子电子器件（quantum electronic devices）领域——一个数据密集型的领域，涉及自旋电子学（spintronics）和量子计算（quantum computing）。使用广泛可用的ChatGPT生成与以下知名实验效应相关的信号：量子比特控制（quantum bit control）、马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermions）、约瑟夫森效应（Josephson effects）、量子点（quantum dots）和量子线（quantum wires）。

Result: AI能够生成与上述效应相关的显著信号。原因在于，量子器件中最清晰的数据可以用相对基础的数学模型表达，AI无需学习专门数据集，仅需掌握物理方程和实验信号的基本特征即可构建逼真的数据集。此外，AI可以对真实数据进行增强（data augmentation），并能模拟常见科学仪器的噪声（noise）。

Conclusion: 为确保已发表数据来自真实实验而非AI合成，建议共享大量原始数据。虽然AI轻松模仿几组数据是容易的，但持续生成长测量序列（long measured sequences）对合成数据的泛滥构成了足够大的障碍。

Abstract: With the advance of generative artificial intelligence (AI) synthetic texts and images have become commonplace. These capabilities offer clear benefits, but have also raised a number of ethical concerns that often have to do with misrepresenting AI outputs as genuine material. A lesser known capability of generative AI is to perform the basic analysis, processing and even synthesis of numerical data. This raises the question of whether AI can be used to imitate experimental data that an expert would consider scientifically meaningful and on par with data in the figures of peer-reviewed manuscripts? In this paper, we focus on synthesizing data inspired by well-known experiments done frequently on quantum electronic devices. This field is related to information technologies such as spintronics and quantum computing, and is considered data-rich and data-driven. We demonstrate that it is possible to generate dramatic signals associated with iconic effects such as quantum bit control, Majorana fermions, Josephson effects, quantum dots and wires using widely available ChatGPT. We find that because some of the clearest data from quantum devices can be expressed in terms of relatively basic mathematical models, AI does not need to learn on the specialized body of data. Instead, knowledge of the physics equations and of the basic features of experimental signals can go a long way towards building a realistic dataset. We also demonstrate that real data can be augmented by AI, and that AI can mimic the noise of common scientific instruments. To help assure that published data come from experiments and are not synthesized by AI, we recommend sharing large volumes of the primary data. While it is straightforward for AI to mimic a few sets of data, consistently generating long measured sequences poses sufficient barriers to the proliferation of undisclosed synthetic data.

</details>


### [35] [Majorana-like fermion physics: Emergence of topologically protected vortical states in graphene interacting with an electromagnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05746)
*H. V. Grushevskaya,George Krylov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 基于准相对论性石墨烯模型（该模型允许拓扑非平凡的类马约拉纳准粒子激发），研究了在外加电磁场下系统复介电常数的频率依赖关系中出现涡旋态，并将类马约拉纳模式的相互作用效应与光学响应中的法诺共振联系起来。该拓扑石墨烯模型被视为三味质量中微子振荡的玩具模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在允许拓扑非平凡的类马约拉纳（Majorana-like）准粒子激发的准相对论性石墨烯模型框架下，探究涡旋态在外加电磁场下系统复介电常数（complex dielectric permittivity）频率依赖关系中的出现。

Method: 采用准相对论性石墨烯模型，该模型支持具有非零Zak相位（Zak phases）作为拓扑荷（topological charges/flavours）的类马约拉纳准粒子激发，并定性分析类马约拉纳模式相互作用与法诺共振（Fano resonances）形成之间的关系。

Result: 石墨烯涡旋态具有非零Zak相位作为拓扑荷（味）；类马约拉纳模式的相互作用与光学响应中法诺共振的形成存在定性关联。

Conclusion: 所构建的石墨烯拓扑模型可被视为三味质量中微子振荡（three-flavour mass-neutrino oscillations）的玩具模型。

Abstract: Within the framework of a quasi-relativistic model of graphene that admits topologically nontrivial Majorana-like quasiparticle excitations, appearance of such vortex states in the frequency dependencies of the complex dielectric permittivity of the system subjected to an external electromagnetic field has been examined. The vortex graphene states possess topological charges (flavours ) being nonzero Zak phases. Interaction effects of Majorana-like modes have been qualitatively related to the formation of Fano resonances in the optical response. The constructed topological model of graphene may be considered as a toy model of three-flavour mass-neutrino oscillations.
