### [36] [Breakdown of Fluctuational Electrodynamics in the Extreme Near Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05845)
*Philippe Ben-Abdallah*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明了传统涨落电动力学（fluctuational electrodynamics）中不同物体热涨落统计独立的假设在极端近场区域失效，并建立了考虑界面间涨落电流关联的微观理论框架，修正了亚纳米间隙下的辐射热流预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涨落电动力学（fluctuational electrodynamics）长期依赖于不同物体中热涨落统计独立的基本假设，但该假设在极端近场区域的有效性尚未得到严格检验。

Method: 采用微观耦合振子模型（coupled-oscillator model）结合坡印廷矢量（Poynting vector）的格林张量（Green-tensor）公式，推导了由涨落电流互相关（fluctuating-current cross correlations）引入的辐射热流修正项。

Result: 对于支持表面声子极化激元（surface phonon-polaritons）的极性材料，当杂化能（hybridization energy）接近本征阻尼率时，关联效应变得显著，并在亚纳米尺度下大幅偏离传统涨落电动力学预测。

Conclusion: 研究建立了极端近场区域关联热涨落的微观理论框架，定量揭示了界面间电磁耦合对辐射传热（radiative heat transfer）的修正作用。

Abstract: Fluctuational electrodynamics relies on the assumption that thermal fluctuations in distinct bodies are statistically independent. We show that this approximation breaks down in the extreme near-field regime, where overlapping evanescent surface fields hybridize optical phonons across nanometric vacuum gaps and generate fluctuating-current cross correlations between opposite interfaces. Using a microscopic coupled-oscillator model combined with a Green-tensor formulation of the Poynting vector, we derive the resulting correlation-induced correction to the radiative heat flux. For polar materials supporting surface phonon-polaritons, these correlations become significant when the hybridization energy is comparable to the intrinsic damping rate and can substantially modify conventional fluctuational-electrodynamics predictions at subnanometric separations. Our results establish a microscopic framework for correlated thermal fluctuations in the extreme near-field regime and quantify their impact on radiative heat transfer.

</details>


### [37] [Non-adiabatic Ehrenfest dynamics with norm-conserving and ultra-soft pseudo-potentials with nuclear velocity corrections on the atomic orbitals within the Projector Augmented Wave Method framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06185)
*Paolo Fachin,Francesco Macheda,Paolo Barone,Francesco Mauri*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从第一性原理出发，推导了在原子轨道基组上包含核速度依赖相位（电子平移因子）的Ehrenfest分子动力学，并在Projector-Augmented-Wave（PAW）方法框架下分析了这些相位对赝势哈密顿量的影响，从而实现了非绝热过程的伽利略不变描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非绝热分子动力学中，当原子核被动态处理时，原子轨道基组会引入核速度依赖的相位（电子平移因子），这些相位在传统处理中常被忽略，导致虚假的非绝热耦合。本文旨在从第一性原理出发，系统推导这些相位的影响，并建立伽利略不变（Galilean-invariant）的非绝热Ehrenfest动力学框架。

Method: 基于第一性原理Ehrenfest分子动力学框架，在原子轨道（atomic-orbital）基组上引入核速度依赖相位。在Projector-Augmented-Wave（PAW）方法框架下，分别针对模守恒赝势（norm-conserving pseudo-potential）和超软赝势（ultra-soft pseudo-potential）两种情况，推导包含这些相位的有效哈密顿量。

Result: 在势能的非局域部分（non-local part）出现了依赖于核速度的Peierls-like相位；在超软赝势情况下，还出现了额外的核速度及加速度依赖的修正项。采用包含速度的原子轨道基组能够实现非绝热Ehrenfest分子动力学的伽利略不变描述，从而消除因忽略核速度相位而产生的虚假非绝热耦合。

Conclusion: 核速度依赖相位对基于局域化轨道的有效哈密顿量具有重要影响，系统纳入这些相位是构建伽利略不变的非绝热分子动力学方法的关键，有助于更准确地模拟涉及动态原子核的量子动力学过程。

Abstract: We derive the first-principles Ehrenfest molecular dynamics describing non-adiabatic processes with the inclusion of the nuclear-velocity-dependent phases (also known as electron-translation factors) on the atomic-orbital basis. These phases, appearing when nuclei are treated dynamically, affect effective Hamiltonians constructed from localised orbitals. In this work, we focus on the effects in the first-principles pseudo-potential Hamiltonian, both for the norm-conserving and ultra-soft cases, derived within the Projector-Augmented-Wave (PAW) method framework. Peierls-like phases depending on the nuclear velocities appear in the non-local part of the potential, while additional nuclear velocity and acceleration-dependent corrections appear in the ultra-soft pseudo-potential case. The use of velocity-including atomic orbital basis enables a Galilean-invariant description of the non-adiabatic Ehrenfest molecular dynamics, removing spurious non-adiabatic couplings that arise from neglecting the nuclear velocity phases in the atomic orbitals.

</details>


### [38] [Eigenmodes of synthetic antiferromagnetic skyrmions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06304)
*Kauser Zulfiqar,Martin Lang,Samuel J. R. Holt,Swapneel Amit Pathak,Florian Bruckner,Hans Fangohr*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过微磁学本征模和环降模拟，系统研究了受限合成反铁磁（SAF）斯格明子在方形、矩形、不等层厚及多斯格明子链等几何构型下的激发模式，发现反铁磁层间耦合显著改变了低频动力学，产生了准简并回旋模、线性平移模以及面外反相呼吸振荡等新特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注铁磁单层中的受限斯格明子激发模式，而合成反铁磁（SAF）双层结构中层间反铁磁耦合如何系统性地改变斯格明子的动力学行为尚缺乏全面的理解，特别是在不同几何约束下的模式演化规律。

Method: 采用微磁学本征模分析（micromagnetic eigenvalue simulation）和环降模拟（ringdown simulation）两种互补方法，系统研究了受限SAF斯格明子在方形、矩形、不等层厚及条带多斯格明子链等多种几何构型下的激发模式。

Result: 方形几何中出现了两个准简并的回旋模（gyrotropic mode），两层旋转方向相同；矩形几何中两层回旋方向相反，演化为近线性平移模（translational mode）；斯格明子链支持具有驻波状空间轮廓的集体平移模和呼吸模（breathing mode），并发现了两层反相振荡的SAF特有呼吸模式。

Conclusion: 该研究系统描述了受限几何、层内耦合与层间耦合相互作用下SAF斯格明子的集体动力学，为理解其激发行为提供了完整图景。

Abstract: We investigate the excitation modes of confined synthetic-antiferromagnetic (SAF) skyrmions using micromagnetic eigenvalue and ringdown simulations. Starting from a single skyrmion in a ferromagnetic layer, where the lowest-frequency modes are a gyrotropic and a breathing mode, we study how antiferromagnetic interlayer coupling modifies the dynamics in SAF bilayers. We consider several geometries: single SAF skyrmions in square and rectangular confinement, unequal layer thicknesses, and strips containing multiple skyrmions.
  The antiferromagnetic coupling strongly modifies the low-frequency dynamics. The square geometry exhibits two nearly degenerate gyrotropic modes, where in each both layers have the same rotation sense. In rectangular geometries, we instead find nearly linear SAF skyrmion translation emerging from opposite gyration sense in the two layers. These translational modes become the characteristic low-frequency excitations of SAF skyrmion chains.
  For skyrmion chains, we identify collective translational and breathing modes with standing-wave-like spatial profiles. Beyond ferromagnetic-like breathing modes, the SAF geometry supports breathing oscillations in which the two layers oscillate out of phase. We further demonstrate signal propagation along extended SAF skyrmion chains with propagation velocities comparable to ferromagnetic skyrmion chains.
  These results provide a systematic description of the collective dynamics of SAF skyrmions arising from the interplay of geometric confinement, intralayer, and interlayer coupling.

</details>

Method: 基于耦合量子点系统（coupled quantum-dot system），该系统通过隧穿耦合（tunnel-coupled）与金属热库（metallic thermal reservoirs）连接，利用热电流实现逻辑操作。同时提出一个实验方案，展示可实现的纳米电子量子电路架构（nano-electronic quantum circuit architecture）。

### [40] [1/3 Fractional and Gapless Integer Quantum Anomalous Hall States in Rhombohedral Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06450)
*Jackson P. Butler,Tonghang Han,Andrew DiFabbio,Zach Hadjri,Emily Aitken,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Long Ju,Raymond C. Ashoori*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在R5G/hBN莫尔超晶格中观测到了填充因子ν=1/3的分数量子反常霍尔（FQAH）效应，填补了该体系中最基本分数态的缺失；通过量子电容和输运测量，发现了从1/3分数陈绝缘体（FCI）到平庸电荷密度波态的拓扑相变，并揭示了体系在1/2填充附近出人意料的粒子-空穴对称性。此外，压缩率测量在ν=1附近区分了有能隙的整数量子反常霍尔态（IQAH）与无能隙、高可压缩的扩展量子反常霍尔态（EQAH），为在零磁场下实现任意子编织和非阿贝尔准粒子提供了热力学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在扭曲双层MoTe₂和菱方n层石墨烯/六方氮化硼（R$n$G/hBN）莫尔超晶格中均发现了分数量子反常霍尔（FQAH）效应，但Jain序列中1/3态——传统分数量子霍尔（FQH）体系中最鲁棒、最基本的态——在FQAH体系中一直缺失。确定其是否存在对理解FQAH机制（尤其是理论上仍有争议的R$n$G/hBN体系）至关重要。

Method: 本文在R5G/hBN莫尔超晶格器件中，通过量子电容（quantum capacitance）和输运（transport）测量的联合方法，在莫尔填充因子ν=1/3处观测FQAH效应；通过调控位移场（displacement field）研究拓扑相变，并结合压缩率（compressibility）测量在ν=1及ν≲1区域表征热力学性质。

Result: 在R5G/hBN中观测到ν=1/3的FQAH态；发现从1/3分数陈绝缘体（FCI）到平庸电荷密度波态的拓扑相变；加入1/3态后，FQAH态在1/2填充附近表现出与最低朗道能级中FQH态高度相似的粒子-空穴对称性；输运测量未显示整数量子反常霍尔态（IQAH）与扩展量子反常霍尔态（EQAH）区域之间的变化，但压缩率测量揭示了从有能隙的IQAH到无能隙、高可压缩的EQAH态的明确转变。

Conclusion: 在R5G/hBN中观测到最基础的1/3 FQAH态，完善了该体系的分数态序列并揭示其与FQH的深层相似性；对丰富相图的热力学表征为零磁场下任意子编织（anyon braiding）和非阿贝尔准粒子（non-Abelian quasiparticles）的工程实现铺平了道路。

Abstract: The fractional quantum anomalous Hall (FQAH) effect occurs in moiré superlattices in both twisted bilayer MoTe$_2$ and rhombohedral $n$-layer graphene aligned to hexagonal boron nitride (R$n$G/hBN) as a novel quantum phase driven by intertwined electron correlation and topology. Although several fractional states in the Jain sequence have been identified, the $1/3$ state, the most robust and fundamental state in conventional fractional quantum Hall (FQH) systems, was missing in either FQAH system. Determining whether it exists would have a major impact on understanding the mechanism of FQAH, especially in the theoretically still-debated R$n$G/hBN system. Here we report the FQAH effect at moiré filling factor $ν= 1/3$ in R$5$G/hBN moiré superlattice devices, through a combination of quantum capacitance and transport measurements. By tuning the displacement field, we observed a topological phase transition from a $1/3$ fractional Chern insulator (FCI) to a trivial charge density wave state. With the inclusion of the $1/3$ state, the FQAH states in R$5$G/hBN now exhibit a surprising level of particle-hole symmetry about half-filling, closely resembling the behavior of FQH states in the lowest Landau level. Additionally, we perform compressibility and transport measurements at a filling of one electron per moiré unit cell, $ν=1$, and also for $ν\lesssim 1$, where previous transport measurements displayed the extended quantum anomalous Hall (EQAH) effect. While our transport measurements show no change between the integer quantum anomalous Hall state (IQAH) and the EQAH region, compressibility measurements reveal a distinct transition from a gapped IQAH state to a gapless and highly compressible EQAH state. Our direct thermodynamic characterization of the rich phase diagram paves the way to engineering of anyon braiding and non-Abelian quasiparticles at zero magnetic field.

### [41] [Superconducting triode effect in a quantum-dot Josephson junction with a biased top gate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06465)
*Yu-Hang Li,Xiaan Du,Hua Jiang,X. C. Xie*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在非对称量子点约瑟夫森结（asymmetric quantum-dot Josephson junction）中实现的超导三极管效应（superconducting triode effect），该效应在保持时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）的前提下，通过顶部栅极（top gate）连续调控超电流的非互易性（non-reciprocity），并在射频辐射下实现全量子化的超电流整流（fully quantized supercurrent rectification）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect）需要同时破缺时间反演对称性和宇称对称性（parity symmetry）。本文旨在探索一种在不破缺时间反演对称性的条件下实现超电流非互易整流的新物理机制，并引入新的调控自由度。

Method: 采用非对称量子点约瑟夫森结，并附加一个金属顶栅极作为额外调控端。通过顶栅极破缺宇称对称性，同时明确保持时间反演对称性，从而实现对超电流非互易效应的连续调控。

Result: 该结中的超电流表现出强烈的非互易效应，可通过顶栅极连续调控以实现理想的单向超电流（unidirectional supercurrent），即超导三极管效应。在射频辐射下，结呈现高度不对称的夏皮罗台阶（Shapiro steps），实现全量子化的超电流整流。

Conclusion: 该工作为在明确保持时间反演对称性的约瑟夫森结中实现超导二极管效应提供了替代的物理机制，并引入了一种操控超电流非互易性的新调控手段（顶栅极）。

Abstract: Non-reciprocal supercurrents enable non-dissipative rectification, holding great promise for superconducting electronics. Conventionally, this non-reciprocity, termed the superconducting diode effect, requires the simultaneous breaking of time-reversal and parity symmetries. Here, we propose a superconducting triode effect in an asymmetric quantum-dot Josephson junction coupled to an additional metallic top gate, which breaks the parity symmetry while explicitly preserving time-reversal symmetry. We demonstrate that the supercurrent across this junction exhibits a strong non-reciprocal effect that can be continuously manipulated via the top gate to achieve an ideal unidirectional supercurrent, thus manifesting a superconducting triode effect. Furthermore, under radio-frequency radiation, this junction exhibits highly asymmetric Shapiro steps, realizing fully quantized supercurrent rectification. Our work not only provides an alternative physical mechanism for the superconducting diode effect observed in Josephson junctions with explicit time-reversal symmetry, but also introduces a new tuning knob to manipulate supercurrent non-reciprocity.

### [42] [Coherent room-temperature dipole synchronization in nanocavity sheets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06490)
*Rakesh Arul,Piper Fowler-Wright,Lille Borresen,Brendon W. Lovett,Jonathan Keeling,Jeremy J. Baumberg*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种在室温下由等离子体纳米腔（plasmonic nanocavity）二维阵列中局部有序的纳米间隙（nanogap）实现的同步偶极子态（synchronized dipole state），其特点是空间相干性显著但时间光子相干性快速衰减，区别于传统激光或玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索基于等离子体纳米腔（plasmonic nanocavity）亚纳米间隙中强近场耦合（strong near-field coupling）的空间远程发射偶极子（spatially distant emissive dipoles）同步现象，并实现室温下的稳定同步偶极子态。

Method: 采用非共振连续波（continuous-wave）泵浦局部有序的等离子体纳米间隙二维阵列（2D arrays），在室温条件下构建驱动-耗散系统（driven-dissipative system），通过测量空间相干性（spatial coherence）的g(1)分布、光谱宽度及发射方向性等表征同步态行为。

Result: 在泵浦增强条件下，观察到g(1)相干性的空间扩展，但并未出现光谱窄化（spectral narrowing）或定向发射；系统展现出快速的时间相干性衰减和复杂的空间关联。与激光、光子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体或激子-极化激元凝聚体不同，该系统表现为快速辐射与非辐射发射抑制了时间光子相干性。

Conclusion: 该室温同步偶极子态为研究驱动-耗散系统中的同步现象提供了新平台，结合超低模式体积（ultralow mode volumes）、高Purcell增强（high Purcell enhancement）及可扩展环境操作能力，有望推动新型光子与量子技术的发展。

Abstract: Plasmonic nanocavities enable the synchronization of spatially distant emissive dipoles through strong near-field coupling in sub-nm gaps. We report formation of a room-temperature synchronized dipole state in locally-ordered plasmonic nanogap 2D arrays under non-resonant continuous-wave pumping. Unlike lasers, photonic Bose-Einstein condensates, or exciton-polariton condensates, this system exhibits spatial coherence across the dipoles, while rapid radiative and non-radiative emission suppresses temporal photon coherence. A change of behaviour is observed with increasing pumping, marked by the spatial spread of g(1) coherence, but without spectral narrowing or directional emission. This driven-dissipative system exhibits fast temporal coherence decay and complex spatial correlations, offering a new platform for studying synchronization at room temperature. Combining ultralow mode volumes, high Purcell enhancement, and scalable ambient operation, it opens pathways for novel photonic and quantum technologies.

### [43] [Nonreversible Gauge Fields in Fokker--Planck Dynamics: Supersymmetric Hamiltonians and Learned Finite Forces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06412)
*Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个将非可逆Fokker–Planck动力学扰动形式化为“规范场”（gauge field）的统一框架，该扰动保持稳态密度不变但改变弛豫谱。基于算符视角（operator viewpoint），该框架统一描述了弛豫间隙、循环概率流、hypocoercive加速和有限控制成本，并引入正则化目标和actor–critic方法学习最优规范场。高斯Ornstein–Uhlenbeck和双阱势基准验证了该方法的有效性，并揭示了随机梯度方法（如Adam）与此框架的物理对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Fokker–Planck动力学研究在保持稳态不变的前提下引入非可逆扰动，但缺乏统一的语言来描述这类扰动对弛豫谱、概率流、加速收敛和有限控制成本的影响，也缺少系统的方法来学习最优扰动。本文旨在构建这一统一形式化框架（formalism），并解决规范场（gauge field）强度的自动选择问题。

Method: 作者将稳态密度保持的非可逆扰动形式化为反对称张量场（antisymmetric tensor field）表示的规范场，在可逆情形下通过相似变换将Fokker–Planck算符映射为Witten–Laplacian型超对称哈密顿量，非可逆规范则表现为保持零模但改变激发谱的非厄米扰动。利用连续时间谱隙无法唯一选择有限规范强度，作者引入有限时间正则化目标函数和actor–critic算法来学习规范场。

Result: 在可解析求解的各向异性高斯Ornstein–Uhlenbeck过程中，谱跃迁（spectral transition）与有限时间最优规范强度出现分离，学习得到的规范场恢复了Lyapunov方程的最优解。在双阱势非凸亚稳态势垒基准中，同样的约束选择机制仍然成立。随机梯度方法中的小批量噪声表现为有效扩散张量，Adam等自适应方法对应于具有可能非平衡电流的度量选择。

Conclusion: 该框架为统一理解非可逆Fokker–Planck动力学中的弛豫间隙、hypocoercivity和有限时间控制成本提供了算符语言，并建立了随机梯度方法（如SGD和Adam）与物理Fokker–Planck系统之间的形式对应关系，具有向更复杂系统推广的潜力。

Abstract: We formulate stationary-density-preserving nonreversible perturbations of Fokker--Planck dynamics as gauge fields that deform relaxation spectra while leaving the invariant state fixed. When detailed balance holds, a similarity transformation maps the reversible Fokker--Planck operator to a Witten-Laplacian-type supersymmetric Hamiltonian; nonreversible gauges then appear as non-Hermitian perturbations that preserve the zero mode but modify the excited spectrum. This operator viewpoint gives a common language for relaxation gaps, circulating probability currents, hypocoercive acceleration, and finite control costs. We represent admissible gauge currents by antisymmetric tensor fields and identify the detailed-balance-violating Ohzeki--Ichiki force as a constant symplectic example whose infinite-strength limit is Hamiltonian dynamics. The continuous-time spectral gap alone does not select a finite gauge strength, so we introduce a finite-time regularized objective and an actor--critic procedure for learning the gauge. An exactly solvable anisotropic Gaussian Ornstein--Uhlenbeck benchmark separates the spectral transition from the finite-time optimum and shows that the learned gauge recovers the Lyapunov-equation optimum. A double-well benchmark then illustrates the same constrained selection in a nonconvex metastable landscape. Stochastic gradient methods enter this framework as physically relevant Fokker--Planck systems: mini-batch noise acts as an effective diffusion tensor, and adaptive methods such as Adam correspond to metric choices with possible nonequilibrium currents.

</details>

### [44] [Quantifying the biophysical properties of stomatocytes in health and disease](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05227)
*Zhaojie Chai,Jianlu Zheng,He Li,Ming Dao,George Em Karniadakis*

Main category: q-bio.CB

TL;DR: 本研究结合耗散粒子动力学模拟与微流控成像，构建了覆盖遗传性口形红细胞增多症（HS）全范围的三种口形红细胞模型，通过五种力学正交测试发现：脾窦间隙穿越由几何形状主导，解释了脾切除的疗效悖论；脱水型红细胞虽易通过脾脏，但抑制膜坦克履带运动并将低剪切全血粘度提高约29%，其微流控中心线偏移信号可无标记区分四种红细胞表型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遗传性口形红细胞增多症（HS）中，脾切除术对过水化型（OHS）有效但对脱水型（DHS）可能引发血栓风险，这一悖论长期未解，原因是现有方法仅能零散测量红细胞生物力学参数，缺乏统一框架。

Method: 采用耗散粒子动力学（DPD）模拟结合微流控成像，在固定膜面积下构建一个正常盘状红细胞和三种体积递减（109.7, 101.5, 89.8 fL）的口形红细胞模型（ST-RBC1-3），覆盖OHS至DHS范围，并在五种力学正交测试中追踪剪切模量、弯曲刚度、表面积体积比（S/V）和细胞质粘度等参数。

Result: 内皮间隙穿越由几何形状主导：过水化ST-RBC1所需临界压力比健康红细胞高一个数量级，而脱水ST-RBC3可自由通过；ST-RBC3抑制膜坦克履带运动（tank-treading），在生理血细胞比容下将低剪切全血粘度提高约29%，堪比戈谢病高粘滞血症；漏斗障碍芯片可将差异放大为中心线偏移信号，预测可分离所有四种红细胞类型（极端表型间约4.5标准差）。

Conclusion: 该研究将单细胞力学、脾过滤和血液流变学统一在一个框架内，解决了脾切除悖论，并为HS的微流控术前风险分层提供了方向。

Abstract: Hereditary stomatocytosis (HS) comprises red blood cell (RBC) disorders characterized by cup-shaped erythrocytes that respond oppositely to splenectomy: curative in overhydrated HS (OHS) but potentially thrombogenic in dehydrated HS (DHS/xerocytosis). This paradox persists because RBC biomechanics is governed by partly independent parameters--shear modulus, bending rigidity, surface-to-volume ratio (S/V), and cytoplasmic viscosity--that existing assays capture only piecemeal. Here we combine dissipative particle dynamics (DPD) simulations with microfluidic imaging to construct a control discocyte and three stomatocyte models (ST-RBC1-3) at fixed membrane area and decreasing volume (109.7, 101.5, 89.8 fL), spanning the OHS-to-DHS range. Tracing this parameter set through five mechanically orthogonal assays, we find that interendothelial-slit (IES) traversal is geometry-dominated: overhydrated ST-RBC1 requires an order of magnitude higher critical pressure than healthy RBCs, whereas dehydrated ST-RBC3 passes freely. ST-RBC3 nonetheless suppresses membrane tank-treading and raises low-shear whole-blood viscosity by ~29% at physiological haematocrit, comparable to Gaucher-disease hyperviscosity. A funnel-obstacle chip amplifies these differences into a label-free centerline-offset signal predicted to separate all four RBC types (~4.5 standard deviations between extreme phenotypes). These results unite single-cell mechanics, splenic filtration, and hemorheology in one framework, resolve the splenectomy paradox, and point toward microfluidic pre-operative risk stratification in HS.

</details>

### [45] [On the potential for inhomogeneities to mimic an evolving dark energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05479)
*Hayley J. Macpherson,Georgios Valogiannis*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 通过数值相对论模拟和广义相对论光线追踪，本工作发现宇宙中的非均匀性（inhomogeneities）可能导致合成观测者推断出暗能量（dark energy）状态方程（equation of state）的视在时间演化，即使宇宙平均而言由宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）描述。在20个观测者样本中，有一个观测者以2-σ显著性推断出与DESI一致的非LCDM参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非均匀性改变宇宙膨胀历史（expansion history）并非新观点，但鉴于DESI结合CMB和超新星观测推断暗能量状态方程存在时间演化这一发现引发广泛关注，有必要重新审视非均匀性对暗能量参数推断的影响。

Method: 采用大尺度结构形成（large-scale structure formation）的数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟，结合非线性广义相对论光线追踪（nonlinear general-relativistic ray tracing），为合成观测者推断暗能量参数；采用简化设置以粗略模拟DESI、超新星和CMB约束的观测特性。

Result: 在20个合成观测者的小样本中，有一个观测者推断出与DESI值在2-σ显著性下一致的参数。尽管在有限样本中这一情形罕见，但表明观测者至少有可能推断出显著的非LCDM参数，即使其宇宙平均而言由宇宙学常数很好地描述。

Conclusion: 非均匀性可以导致暗能量参数出现视在时间演化信号的假象，这至少为部分DESI观测结果提供了一种可能的系统学解释，同时也对仅依据当前观测数据就推断暗能量本质持谨慎态度提供了理论支持。

Abstract: In this work we explore the ability of inhomogeneities to result in an apparent dynamical evolution of dark energy. The idea that inhomogeneities may alter the expansion history of the Universe is not a new one. However, with the current excitement surrounding the inferred time-evolution of the equation of state of dark energy by the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI), combined with Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) and supernovae observations, it is worth revisiting. We use numerical relativity simulations of large-scale structure formation combined with nonlinear general-relativistic ray tracing to infer dark energy parameters for synthetic observers. We adopt a simplified set-up to roughly mimic the observational properties of the DESI plus supernovae and CMB constraints. In our small sample of 20 observers, we find one who infers parameters consistent with the DESI values at 2-$σ$ significance. While it is rare in our limited sample size, we show that it is at least possible for observers to infer significant non-LCDM parameters when their universe is well-described by a cosmological constant on average.

</details>


### [46] [The Atacama Cosmology Telescope: Probing new signatures of ultralight axions with gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06410)
*Alex Laguë,Keir K. Rogers,Mathew S. Madhavacheril,J. Richard Bond,Erminia Calabrese,Mark J. Devlin,Jo Dunkley,Vera Gluscevic,Renée Hložek,Hidde T. Jense,Thibaut Louis,Frank J. Qu,Bernardita Ried Guachalla,Neelima Sehgal,Blake D. Sherwin,Suzanne T. Staggs,Alexander van Engelen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文利用普朗克（Planck）、阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜（ACT）和南极望远镜（SPT-3G）的宇宙微波背景（CMB）引力透镜数据，结合先进的模拟校准非线性成团模型，对超轻轴子（ULA）暗物质候选者给出了目前最强的质量约束：质量$10^{-26}$ eV的轴子占暗物质比例低于1.5%，$10^{-25}$ eV的轴子低于9%（95%置信水平），并在$10^{-24.5}$ eV处发现微弱的非零轴子密度偏好（2.1σ）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻轴子（ULA）是标准模型（Standard Model）诸多扩展中自然涌现的暗物质候选粒子，其中质量$m_\mathrm{a} \lesssim 10^{-27}$ eV的ULA已受到CMB温度与极化观测的强约束。然而，在更高质量区间（$10^{-26}\;\mathrm{eV}\leq m_\mathrm{a}\leq 10^{-24.5}\;\mathrm{eV}$）的ULA仍可能以暗物质百分之几的比例存在，并有潜力缓和物质成团性（matter clustering）推断之间的张力，因此需要利用CMB引力透镜数据进一步检验这一参数空间。

Method: 该工作拟合了Plank、ACT和SPT-3G三组实验的CMB引力透镜（gravitational lensing）最新测量数据，采用经过模拟校准（simulation-calibrated）的非线性成团模型（nonlinear clustering model）描述ULA的宇宙学行为，从而在相关质量区间内提取约束条件。

Result: 研究给出了该质量区间内目前最强的约束：$10^{-26}$ eV的ULA占暗物质比例低于1.5%，$10^{-25}$ eV的轴子占比低于9%（两者均为95%置信水平）。在$10^{-24.5}$ eV处检测到2.1σ的非零轴子密度偏好，但该信号主要由少数数据点驱动。

Conclusion: 当前数据在$10^{-24.5}$ eV处显示出微弱的非零轴子密度偏好，但因其主要来自少数数据点，该信号尚需进一步的非线性ULA物理研究才能确认或排除。总体而言，中低质量区的ULA在暗物质占比上受到显著限制。

Abstract: Ultralight axions (ULAs) are well-motivated dark matter particle candidates that arise in many extensions of the Standard Model of particle physics. ULAs with mass $m_\mathrm{a} \lesssim 10^{-27}$ eV have been strongly constrained by cosmic microwave background (CMB) observations in temperature and polarization. We fit recent measurements of gravitational lensing of the CMB from \textit{Planck}, the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) and the South Pole Telescope (SPT-3G) using a state-of-the-art simulation-calibrated nonlinear clustering model for ULAs. We derive the strongest constraints on ULAs in the mass range $10^{-26}\;\mathrm{eV}\leq m_\mathrm{a}\leq 10^{-24.5}\;\mathrm{eV}$. ULAs of this mass have been shown to alleviate tensions between inferences of the matter clustering if they compose a few percent of the total dark matter content of the Universe. We conclude that ULAs with a mass of $10^{-26}$ eV make up less than 1.5\% of the dark matter and $10^{-25}$ eV axions make less than 9\% (both at 95\% confidence level). We identify a slight preference for non-zero axion density at $10^{-24.5}$ eV at $2.1σ$. We find that the preference for ULAs is largely driven by a few data points and that further investigation of non-linear ULA physics is needed to confirm or rule out this signal.

### [47] [Phenomenology of Inflaton-Driven Early QCD Confinement and Solution to Axion Isocurvature Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06484)
*Evangelos I. Sfakianakis,Barmak Shams Es Haghi,Katherine Freese*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过暴胀子（inflaton）与标准模型胶子（gluons）的直接耦合来动态调制QCD禁闭标度（confinement scale）的机制，使轴子（axion）在宇宙微波背景（CMB）时期变重以压制等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations），随后变轻以通过德西特（de Sitter）涨落或热涨落产生暗物质（dark matter）。该机制嵌入α-吸引子（α-attractor）暴胀模型，并分析了再加热（reheating）途径、超对称（supersymmetry）及再加热温度等参数空间的可实现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准QCD轴子作为暗物质候选者时，在暴胀期间产生的等曲率扰动会对CMB观测造成显著约束，传统模型难以同时满足轴子质量与暗物质丰度的要求。本文旨在通过暴胀期间动态调控QCD禁闭标度，使轴子质量先重后轻，从而同时解决等曲率扰动压制与暗物质产生的问题。

Method: 引入暴胀子与标准模型胶子的直接耦合，动态改变QCD禁闭标度（confinement scale）的时间演化；将这一机制嵌入α-吸引子（α-attractor）暴胀模型，系统扫描参数空间；分别考虑再加热通过胶子、通过重右手中微子（heavy right-handed neutrinos）及自由再加热温度三种情景，并在超对称框架下分析大汤川耦合（Yukawa couplings）导致的圈图修正（loop corrections）对暴胀动力学的影响。

Result: 在最小情景（再加热通过胶子）中，成功产生暗物质要求退禁闭（deconfinement）在CMB窗口之后不久发生。通过重右手中微子再加热通常需要大汤川耦合，进而产生可观圈图修正破坏暴胀动力学，但超对称可以缓解这一冲突；对超对称破缺（SUSY breaking）标度的约束使得该机制在高原暴胀（plateau models of inflation）模型中仍可行。将再加热温度（reheat temperature）作为自由参数可进一步扩大可行参数空间。

Conclusion: 动态调制QCD禁闭标度的机制为轴子暗物质与暴胀宇宙学提供了统一的解释框架。在α-吸引子模型框架下，该机制在多种再加热途径中均有可行的参数区域，且超对称的引入能够缓解大汤川耦合带来的动力学问题，为未来CMB及暗物质实验提供了可检验的预言。

Abstract: We study the phenomenology of early QCD confinement during inflation, driven by a direct coupling between the inflaton and Standard Model gluons. This coupling dynamically raises the QCD confinement scale, making the axion sufficiently heavy to suppress isocurvature perturbations during the CMB epoch. As inflation proceeds, the confinement scale decreases and the axion becomes light, allowing de Sitter fluctuations during the late stages of inflation or post-inflationary thermal fluctuations to generate the observed dark matter abundance. In addition, QCD-induced corrections to the inflationary potential can shift the scalar spectral index towards smaller values, providing a further observational handle. We embed this mechanism in an $α$-attractor model of inflation and explore the resulting parameter space. We show that, in the minimal scenario with reheating into gluons, successful dark matter production requires deconfinement to occur shortly after the CMB window. Extensions involving reheating through heavy right-handed neutrinos generally require large Yukawa couplings, which induce sizable loop corrections that spoil inflationary dynamics. We show that this tension can be resolved in the presence of supersymmetry and derive constraints on the SUSY breaking scale that allow the mechanism to remain viable within plateau models of inflation. Treating the reheat temperature as a free parameter further enlarges the viable parameter space.

</details>

### [48] [Gradient descent at the Edge of Stability: free energy model and kinetic description of the two-layer network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05326)
*Antonin Chodron de Courcel*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对梯度下降在“不稳定边缘（Edge of Stability）”动态中的行为，提出了一种连续时间有效模型（continuous-time effective model），通过耦合平均轨迹与快速振荡的时间平均协方差，引入包含曲率相关“熵”项的有效自由能（effective free energy），并推导出描述权重及其波动联合分布的均值场动力学方程（mean-field kinetic equation），在矩阵分解与深度学习任务（CIFAR-10）上验证了该模型对振荡包络的捕捉能力与自由能的预测效力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Edge of Stability训练体制（Edge of Stability regime）下，当学习率较大时，损失函数与锐度（sharpness）会出现持续振荡，传统的梯度下降分析方法难以捕捉这一不稳定动态。

Method: 1) 提出连续时间有效模型，耦合平均轨迹与快速振荡的时间平均协方差。2) 定义有效自由能，将原始风险泛函（risk functional）与曲率相关的“熵”项相结合。3) 针对宽两层神经网络（wide two-layer neural networks）在稳定非零振荡下的优化，推导均值场极限（mean-field limit），得到描述权重及其波动联合分布的新型动力学方程（kinetic equation），并证明该方程可解释为宏观自由能的Wasserstein-2梯度流（Wasserstein-2 gradient flow）。

Result: 模型能够在平均权重与振荡动态时间尺度相近的情形下追踪振荡包络（envelope of the oscillations），即捕获某些神经网络架构训练中出现的尖峰（spikes）。在矩阵分解和CIFAR-10深度学习任务上的数值实验验证了模型对振荡包络的准确性以及有效自由能的预测能力。

Conclusion: Edge of Stability动态中，有效自由能是监控不稳定训练的关键量；所提出的均值场动力学方程及其Wasserstein-2梯度流解释为该类振荡动态提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of gradient descent in the Edge of Stability regime, where the learning rate is large enough to induce persistent oscillations in the loss and the sharpness. We propose a continuous-time effective model that tracks the evolution of the average trajectory coupled with the time-averaged covariance of its fast oscillations. Our analysis reveals that the natural quantity to monitor in such unstable regimes is an effective free energy, which combines the original risk functional with a curvature-related "entropic" term. Our model allows us to track the envelope of the oscillations even in situations where its dynamics evolve on similar timescales as the averaged weights. Otherwise stated, we can track the spikes that occur during the training of some neural network architectures. For wide two-layer neural networks optimized under stable non-vanishing oscillations, we derive a mean-field limit that results in a novel kinetic equation describing the joint distribution of weights and their fluctuations. We show that this equation can be interpreted as a Wasserstein-2 gradient flow of a macroscopic free energy. Finally, we provide numerical evidence on matrix factorization and deep learning tasks (CIFAR-10) to demonstrate the model's accuracy in capturing the envelope of the oscillations and the predictive power of the effective free energy.

</details>

### [49] [HVPE Growth of Si-Doped $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ on Sapphire: Influence of Substrate Offcut on Structural and Electrical Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05607)
*Sourav Sarker,Saleh Ahmed Khan,Ahmed Ibreljic,Anhar Bhuiyan*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文采用氢化物气相外延（HVPE）在蓝宝石衬底上异质外延生长掺硅的β-Ga₂O₃薄膜，系统研究了蓝宝石斜切角（offcut）对生长动力学、表面形貌、晶体质量和电输运特性的影响。结果表明，增大斜切角可显著改善表面形貌和晶体质量，并在6°斜切衬底上实现了100 cm²/V·s的最高室温电子迁移率，为在低成本异质衬底上规模化制备高质量β-Ga₂O₃外延层提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: β-Ga₂O₃是一种宽禁带半导体，在功率电子器件领域具有重要应用前景，但高质量外延生长尤其是异质外延在低成本衬底上的实现仍面临挑战。本文旨在通过系统研究蓝宝石衬底斜切角对HVPE生长β-Ga₂O₃薄膜的影响，探索优化生长条件以提升晶体质量和电学性能的途径。

Method: 采用氢化物气相外延（hydride vapor phase epitaxy, HVPE）在蓝宝石（sapphire）衬底上异质外延生长掺硅的β-Ga₂O₃薄膜，系统改变衬底斜切角（offcut angle，0°至8°）以及生长参数（HCl流量、生长压力、源-衬底距离），并通过生长动力学、表面形貌、摇摆曲线半高宽及温度依赖的电输运测量对薄膜进行表征。

Result: 生长速率最高可达30 μm/hr；随着斜切角从0°增大至8°，表面形貌从多方向生长转变为高度有序的台阶主导表面，表面粗糙度从14.69 nm降至2.74 nm，摇摆曲线（rocking-curve）半高宽（FWHM）从994 arcsec降至414 arcsec。在6°斜切衬底上，载流子浓度范围为1.0×10¹⁷至3.4×10¹⁸ cm⁻³，最大室温电子迁移率（electron mobility）为100 cm²/V·s（对应载流子浓度1.0×10¹⁷ cm⁻³），为HVPE在异质衬底上生长β-Ga₂O₃的最高报道值。施主激活能（donor activation energy）分别为35 meV和90 meV，受主浓度（acceptor concentration）低至3×10¹⁵ cm⁻³。

Conclusion: HVPE方法能够在低成本蓝宝石异质衬底上生长出具有良好晶体质量和载流子输运特性的高质量β-Ga₂O₃外延层，通过优化衬底斜切角可显著提升薄膜性能，为β-Ga₂O₃的可规模化异质外延提供了有前景的技术路线。

Abstract: Si-doped $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ films were heteroepitaxially grown on sapphire substrates using HVPE. The influence of sapphire offcut on growth kinetics, surface morphology, crystalline quality, and electrical transport properties was systematically investigated. Growth kinetics studies revealed a strong dependence of deposition rate on HCl flow, growth pressure, and source-to-substrate distance, with growth rates reaching up to 30 $μ$m/hr. Increasing sapphire offcut angle from 0$^\circ$ to 8$^\circ$ promoted a transition from multidirectional growth to highly aligned terrace-dominated surfaces, reducing the surface roughness from 14.69 to 2.74 nm. The improved surface morphology was accompanied by enhanced crystalline quality, with phase-pure (-201)-oriented $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ growth and a reduction in the rocking-curve full width at half maximum from 994 to 414 arcsec as the sapphire offcut increased. Electrical characterization of films grown on 6$^\circ$ offcut substrates yielded carrier concentrations ranging from $1.0\times10^{17}$ to $3.4\times10^{18}$ cm$^{-3}$. A maximum room-temperature electron mobility of 100cm$^2$/V$\cdot$s was achieved at a carrier concentration of $1.0\times10^{17}$cm$^{-3}$, representing the highest reported room-temperature mobility for HVPE-grown $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ on a foreign substrate. Analysis of the temperature-dependent transport characteristics yielded donor activation energies of 35 and 90 meV together with a low acceptor concentration of $3\times10^{15}$ cm$^{-3}$, consistent with the improved crystalline quality achieved on the offcut sapphire substrates. These results demonstrate that HVPE is capable of producing high-quality $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ heteroepitaxial layers with good crystalline quality and carrier transport characteristics, providing a promising pathway for scalable $β$-Ga$_2$O$_3$ epitaxy on low-cost foreign substrates.

</details>


### [50] [Electrolyte Bonding Engineering for Highly Uniform GeTe-based CBRAM and Parallel Hebbian Learning in Selector-free Hopfield Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05768)
*Jiin Bang,Jingyeong Hwang,Unhyeon Kang,Seungmin Oh,Kyungmin Lee,Jaehyun Park,Younghyun Lee,Hyun Jae Jang,Seongsik Park,YeonJoo Jeong,Inho Kim,Jong Keuk Park,Suyoun Lee*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过调控Ge-Te固态电解质的组分（优化比为Ge₃.₅Te₁）将导电桥随机存取存储器（CBRAM）的器件间电阻变异性（D2D variability）抑制约三个数量级，并基于该均匀性提升，在无选择器（selector-less）的16×16交叉阵列上构建了4×4 Hopfield联想记忆网络，实现了二值模式对的并行编程与成功召回，为无选择器硬件实现联想记忆提供了概念验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hopfield网络为节能型联想记忆提供了硬件友好的框架，但其在忆阻器（memristor）交叉阵列中的实际应用受到器件间变异性的严重阻碍，该变异性使得可靠的并行编程（parallel programming）难以实现。本文旨在通过电解质组分工程解决这一瓶颈问题。

Method: 在导电桥随机存取存储器（CBRAM）器件中，系统调控Ge-Te固态电解质的Ge:Te组分比，通过拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）表征键合网络结构；将优化后的Cu/Ge₃.₅Te₁ CBRAM集成到无选择器的16×16交叉阵列中，采用半选择方案（half-selection scheme）实现4×4 Hopfield联想网络的完全并行编程。

Result: Ge₃.₅Te₁电解质组分将被选为最优，其随机电阻变异相较于GeSe基器件抑制了约三个数量级；拉曼光谱显示该改进源于以非对称伸缩GeTe₄四面体单元为主的键合网络，该网络形成相互连通的自由体积通道，限制并稳定了Cu⁺离子的迁移路径。基于此均匀性，在无选择器16×16交叉阵列上演示了可学习与召回二值模式对的4×4 Hopfield联想网络，在无选择器条件下成功召回最多两个存储关联。

Conclusion: 结果表明，电解质键合结构在决定忆阻器均匀性中起关键作用，提供了一条面向可扩展、并行神经形态计算系统（neuromorphic computing systems）的材料驱动路径。该工作为无选择器硬件实现联想记忆建立了概念验证（proof-of-concept）。

Abstract: Hopfield networks offer a hardware-friendly framework for energy-efficient associative memory, yet their practical realization in memristor crossbar arrays is critically hindered by device-to-device (D2D) variability, which prevents reliable parallel programming. Here, we address this bottleneck through systematic composition engineering of the Ge-Te solid electrolyte in conductive bridge random access memory (CBRAM) devices. By varying the Ge:Te ratio, we identify Ge3.5Te1 as an optimal electrolyte composition that suppresses stochastic resistance variation by approximately three orders of magnitude compared to GeSe-based devices. Raman spectroscopy reveals that this dramatic improvement originates from a bonding network dominated by asymmetric-stretching GeTe4 tetrahedral units, which form interconnected free-volume channels that confine and stabilize Cu+ ion migration pathways. Leveraging this enhanced uniformity, we fabricate a selector-less 16x16 Cu/Ge3.5Te1 CBRAM crossbar array and demonstrate a 4x4 Hopfield associative network capable of learning and recalling binary pattern pairs via fully parallel programming using a half-selection scheme. Successful pattern recall is achieved for up to two stored associations despite the absence of selector elements, establishing a proof-of-concept for selector-free hardware implementations of associative memory. These results highlight the critical role of electrolyte bonding structure in determining memristor uniformity and provide a materials-driven pathway toward scalable, parallel neuromorphic computing systems.

</details>

### [51] [GPU optical photon Monte Carlo for noble liquid detectors: validation against Geant4 in a large liquid argon TPC benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05385)
*Gabor Galgoczi,Xuyang Ning,Dmitri Smirnov,Brett Viren,Chao Zhang*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出 Simphony（原名 EIC-Opticks），一种基于 GPU（CUDA 和 NVIDIA OptiX）的光学光子蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟工具，用于替代传统基于 CPU 的 Geant4 光学模拟。在 14.7 kt 液氩时间投影室（Time Projection Chamber）基准测试中，Simphony 与 Geant4 在探测光子比、时间谱和波长谱上达到亚百分比级别的一致性，并在 NVIDIA RTX 4090 上实现了约 1053 倍的光学传输加速和 89 倍的端到端加速，使大规模光学光子蒙特卡洛模拟在探测器开发与机器学习数据集生成中变得实用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光学光子蒙特卡洛模拟是稀有液体时间投影室（Time Projection Chamber, TPC）中计算开销最大的环节。传统的基于 CPU 的 Geant4 模拟在处理大量光学光子时效率低下，难以满足探测器设计研究中重复的几何相关模拟以及重建与粒子识别工作流中对标注光学数据集的需求。

Method: Simphony 在 Opticks 框架基础上集成了 CUDA 和 NVIDIA OptiX 光线追踪引擎，实现了 Geant4 中 G4OpWLS 波长位移模型（wavelength-shifting model）的 GPU 版本。该工具能返回每次探测命中（detected hit）的蒙特卡洛真值（Monte Carlo truth），且每个光子的额外开销较低。

Result: 在简化 14.7 kt 液氩 TPC 基准测试中，三次 2.5 GeV 电子配对模拟各产生约 6100 万光学光子，Simphony 与 Geant4 的集成探测光子比在亚百分比级别一致，到达时间谱和波长谱的卡方自由度比（$\chi^2/\text{ndf}$）分别为 0.98 和 1.08。包含μ子和近切伦科夫阈值质子样本的比率 $R_N$ 分别为 $1.0017\pm0.0008$ 和 $1.0005\pm0.0014$。在 RTX 4090 上，四个 2.5 GeV 电子事件的叠加发射传输 2.43 亿光学光子仅需 $3.03\pm0.06$ 秒，光学传输速度提升为 $1053\pm55$ 倍，端到端时间加速为 $89\pm5$ 倍。

Conclusion: Simphony 使显式光学光子蒙特卡洛模拟在探测器开发研究和机器学习光学响应数据集生成中变得实用，验证了 GPU 加速光学模拟在大规模粒子探测器应用中的可行性与高效性。

Abstract: Optical photon Monte Carlo simulation is a computational bottleneck for noble liquid Time Projection Chambers. Design studies require repeated, geometry dependent simulations of timing, wavelength shifting, and optical response, while reconstruction and particle identification workflows need labeled optical datasets. We present Simphony, a GPU optical simulation tool, formerly EIC-Opticks, built on Opticks with CUDA and NVIDIA OptiX. Simphony implements a GPU version of the Geant4 G4OpWLS wavelength-shifting model and returns Monte Carlo truth for detected hits with low per-photon overhead. We validate Simphony against Geant4 11.3.2 in a simplified \SI{14.7}{kt} liquid argon Time Projection Chamber benchmark with a two-stage wavelength-shifting shell and idealized photon counting detector. For three paired \SI{2.5}{GeV} electron simulations, each producing about 61 M optical photons, the integrated detected-photon ratio agrees with Geant at the subpercent level. The detected arrival time and wavelength spectra give \chisqndf values of 0.98 and 1.08. Contained muon and near-Cerenkov-threshold proton samples give $R_N=1.0017\pm0.0008$ and $R_N=1.0005\pm0.0014$, confirming agreement for distinct source topologies. On an NVIDIA RTX 4090, a stacked launch of four 2.5 GeV electron events transports 243 M optical photons in $3.03\pm0.06$ s, giving $80.2\pm1.6$ M photons s$^{-1}$. Relative to a single-thread Geant reference and including GPU overheads and host-device transfers, the optical transport speedup is $1053\pm55$; the end-to-end wall time acceleration is $89\pm5$. These results show that Simphony can make explicit optical photon Monte Carlo practical for detector development studies and for generating machine learning optical response datasets.

*J. D. Kalow,J. T. Hinchen,G. Harris,E. Koukina,D. M. Harrington,P. C. McDaniel,N. J. Brennan,A. Golossanov,I. D. Spool D. Zajac,M. Mundt,S. Varner,M. Russell,S. Bull,K. McCormack,D. Mayer,L. E. Knaian,M. Khandaker,W. Stadolnik,W. R. Cutler,A. Sampat,K. Lau,J. Betances,C. Fagan,C. R. Shmayda,M. Koch,K. Payne,N. J. L. MacFadden,J. Simon,K. Peterson,A. Gami,S. Machavarapu,A. Tejeda,J. Katz,J. Method: 开发了MuFusE专用的大体积金刚石对顶砧（DAC），集成了低温装样、全金属密封和柔性波纹管（bellows），配合远程气动驱动和二次安全壳（secondary containment），采用5 mm直径金刚石砧（diamond anvil）并取向于高强μ子束路径；通过激光光谱法（laser spectroscopy）原位测量样品压力和组成。

Result: 装置在液体密度下实现了19.2 mm³的稳定样品体积，最高压力达933 MPa，最高温度达400 K；成功安全处理25 Ci氚库存，并保持清晰的测量光学路径。

Conclusion: 该DAC装置在样品体积、压力和温度等关键性能指标上均显著超过此前静态d-t靶的报道极限，为推进μCF高精度聚变测量提供了可行的实验平台。

Abstract: A new large-volume diamond anvil cell (DAC) has been developed for the Muon-catalyzed Fusion ($μ$CF) Experiment (MuFusE), enabling the compression and heating of deuterium-tritium (d-t) mixtures to pressures and temperatures needed to advance $μ$CF research. The MuFusE DAC achieves the large sample volumes necessary for high-precision fusion measurements while integrating cryogenic loading, all-metal sealing, and flexible bellows to maintain a secure environment during cell compression. Combined with remote pneumatic actuation and secondary containment, the DAC safely managed a 25 Ci tritium inventory while providing a clear optical path for in situ measurements of sample pressure and composition via laser spectroscopy. Utilizing 5 mm diameter diamond anvils oriented in the path of a high-intensity muon beam, the apparatus achieved a stable sample volume of 19.2 mm$^3$ at liquid density, pressures up to 933 MPa and temperatures up to 400 K - benchmarks that significantly exceed previously reported limits for static d-t targets.

### [53] [Dirac operators for infinite-dimensional color Lie algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05802)
*Steffen Schmidt,Konstantin Wernli*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文构建了无限维Z-分次颜色李代数的（相对）三次狄拉克算子（cubic Dirac operator），建立了Parthasarathy型平方公式，并将Chern-Weil同态推广至完备g-微分代数；应用方面，在可对称化Kac-Moody超代数中验证了Kac-Peterson类平凡性，对osp(1|2n)仿射超代数计算了Dirac核的核，并导出了用于酉性判别的Dirac不等式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将有限维李代数中经典的三次狄拉克算子理论推广到无限维Z-分次颜色李代数（color Lie algebras）框架下，并建立相应的不变性修正与平方公式，为后续超代数表示论中的酉性判别提供工具。

Method: 基于Z-分次确定的量子Weyl代数（quantum Weil algebra）的完备化空间定义算子；利用Kac-Peterson类（Kac-Peterson class）的color类比来衡量正规排序Casimir算子与三次狄拉克算子的非不变性；通过Chern-Weil同态（Chern-Weil homomorphism）的推广建立经典-量子对应。

Result: 建立了修正后的（相对）三次狄拉克算子的Parthasarathy型平方公式；在可对称化Kac-Moody超代数（symmetrizable Kac-Moody superalgebras）中Kac-Peterson类平凡且原始元为Weyl向量；对osp(1|2n)仿射超代数在可积最高权超模上计算了Dirac核的核；得到了ω-可酉化最高权超模的Dirac不等式；在sl(m|n)仿射超代数情形下将Dirac核与李超代数上同调等同。

Conclusion: 所构建的广义三次狄拉克算子框架成功覆盖了Kac-Moody超代数等重要情形，平方公式与Dirac不等式为酉性判别提供了有效判据，Chern-Weil同态的推广深化了狄拉克算子与Chern-Simons经典元素之间的内在联系。

Abstract: We construct cubic Dirac operators and relative cubic Dirac operators for infinite-dimensional quadratic $\mathbb{Z}$-graded color Lie algebras with finite-dimensional components. These operators are defined in completions of the quantum Weil algebra determined by the $\mathbb{Z}$-grading. The same grading fixes the normal-ordering convention. The failure of the normally ordered Casimir to be central, and of the normally ordered cubic Dirac operator to be $\mathfrak{g}$-invariant, is measured by a color analogue of the Kac-Peterson class. If this class is trivial, the Casimir admits a central correction and the cubic Dirac operator admits a corrected $\mathfrak{g}$-invariant form. For the corrected (relative) cubic Dirac operators, we establish Parthasarathy-type square formulas. We also extend the Chern-Weil homomorphism to completed $\mathfrak{g}$-differential algebras and identify the classical element whose quantization is the cubic Dirac operator with the Chern-Simons element associated with the quadratic invariant polynomial defined by $B$.
  As applications, we consider symmetrizable Kac-Moody superalgebras. In this setting the Kac-Peterson class is trivial, with primitive given by the Weyl vector. For the affine Kac-Moody superalgebra associated to $\mathfrak{osp}(1\vert 2n)$, we compute $\mathrm{ker}\operatorname{D}_{\mathfrak{g},\mathfrak{g}_{\bar{0}}}^{2}$ on integrable highest weight supermodules. We then apply the relative square formula to $ω$-unitarizable highest weight supermodules and obtain a Dirac inequality giving necessary conditions for unitarity. Finally, under assumptions satisfied by Kac-Moody superalgebras such as $\widehat{\mathfrak{sl}}(m\vert n)$, we identify the Dirac kernel with Lie superalgebra cohomology.

### [54] [Aqueous-alcohol mixtures in dimension two: miscibility and micro-segregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05862)
*Camille de la Vaissiere,Ayse Butuner,Aurélien Perera*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究利用二维（2D）位点相互作用模型，通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟混合水和三种醇（甲醇、戊醇、辛醇），发现二维模型下醇始终完全互溶，但随醇尾链增长出现显著微观偏析（micro-segregation），且该现象源于电荷排序机制（charge ordering mechanism）而非二维涨落增强；水分子的强自聚集驱动微观偏析，但水-醇界面接触阻止了完全相分离（phase separation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在澄清真实微观非均匀体系（micro-heterogeneous systems）模拟中的相关问题，特别是水和醇类混合物从丁醇（butanol）开始出现宏观相分离，而二维模型却始终完全互溶这一差异背后的机制。

Method: 采用二维位点相互作用模型（2D site interaction models）对水和醇类进行不同比例混合，通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟进行研究；利用对关联函数（pair correlation functions）、结构因子（structure factors）和 Kirkwood-Buff 积分（Kirkwood-Buff integrals）监测微观非均匀性的发展。

Result: 二维醇类始终与水完全互溶（fully miscible），但随着醇尾链（alcohol tail length）增加，体系出现越来越显著的微观偏析；微观偏析由水分子的强自聚集（self-aggregation）驱动，但水域边缘（outer rim of water domains）的水-醇接触阻止了完全相分离；Kirkwood-Buff 积分缺乏局部自平均（local self-averaging），体现了能量驱动局部结构维持与熵驱动全局均匀性之间的张力。

Conclusion: 微观偏析并非二维体系固有涨落增强的简单结果，而是电荷排序机制下涨落重组（reorganization of fluctuations）的产物；二维模型化能够更好地捕捉和揭示真实含氢键（hydrogen bonding）混合液体的物理机制。

Abstract: Two dimensional site interaction models of water and alcohols are mixed in various proportions and studied by Monte Carlo simulations, with the purpose to clarify problems related to simulation of real micro-heterogeneous systems. Three alcohols are considered, methanol, pentanol and octanol. The main finding is that, while real alcohols demix with water from butanol onward, their 2D analogs are always fully miscible, while developing increasingly pronounced micro-segregation as the alcohol tail length increases. This is not a consequence of the intrinsically higher fluctuations in 2D, but rather a reorganization of these fluctuations under the charge ordering mechanism. The second finding is that water drives the micro-segregation through strong self-aggregation, but this is not enough to achieve full phase separation because of the water-alcohol contact at the outer rim of the water domains. In this work we examine how this local heterogeneity develops with increasing alcohol alkyl tails, monitored with the study of pair correlation functions, structure factors and Kirkwood-Buff integrals. The absence of clear local self-averaging of the latter provides an illustration of the tension between energy driven maintaining of local structures and entropy driven global homogeneity. In that, the 2D modelisation of real hydrogen bonding mixtures allows to better capture and reveal the physics behind the chemistry of these liquids.

</details>


### [55] [Run and tumble dynamics of a soft robotic cell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05923)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 短时间呈现弹道运动（ballistic motion），长时间过渡为扩散（diffusion）；膜软度作为单一控制参数可连续调节持续运动、间歇性和长时间输运。

Conclusion: 识别了该行为的最小物理要素，建立了可编程软活性输运的设计原则，为活性物质物理与合成机器人学的交叉领域开辟新方向。

Abstract: The continuous regulation of transport properties through softness remains a longstanding challenge in active matter. Here, we show that encasing a programmable active particle within a deformable membrane naturally gives rise to intermittent stop-and-go dynamics, with ballistic motion at short times crossing over to diffusion at long times. Crucially, membrane softness acts as a single control parameter that continuously tunes persistence, intermittency, and long-time transport, linking the internal driving to the emergent locomotion of the synthetic cell. Combining experiments, simulations, and a run-and-tumble theoretical framework, we identify the minimal physical ingredients underlying this behavior and establish design principles for programmable soft active transport, opening new avenues at the interface of active matter physics and synthetic robotics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用由刚性玻璃和柔性基底构成的混合液晶盒（hybrid liquid crystal cells），通过机械形变诱导铁电向列相中的长程有序极化排列，并利用几何驱动排列（geometry-driven alignment）机制实现极化方向控制。

Result: 机械形变可抑制极化畴（polarization domains），在毫米级区域内产生长程有序排列；所选的极化方向表现出明显的材料依赖性。基于此开发的能量采集器可将机械形变转换为约1 V的输出电压。

Abstract: Ferroelectric nematic liquid crystals (FNLCs) combine fluidity with spontaneous polarization, offering promising avenues for flexible electromechanical systems. Here, we demonstrate that mechano-electrical conversion in FNLCs can be enhanced by mechanically programming a robust macroscopic polarization alignment. Using hybrid liquid crystal cells composed of rigid glass and flexible substrates, we show that deformation in the ferroelectric nematic phase suppresses polarization domains and produces long-range ordered polarization alignment over millimeter-scale areas. This geometry-driven alignment originates from coupling between the FNLC's spontaneous splay deformation and the deformation-imposed cell geometry, and we further find that the selected polarization direction exhibits clear material dependence. Leveraging this deformation-enabled alignment, we develop an FNLC-based energy harvester that converts mechanical deformation into an output of approximately 1 V. These findings establish geometry-driven alignment as a practical design strategy for boosting FNLC mechano-electrical conversion while providing polarization control for soft electronic devices.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本文提出的悬挂链强化模型能够有效描述软-硬固体界面的静摩擦力随老化时间的变化，为理解相关界面摩擦行为提供了理论框架。

### [58] [Investigating frictional instability due to pressurization in granular media: insights from coupled computational fluid dynamics discrete element method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06257)
*Bimal Chhushyabaga,Behrooz Ferdowsi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过3D耦合CFD-DEM模拟，揭示了孔隙压力诱导颗粒剪切层失稳的微观机制，指出失稳由孔隙压力与有效应力、排水条件、膨胀/压缩、水力连通性及颗粒组构（granular fabric）的耦合演化共同控制，而非仅由孔隙压力单独决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体增压可激活断层、斜坡和注入扰动储层中亚临界应力颗粒层的活动，但压力扩散、排水和接触网络退化之间的颗粒尺度反馈机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用3D耦合CFD-DEM（计算流体动力学-离散元法）模拟，首先通过应变控制试验确定摩尔-库仑（Mohr-Coulomb）强度包络线；随后施加亚临界剪应力，在排水和不排水两种边界条件下增加基底孔隙压力，进行应力控制模拟。

Result: 不排水边界保留超孔隙压力，而排水边界维持垂直梯度并抑制超压；内部场显示交替的膨胀和压缩带，以及孔隙度衍生渗透率代理的重组。微观力学诊断表明，局部颗粒旋转、力链重组和配位数变化主要由剪应力水平控制，而非排水条件。后破坏弱化伴随方向性力链组织的丧失；摩擦-速度和摩擦-孔隙度轨迹显示从膨胀主导的强化向孔隙压力主导的弱化转变。粘性数（viscous number Iv, 10^-8 ≤ Iv ≤ 10^-5）可部分组织低Iv蠕变响应，但无法形成唯一的局部流变学。

Conclusion: 排水控制的水力-力学反馈和组构退化将孔隙压力驱动转化为失稳，这阐明了受控于排水条件的水力-力学反馈与颗粒组构退化如何将孔隙压力驱动转化为失稳过程。

Abstract: Fluid pressurization can reactivate subcritically stressed granular layers in faults, slopes, and injection-perturbed reservoirs, but grain-scale feedbacks among pressure diffusion, drainage, and contact-network degradation remain unresolved. Here, 3D coupled CFD-DEM simulations investigate pore-pressure-induced reactivation of confined, fluid-saturated granular shear layers under imposed shear stress. Strain-controlled tests define the Mohr-Coulomb strength envelope; stress-controlled simulations then impose subcritical shear stresses while basal pore pressure increases under drained and undrained conditions. Instability is governed not by pore pressure alone, but by its coupled evolution with effective stress, drainage, dilation or compaction, hydraulic connectivity, and granular fabric. Undrained boundaries retain excess pore pressure, whereas drained boundaries maintain vertical gradients and suppress excess pressure. Internal fields reveal alternating dilation and compaction bands and reorganization of a porosity-derived permeability proxy, showing that hydraulic pathways evolve during deformation. Micromechanical diagnostics identify localized particle rotation, force-chain reorganization, porosity redistribution, and coordination-number variations controlled mainly by imposed shear-stress level rather than drainage. Second-order fabric metrics show that post-failure weakening coincides with loss of directional force-chain organization, especially at lower shear. Friction-velocity and friction-porosity trajectories indicate a transition from dilatancy-dominated strengthening to pore-pressure-driven weakening. Viscous-number scaling partially organizes the low-Iv creeping response, 10^-8 <= Iv <= 10^-5, but not onto a unique local rheology. These results clarify how drainage-controlled hydromechanical feedbacks and fabric degradation convert pore-pressure forcing into instability.

</details>

### [59] [Hypergroup Symmetry in Relative Quantum Field Theories and Chiral Algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05279)
*Terry Gannon,Brandon C. Rayhaun*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文为二维相对量子场论（relative QFT）中的不可逆对称性（noninvertible symmetries）建立了一般性框架，扩展了绝对QFT的已知结果，强调体拓扑曲面、超群（hypergroups）和穹代数（dome algebras）等新特征，并揭示了与有理手征代数（rational chiral algebras）中有限对称性及二维CFT边界条件之间的深刻联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相对QFT（即生活于更高一维拓扑QFT边界上的量子场论）中的不可逆对称性缺乏系统研究。现有成果多针对绝对QFT，而相对设定下会出现体拓扑曲面、超群等全新结构，亟需建立统一的形式化框架。

Method: 通过引入体拓扑曲面（topological surfaces of the bulk）这一关键角色，并推广管代数（tube algebras）至穹代数（dome algebras）以及超群（hypergroups）等代数结构，构建了适用于二维相对QFT的一般框架，并将其与有理手征代数的有限对称性一一对应。

Result: 揭示了相对框架对绝对理论的多重含义：解释了如何将二维CFT左、右手征代数的对称性“粘合”成全理论的拓扑线缺陷（topological line defects）；导出了二维CFT边界条件与其手征代数对称性间的精确对应关系；证明了对角有理CFT中拓扑线缺陷在边界条件上可递作用，且恒等Cardy态（identity Cardy state）在所有边界条件中g函数最小。举例说明，若存在中心荷c=8的有理手征代数且其模张量范畴为Haagerup融合范畴的Drinfeld中心，则该代数必为秩为2的超群在SU(3)_1⊗(E_6)_1手征代数上作用的不动点。

Conclusion: 本文建立的相对QFT对称性框架统一处理了体拓扑结构与边界对称性，将对称性分类与手征代数的共形嵌入（conformal embeddings of finite index）精确对应，并为理解二维CFT边界条件及其对称结构提供了代数化的系统工具。

Abstract: A QFT is said to be relative if it lives at the boundary of a topological QFT in one higher dimension. We develop a general framework for working with noninvertible symmetries of relative theories in two spacetime dimensions, extending several well-known results for absolute QFTs. We emphasize various new features which arise in the relative setting, including the role of topological surfaces of the bulk, and the appearance of hypergroups and certain generalizations of tube algebras known as dome algebras. Our formalism is particularly well-suited for studying rational chiral algebras, where it predicts that finite symmetries are in explicit one-to-one correspondence with conformal embeddings of finite index.
  We describe several implications of our framework for absolute theories. First, we explain how to "glue" together symmetries of the left- and right-moving chiral algebras of a 2D CFT to produce topological line defects of the full theory. Second, we derive a precise correspondence between boundary conditions of a 2D CFT and symmetries of its chiral algebra. This correspondence has several structural corollaries: in diagonal rational CFTs, we demonstrate that the topological line defects of the theory act transitively on its boundary conditions, and further that the identity Cardy state has the smallest $g$-function amongst all boundary conditions, including those which only preserve Virasoro symmetry.
  We conclude by illustrating our results in a variety of examples. For instance, we show that, if there exists a rational chiral algebra with central charge $c=8$ whose modular tensor category is the Drinfeld center of the Haagerup fusion category, then it must arise as the fixed points of a rank-2 hypergroup acting on the $SU(3)_1\otimes (E_{6})_1$ chiral algebra.

</details>


### [60] [Kaleidoscopes, Waves and the Prepotential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05280)
*Rafael Álvarez-García,Fabian Ruehle*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文揭示了卡拉比-丘（Calabi-Yau）三维流形上的同构突变（isomorphic flops）对应的考克斯特群（Coxeter group）对称性，指出其作用于Kähler模空间时，使得四维𝒩=2 Type IIA紧化中的预势（prepotential）必须构成考克斯特不变函数。文章构建了CICYs（complete intersection Calabi-Yau manifolds）中所有此类对称性的数据库，论证了该不变函数满足亥姆霍兹方程（Helmholtz equation），并可将世界面瞬子（worldsheet instanton）贡献的轨道求和（orbit sums）重新分解为拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子（Laplace-Beltrami operator）的本征函数展开，后者在模空间内部快速收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解卡拉比-丘流形上同构突变所对应的拓扑转变及其在模空间上诱导的考克斯特对称性，并探索这些对称性如何约束四维𝒩=2 Type IIA紧化中的预势结构。

Method: 构建Kähler-favorable CICYs中所有由同构突变产生的考克斯特对称性数据库；分析考克斯特群在Kähler模空间上的作用，提取不变的双线性型并将其解释为度量；构造相应的拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子，并论证考克斯特不变函数满足亥姆霍兹方程。

Result: 发现考克斯特不变函数是拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子的亥姆霍兹方程的解，预势可分解为该算子的本征函数（eigenfunctions）展开；原始世界面瞬子贡献的轨道求和与重求和后的表达式在收敛速率上互补，后者在模空间内部区域仅需前几项即可实现尖锐局域化收敛。

Conclusion: 同构突变诱导的考克斯特对称性为预势提供了强有力的结构约束，通过拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子的本征函数分解，可以显著改善世界面瞬子贡献的收敛行为，从而在模空间内部实现更高效的解析计算。

Abstract: Isomorphic flops are topology-changing transitions connecting two diffeomorphic families of Calabi-Yau threefolds. They correspond to the generators of certain Coxeter groups acting on the moduli space. As a consequence of these symmetries, the prepotential of 4D $\mathcal{N} = 2$ Type IIA compactifications on such varieties must assemble into Coxeter-invariant functions. We construct a database of all Coxeter symmetries from isomorphic flops in Kähler-favorable CICYs. The action of the Coxeter group on the Kähler moduli space leaves a symmetric bilinear form invariant, which we interpret as a metric and construct its associated Laplace-Beltrami operator. We argue that the Coxeter-invariant functions featured in the prepotential solve the Helmholtz equation with this Laplacian, and that the prepotential can then be resummed into a decomposition in terms of eigenfunctions of the Laplace-Beltrami operator. The convergence rate of the raw orbit sums of worldsheet instanton contributions and the resummed expressions are complementary, with the latter sharply localizing around the first few terms in the interior of the moduli space.

</details>


### [61] [The Double Well Done Doubly-Well](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05282)
*Aurélien Dersy,Matthew D. Schwartz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从精确WKB（exact WKB）和欧几里得路径积分（Euclidean path integral）两种互补方法，系统地构建了对称双势阱（symmetric double-well potential）能谱的完整跨级数（trans-series），展示了重聚（resurgence）如何将微扰与非微扰物理统一在一个严格约束的框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称双势阱是微扰与非微扰物理深度纠缠的最简单量子力学系统之一，其能级具有非解析展开和阶乘增长的系数，而宇称劈裂（parity splitting）指数级小且对微扰论不可见。重聚（resurgence）将这两个特征联系起来，但需要一个自洽的跨级数（trans-series）形式体系来统一描述。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：在精确WKB（exact WKB）中，利用Delabaere--Dillinger--Pham（DDP）关系编码的Stokes现象（Stokes phenomena）控制波函数经过转折点的解析延拓，通过Voros符号（Voros symbols）表达的量子化条件确定完整跨级数；在路径积分中，经典鞍点是欧几里得时间的双周期椭圆函数（doubly-periodic elliptic functions），Lefschetz thimble分解（Lefschetz thimble decomposition）决定哪些鞍点有贡献，配分函数跨级数在每个瞬子阶数下T依赖性是准零模thimble积分确定的简单多项式。

Result: 两种方法使用共同的数学基础设施，以互补方式部署：DDP关系是局域的，无需知道能量曲面的全局拓扑（该曲面是椭圆曲线）；路径积分中椭圆曲线以不同方式进入，Stokes现象在准零模（quasi-zero modes）的有限维流形上演化而非波函数的解析延拓。两种方法均通过四瞬子（four-instanton）能级和三圈（three-loop）阶进行了明确计算。

Conclusion: 对称双势阱是探索重聚（resurgence）的理想场所，两种方法共同表明微扰与非微扰部分可以通过跨级数严格约束在一起，且路径积分导出的配分函数跨级数比能量跨级数简单得多。

Abstract: The symmetric double-well potential is one of the simplest quantum-mechanical systems in which perturbative and non-perturbative physics are deeply entangled. Its energy levels have non-analytic expansions in inverse powers of the inter-well separation, with factorially growing coefficients, while the parity splitting is exponentially small and invisible to perturbation theory. Resurgence ties the two features together, organizing the exact spectrum into a single tightly-constrained trans-series. This paper gives a self-contained account of this trans-series from two complementary approaches: exact WKB and the Euclidean path integral, developed in a common notation with explicit calculations through the four-instanton level and three-loop order. In exact WKB, Stokes phenomena encoded in the Delabaere--Dillinger--Pham relations control the analytic continuation of the wavefunction past turning points. The quantization condition expressed in terms of Voros symbols then determines the full trans-series. The DDP relations are local and do not require knowing the global topology of the energy surface, but that surface is an elliptic curve. In the path integral, elliptic curves enter differently: the classical saddle points are doubly-periodic elliptic functions of Euclidean time, and Stokes phenomena play out within the finite-dimensional manifold of quasi-zero modes rather than through analytic continuation of the wavefunction. A Lefschetz thimble decomposition determines which saddles contribute, and the resulting partition function trans-series is much simpler than the energy trans-series: at each instanton order the $T$-dependence is a polynomial fixed by the quasi-zero-mode thimble integrals. Together, the two approaches deploy a shared mathematical infrastructure in complementary ways, showing that the double well is an ideal setting to explore resurgence.

</details>


### [62] [String dualities and wedge singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05287)
*Ivano Basile,Dieter Lust*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究具有楔形奇点（wedge singularity）背景中的弦传播，聚焦于两个圆的楔和（wedge sum）。基于该构造被认为是M理论描述0型弦的量子几何（quantum geometry）的提议，作者结合世界面（worldsheet）效应与涌现提议（emergence proposal），验证IIA弦能否自洽地再现弱耦合0A弦框架的预期。结果表明，在特定标度极限下，所得势能正确再现了 tachyons 的树级质量。此外，利用拓扑模形式（topological modular forms）讨论了世界面方法可能存在的运动学障碍及未解问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最近有提议指出，两圆楔和结构可提供一种M理论描述0型弦的量子几何，并衍生出更广泛的非超对称对偶网络（non-supersymmetric duality web）。本文旨在检验IIA弦的世界面特征能否与强耦合要素结合，自洽地复现弱耦合0A弦框架的理论预期。

Method: 将楔形奇点引入的世界面效应与应用于探测该奇点的D0膜（D0-brane）的涌现提议相结合，构建势能分析。同时采用拓扑模形式框架讨论世界面方法可能面临的运动学限制。

Result: 在特定标度极限（scaling limit）下，所得势能成功再现了tachyon正确的树级质量（tree-level mass）。

Conclusion: IIA弦的世界面处理与涌现提议的结合，可以在特定极限下与弱耦合0A弦的预期一致；但仍存在一些与拓扑模形式相关的运动学障碍及开放性问题，有待进一步研究。

Abstract: We study strings propagating in backgrounds with a wedge singularity, namely whose internal sector describes a wedge sum of closed manifolds. We focus on the wedge sum of two circles, which was recently argued to provide a quantum geometry for an M-theoretic description of type 0 strings, along with a much wider non-supersymmetric duality web stemming from quotients thereof. In the context of this proposal, we investigate whether the worldsheet features of type IIA strings, together with strong-coupling ingredients, can consistently reproduce the expectation of a weakly coupled type 0A frame. To this end, we combine worldsheet effects due to the wedge singularity with the emergence proposal applied to D0-branes probing it. We find that the resulting potential reproduces the correct tree-level mass of the tachyon in a specific scaling limit. We also discuss the possibility of kinematic obstructions to our worldsheet approach using the framework of topological modular forms, and comment on some puzzles and open questions.

</details>


### [63] [Unitarity, Recursion and Soft Limits in (EA)dS through Dressing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05289)
*Arhum Ansari,Deep Mazumdar,Brijesh Thakkar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用（E）AdS宇宙学关联函数（cosmological correlator）可表示为被辅助传播子（auxiliary propagator）“穿衣”的平时空振幅这一新框架，展示了宇宙学可观测量（cosmological observable）的若干结构性质直接源于平时空。具体推导了自旋关联函数的宇宙学切割规则（cutting rule）、宇宙学树定理（tree theorem），并通过“穿衣”技术将BCFW递推关系（BCFW recursion relation）提升至（E）AdS。还发现平时空软定理（soft theorem）重现了（E）AdS关联函数的软极限，且在次领头阶软极限中存在涌现的普适结构。这些结果表明宇宙学关联函数的关键特征可以系统性地理解为平时空物理的“穿衣”表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学关联函数是连接早期宇宙理论模型与观测数据的关键工具，但其在（E）AdS空间中的计算与结构分析十分复杂。本文的动机在于探究这些宇宙学可观测量是否能够从更简单的平时空物理中导出一个统一的理解框架。

Method: 基于“宇宙学关联函数可表示为被辅助传播子‘穿衣’的平时空振幅”这一新框架，方法上系统性地将平时空中的已知定理（光学定理、Feynman树定理、BCFW递推、软定理）通过“穿衣”过程提升至（E）AdS，从而推导出对应的宇宙学版本。

Result: 成功推导了自旋关联函数的宇宙学切割规则（源自平时空光学定理）、宇宙学树定理（源自Feynman树定理），并将BCFW递推关系推广至（E）AdS。还验证了平时空软定理可重现（E）AdS关联函数的软极限，并在次领头阶软极限中发现了涌现的普适结构。

Conclusion: 宇宙学关联函数的关键结构特征可以被系统性地理解为平时空物理的“穿衣”表现，这为统一理解宇宙学可观测量提供了坚实的理论基础，并暗示了更广泛的深层联系。

Abstract: Using the recently developed framework in which cosmological correlators in (E)AdS are represented as flat-space amplitudes dressed by auxiliary propagators, we show that several structural properties of the cosmological observables have a direct flat-space origin. We derive cosmological cutting rules for spinning correlators from the flat-space optical theorem, obtain the cosmological tree theorem from the Feynman tree theorem, and uplift BCFW recursion relations to (E)AdS via dressing. We also show that flat-space soft theorems reproduce the soft limits of (E)AdS correlators, and find indications of an emergent universal structure in subleading soft limits. These results provide evidence that key features of cosmological correlators can be systematically understood as dressed manifestations of flat-space physics.

### [64] [Krylov Complexity: Flat bands and Carroll breaking deformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05303)
*Aritra Banerjee,Arpan Bhattacharyya,Rudranil Basu,Sayan Das*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用Krylov复杂性（Krylov complexity）探究Carroll破缺微扰淬火下平带系统的态动力学，发现Krylov复杂性增长能够锐利分辨不同Carroll扇区对退局域化微扰的相位依赖性韧性，并在连续Carroll标量场理论中补充了梯度形变下的Krylov增长机制，该机制展现出显著的紫外/红外（UV/IR）混合特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平带系统在紧致局域态（Compact Localised States, CLS）表述下具备超平移对称性（supertranslation symmetry），从而内禀地具有Carroll对称性（Carrollian symmetry）。现有研究尚未充分揭示此类Carroll扇区在退局域化微扰下的动力学响应，尤其缺乏量化其相位依赖性韧性的诊断工具。

Method: 以所有能带平坦（All Bands Flat, ABF）的费米子梯子哈密顿量（Fermionic ladder Hamiltonian）为具体模型，引入超平移保持的相互作用，利用Krylov态复杂性（Krylov state complexity）作为探针，分析跨越临界线的淬火（quench）过程；同时构建连续Carroll标量场理论（Carroll scalar field theory）中的梯度形变（gradient deformation）模型，作为补充机制。

Result: Krylov复杂性的增长行为能够锐利地分辨不同Carroll扇区在面对退局域化微扰时的相位依赖性韧性；连续Carroll标量场中的Krylov增长表现出强烈的紫外敏感性（ultraviolet sensitivity），即紫外/红外混合（UV/IR mixing）。

Conclusion: Krylov复杂性是量化平带系统中Carroll扇区稳定性的有效工具，其增长模式直接反映了Carroll对称性破缺微扰下系统的局域化-退局域化转变；UV/IR混合现象表明该诊断方法在连续场论情形下同样具有敏感性及适用性。

Abstract: Systems with flat band structures, when written in the language of Compact Localised States (CLS), have been shown to be explicitly invariant under supertranslation symmetries, making Carrollian symmetries inherently important for such systems. In this work, we explore the state dynamics of these systems, focusing on quenches induced by Carroll breaking perturbations, through the probe of Krylov (spread) Complexity. We specialise to Fermionic ladder Hamiltonians with all bands flat (ABF) scenario, augmented by a supertranslation preserving interaction, and discuss Krylov state complexity for quenches across critical lines. We further discuss how the growth of Krylov complexity sharply resolves the phase-dependent resilience of Carrollian sectors against delocalising perturbations. This is augmented by a complementary mechanism for Krylov growth in a continuum Carroll scalar field theory with a gradient deformation, which exhibits strong ultraviolet sensitivity (UV/IR mixing).

</details>


### [65] [Mass-Flow Invariance of $Q$-Cohomology in BMN Matrix Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05314)
*Chi-Ming Chang,Zhengyuan Du,Sarthak Duary,Kangning Liu,Yi-Xiao Tao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了BMN矩阵量子力学中动力学超荷对质量参数μ的依赖关系，通过构造相似变换证明了超荷的流在Q-上同调意义上的非重整化性，并在N=2理论中进行了具体验证，同时分析了BPS字母上的诱导作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索BMN矩阵量子力学（BMN matrix quantum mechanics）中动力学超荷（dynamical supercharge）随质量参数μ的依赖行为，验证其Q-上同调（Q-cohomology）是否满足非重整化（non-renormalization）性质。

Method: 在固定正则矩阵变量下对μ求导，证明十六分量超荷通过厄米二次玻色算符K和旋量空间因子iγ^{123}的伴随作用演化；投影到γ^{123}本征空间后，该流积分有限相似变换；对幂零分量Q(μ)得到代数质量流非重整化表述；提出比较M的二次增长与BMN振子波函数高斯衰减的小步判据，并在N=2理论中具体验证。

Result: 推导出Q(μ)与Q(μ₀)之间的有限相似变换关系，建立了质量流非重整化陈述；在N=2理论中，两个真空扇区（平庸真空和不可约模糊球真空）上验证了小步判据的适用性；计算了Q_BPS在对应BPS字母上的诱导作用：平庸扇区与N=4 SYM标准BMN扇区BPS字母微分一致，而不可约扇区为零。

Conclusion: BMN矩阵量子力学的动力学超荷在Q-上同调意义上具有代数非重整化性质，其Hilbert空间版本需要解析性控制，与Witten关于超对称量子力学的论证平行。

Abstract: We study the dependence of the dynamical supercharges of BMN matrix quantum mechanics on the mass parameter $μ$. Taking the $μ$-derivative at fixed canonical matrix variables, we show that the sixteen-component supercharge evolves by the adjoint action of a Hermitian quadratic bosonic operator $\mathcal{K}$, together with the spinor-space factor $iγ^{123}$. After projection to a $γ^{123}$-eigenspace, this flow integrates to a finite similarity transformation. For the nilpotent component $Q(μ)=\mathcal Q^4_-(μ)$, one obtains $Q(μ)=M(μ,μ_0)Q(μ_0)M(μ,μ_0)^{-1}$, giving an algebraic mass-flow non-renormalization statement for the $Q$-cohomology. The corresponding Hilbert-space statement has an analytic qualification, parallel to Witten's argument for supersymmetric quantum mechanics: $M$ is non-unitary and unbounded, so its action on the normalizable domain must be controlled. We formulate a small-step criterion by comparing the quadratic growth of $M$ with the Gaussian falloff of BMN oscillator wavefunctions within each component $μ>0$ or $μ<0$. As a concrete check, we evaluate this condition in the $N=2$ theory, whose two vacuum sectors are built on the trivial vacuum and the irreducible fuzzy-sphere vacuum. We also compute the induced $Q_{\rm BPS}$-action on the corresponding BPS letters: in the trivial sector it agrees with the standard BMN-sector BPS-letter differential of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM, while in the irreducible sector it vanishes.

</details>

Abstract: We use numerical relativity to study the non-linear instability of five-dimensional black strings in Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. Black strings evolve into a series of black holes joined by thinner string-like segments, but key features of the dynamics depend on the sign of the Gauss-Bonnet coupling. For positive coupling, favored by UV considerations, the growth of curvature invariants is limited within the validity of effective field theory (EFT), suggesting a mechanism for restoring weak cosmic censorship. For negative coupling this cap is absent and curvatures may grow until the EFT breaks down.

We develop the Poincare-Carrollian intertwiner as the central method. Method: 研究分析了阿贝尔-希格斯涡旋解的结构，表征了其宽度、曲率轮廓及其趋近理想弦极限的行为；通过研究光子在场弦时空中的传播，比较了有限核心涡旋与理想无限细弦的光学差异。

Abstract: We study the optical properties of gravitating Abelian-Higgs cosmic strings and compare them with those of the idealized infinitely thin string. We analyze the structure of the corresponding vortex solutions, characterizing their width, curvature profile, and approach to the ideal string limit. By investigating photon propagation in the string spacetime, we show that the finite core of the vortex gives rise to distinctive observational signatures absent in the ideal string approximation, including a characteristic triple-imaging configuration, strong demagnification of the central image, and a nontrivial Shapiro time delay between external and internal images. ### [71] [The spectrum of the bosonic ambitwistor string revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05500)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用动量空间（momentum space）方法进行代数化处理，将BRST上同调解释为庞加莱群（Poincaré group）的诱导表示。通过将BMS₃李代数（BMS₃ Lie algebra）的半无穷上同调（semi-infinite cohomology）与中心荷相对商化，分析谱在洛伦兹群（Lorentz group）的稳定子群H上的模结构。

Result: 所有上同调均位于无质量扇区；除闭弦标准无质量态（膨胀子、度规和Kalb-Ramond场）外，还发现一个额外的无质量矢量。谱的非幺正性表明该矢量不能解释为麦克斯韦场。

Conclusion: 该谱是非幺正的，因此额外的无质量矢量不具备作为麦克斯韦场的物理解释，这意味着玻色型环绕扭转弦的谱结构与标准场论幺正性要求相冲突。

Abstract: We revisit the calculation of the spectrum of the bosonic ambitwistor string, understood as the BRST cohomology or, equivalently, as the semi-infinite cohomology of the $\mathrm{BMS}_3$ Lie algebra relative to the centre with values in a particular module. We work in momentum space, which allows us to work algebraically and interpret the BRST cohomology as inducing representations of the Poincaré group. In agreement with the existing literature, we find that all the cohomology resides in the massless sector, but a careful representation-theoretic analysis of the spectrum reveals, in addition to the usual massless sector of the closed bosonic string (dilaton, metric and Kalb--Ramond field), also a massless vector. We devote a large part of the paper to describing the cohomology at a massless momentum $p$ as a module over the stabiliser $H$ of $p$ in the Lorentz group, a task which is made difficult due to $H$ not acting reducibly when $p\neq 0$. This allows us to conclude that the spectrum is not unitary, forbidding the interpretation of the extra massless vector as a Maxwell field.

Method: 通过构造具体初始数据集合，分析狄利克雷边界条件下引力演化的动力学行为。在任意维度下考察宇宙学例子，在2+1维中特别分析BTZ黑洞外的狄利克雷墙演化，并在更高维中构造俘获面触及边界墙的情形。

Abstract: We study evolution in Einstein-Hilbert gravity with Dirichlet boundary conditions imposed on a finite surface. We argue that there are open sets of initial data where such evolutions terminate at finite times due to singularities that reach the boundary. In any dimension, the simplest such examples occur in cosmologies. However, in 2+1 dimensions we also show that Dirichlet walls initially outside a BTZ black hole can fall through the horizon, and that this also leads to generic singularities. Method: 从U(1) gerbe的局部Čech数据出发，构造对应的李2-广群（Lie 2-algebroid）和精确库朗广群（exact Courant algebroid），利用该几何框架建立BV-BRST复形，将场-鬼塔直接编码于局部gerbe数据中，并通过联络结构（connective structure）、弯曲（curving）与3-形式曲率之间的关系导出高阶Russian公式。

Result: 得到的Čech-德拉姆双复形为U(1) 1-形式对称性的反常下降（anomaly descent）提供了自然框架，并在麦克斯韦理论（Maxwell theory）中给出了显式构造实例。

Conclusion: 李2-广群与库朗广群构成的几何框架能够统一描述更高形式规范理论的BV-BRST结构与反常下降机制。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum aspects of gauging continuous 1-form global symmetries. In this paper, we study the BV-BRST quantization of a $U(1)$ 2-form gauge field, described geometrically by a $U(1)$ gerbe. Starting from the local Čech data of the gerbe, we construct the corresponding infinitesimal symmetry structure in terms of a Lie 2-algebroid, and show that, together with the associated exact Courant algebroid, it provides a natural geometric framework for the BV-BRST complex of this higher-form gauge theory. In this formulation, the field-ghost tower is encoded directly in the local gerbe data, and the higher Russian formula arises naturally from the relations among the connective structure, the curving, and the 3-form curvature. We further show that the resulting Čech-de Rham bicomplex provides a natural setting for anomaly descent for $U(1)$ 1-form symmetries, and illustrate the construction with explicit examples in Maxwell theory.

</details>


### [74] [Hodge theory and $G_4$ fluxes in weighted projective spaces: Galois action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05530)
*Hugo Fortin,Daniel López Garcia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将G₄-通量与一般Hodge圈的研究从普通Fermat六次四维簇推广到加权投影空间中的Fermat型超曲面，发现加权情形下Galois作用不保持(2,2)-子空间，导致对称通量需额外考虑中上同调分量；在最大对称Fermat点上通过显式周期构造得到，多数加权例子中对称一般Hodge圈超出膜tadpole上界，而h^1,1=11的36次例子在最大对称位形上验证了tadpole猜想，揭示非均匀Galois轨道是导致大tadpole电荷的算术机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将G₄-通量(flux)与一般Hodge圈(general Hodge cycle)的研究从普通Fermat六次四维簇推广到加权投影空间中的Fermat型超曲面(tame Fermat-type hypersurfaces in weighted projective space)，探究加权设定中Galois作用对周期结构的影响，并检验对称一般Hodge圈能否满足M2-brane tadpole上界(tadpole bound)。

Method: 在最大对称Fermat点(maximally symmetric Fermat points)上显式计算周期矩阵(period matrices)与对称不变Hodge轨迹；利用Movasati的周期描述、分圆周期矩阵(cyclotomic period matrices)以及Hermite/Smith标准型约化，构造中上同调(middle cohomology)中对称自对偶类(self-dual class)的整格点阵。

Result: 在加权投影空间ℙ₁,₁,₁,₁,₄,₄中的12次例子与用作对比的8次加权例子中，最短的对称一般Hodge圈均超过tadpole上界；在ℙ₁,₁,₁,₉,₁₂,₁₂中的36次例子（h^1,1=11）中，tadpole猜想在最大对称位形上得到验证。

Conclusion: 在加权Fermat例子中，“对称通量(symmetric flux)”的相关概念必须同时考虑簇的自同构(automorphisms)和周期域上的Galois作用；非均匀Galois轨道(non-uniform Galois orbits)为对称Hodge类获取大tadpole电荷(tadpole charge)提供了天然的算术机制。

Abstract: We extend the explicit study of $G_4$-fluxes and general Hodge cycles from the ordinary Fermat sextic fourfold to tame Fermat-type hypersurfaces in weighted projective space. The main new feature in the weighted setting is that the Galois action on the cyclotomic period data need not preserve the $(2,2)$-subspace. As a consequence, the rational reconstruction of an integral self-dual class can involve additional middle-cohomology components, increasing the norm of the corresponding flux.
  We work at maximally symmetric Fermat points, where the period matrices and symmetry-invariant Hodge loci can be computed explicitly. Using Movasati's description of periods, cyclotomic period matrices, and Hermite/Smith normal form reductions, we construct the relevant integral lattices of symmetric self-dual classes in middle cohomology. This gives a controlled test of whether symmetric general Hodge cycles can satisfy the M2-brane tadpole bound.
  Our main conclusion is empirical. In the degree 12 example in $\mathbb{P}_{1,1,1,1,4,4}$, and in the degree 8 weighted example used as a comparison, the shortest computed symmetric general Hodge cycles overshoot the tadpole bound. In the degree 36 example in $\mathbb{P}_{1,1,1,9,12,12}$, which has $h^{1,1}=11$, the most general example we have, the tadpole conjecture is indeed verified at the maximally symmetric locus, although the computations get difficult and computationally expensive.
  These computations suggest that, in weighted Fermat examples, the relevant notion of a ``symmetric flux'' must take into account not only automorphisms of the variety but also the Galois action on the period field. Non-uniform Galois orbits provide a natural arithmetic mechanism by which symmetric Hodge classes can acquire large tadpole charge.

### [75] [Notes on (-2)-form symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05543)
*Pinak Banerjee,Alonso Perez-Lona,Daniel Robbins,Subham Roy,Eric Sharpe,Xingyang Yu*

TL;DR: 该论文通过(d+1)维对称拓扑场论(SymTFT)中的非本征余维一缺陷，系统研究了d维量子场论的(-2)-形式对称性，展示了其与异常数据、非可逆对称性结合子数据的关联，并通过多种理论模型和全息实现进行了具体构造与验证。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先基于(d+1)维SymTFT中的非本真(non-genuine)余维一缺陷构造(-2)-形式对称性；随后在二维玩具模型、三维ABJM型理论、四维广义杨-米尔斯理论以及融合范畴示例中加以说明；并发展了三明治实现(club-sandwich realization，即季规范操作)与嵌套离散规范化的替代方案；最后通过全息实现(IIA型Romans质量充当(-2)-形式背景)给出自上而下的验证。

Result: (-2)-形式对称性能够改变SymTFT作用量，进而联系具有不同异常数据或非可逆对称性结合子数据(如Rep(D₄)与Rep(Q₈))的理论；三明治实现可以将季规范操作作为界面衔接不同重整化群流；全息实现中Romans质量的平移对应边界异常系数的平移。

Conclusion: (-2)-形式对称性为关联不同整体对称性结构的量子场论提供了新的理论框架，并且在耦合体-边界系统中也具有进一步推广的讨论空间。

Abstract: We study $(-2)$-form symmetries of a $d$-dimensional quantum field theory, via a $(-1)$-form symmetry of its $(d+1)$-dimensional Symmetry Topological Field Theory (SymTFT), realized by a non-genuine codimension-one defect in the SymTFT bulk attached to a spacetime-filling topological operator. Unlike a $(-1)$-form symmetry of a $d$-dimensional theory, which merely shifts a parameter of the absolute theory, a $(-2)$-form symmetry modifies the SymTFT action, and thereby relates theories whose ordinary global symmetries differ by anomaly data or by the associator data of a non-invertible symmetry. We illustrate the construction in two-dimensional toy models, three-dimensional ABJM-type theories, four-dimensional generalized Yang--Mills theory, and in a fusion-categorical example relating the non-invertible symmetries $\operatorname{Rep}(D_4)$ and $\operatorname{Rep}(Q_8)$. We then develop a club-sandwich realization, in which a quarter-gauging operation interfaces between IR phases of distinct RG flows of a common UV theory, and an alternative realization via nested discrete gauging. Finally, we present a holographic, top-down realization in which the type IIA Romans mass plays the role of a $(-2)$-form background for a three-dimensional Chern--Simons-matter theory, with shifts of the Romans mass realizing shifts of the boundary anomaly coefficients. We also discuss related constructions for coupled bulk--boundary systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>
