Method: 采用线性协变规范（linear covariant gauges）对SU(2) Yang-Mills-Chern-Simons理论进行量子化，引入希格斯场并消除无穷小Gribov副本（infinitesimal Gribov copies）。通过求解Gribov参数的间隙方程（gap equation），将其作为其他质量参数和规范耦合的函数来固定，从而在参数空间内施加约束条件。

Result: 识别出两种不同的相：约束相（confining phase），所有极点均为复数；退约束相（deconfined phase），可出现类似物理胶子（would-be physical gluon）的激发。Gribov参数的竞争性质量效应被揭示，其对于理论能谱的表征具有显著影响。

Conclusion: Gribov参数通过间隙方程自洽确定，而非视为自由参数，这使质量参数间的竞争关系透明化，并约束了参数空间。Gribov参数在区分约束与退约束相中起关键作用。

Abstract: We explore Yang-Mills-Chern-Simons theories coupled to a Higgs-like field in the fundamental representation of $SU(2)$ quantized in linear covariant gauges in three Euclidean dimensions. We analyze the modifications in the analytic structure of the gluon propagator due to the elimination of infinitesimal Gribov copies. The interplay between the Higgs, the Chern-Simons and Gribov mass parameters is investigated. Two different phases are identified: a confining one, where all poles are complex, and a deconfined one, where would-be physical gluon excitation can appear. Unlike previous works, the Gribov parameter is consistently fixed by its gap equation as a function of the other mass parameters and the gauge coupling. This imposes a constraint in the parameter space and makes transparent how the competition of the mass parameters affects the relevance of the Gribov parameter for the characterization of the spectrum of the theory.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在宽条带极限（大l）下，这些纠缠量的l依赖呈现幂律形式（power-law form），受系统红外标度（IR scaling）支配。在固定大l下，所有纠缠量在临界点附近展现出清晰特征。此外，通过不同方向的条带探测系统各向异性（anisotropy），发现各向异性的大l行为能够区分非平庸相与平庸相。

Conclusion: 多体全息纠缠（multipartite holographic entanglement）可作为灵敏且非局域的工具，用于探测拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）和各向异性红外物理（anisotropic IR physics）。

Abstract: We study multipartite entanglement structures in the zero-temperature holographic Weyl semimetal, focusing on tripartite and four-partite structures. For strip regions, we compute the conditional mutual information, the entanglement wedge cross section, tripartite measures $κ$ and the Markov gap, multi-EWCS, and two multi-EWCS based four-partite signals $Δ$ and $g$. These quantities are studied as functions of the strip width $l$ and the tuning parameter across the topological transition. At large $l$, their $l$ dependence takes a power-law form governed by the IR scaling of the system. At fixed large $l$, all these entanglement quantities develop clear features near the critical point, showing that tripartite and four-partite entanglement structures can diagnose the topological quantum phase transition. We further study strips pointing in different directions to probe the anisotropy of the system. The anisotropic large l behavior distinguishes the nontrivial phase from the trivial phase. These results establish multipartite holographic entanglement as a sensitive, nonlocal probe of topological phase transitions and anisotropic IR physics.

### [79] [Chiral symmetry breaking in models with unconventional supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06221)
*Pedro D. Alvarez,Cristian Villavicencio,Jorge Zanelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究基于超李代数 su(2,2|3) 的几何构造规范理论中的动力学质量生成。该理论将引力、杨-米尔斯场和费米子统一为单一规范联络的分量，不含基本标量场或人为的四费米子相互作用。费米子自相互作用不可避免地从几何结构中产生，通过非最小耦合和挠率（torsion）实现。在低能有效描述下，这些相互作用生成 Nambu-Jona-Lasinio 型势，触发手征对称性破缺并形成费米子质量隙。质量生成是底层规范-几何与代数结构的直接结果，而非独立的动力学假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 该几何构造自动产生费米子自相互作用，无需引入基本标量场或人为四费米子项；在低能有效描述下，这些相互作用形成 Nambu-Jona-Lasinio 型势，触发手征对称性破缺（chiral symmetry breaking）并产生费米子质量隙（mass gap）。

Conclusion: 动力学质量生成是该理论底层规范-几何与代数结构的直接必然结果，而非外加的动力学假设，表明该统一框架可能提供一种从几何原理出发理解费米子质量起源的新路径。

Abstract: We investigate dynamical mass generation in a geometrically constructed gauge theory based on the super Lie algebra $su(2,2|3)$, in which gravity, Yang-Mills fields, and fermions are unified as components of a single gauge connection. The model contains no elementary scalar fields and no ad hoc four-fermion interactions. Instead, fermionic self-interactions arise unavoidably from the geometric structure of the theory, through nonminimal couplings and torsion associated with the unified connection. Upon reduction to an effective low-energy description, these interactions generate a Nambu-Jona-Lasinio--type potential that triggers chiral symmetry breaking and the formation of a fermion mass gap. In this framework, mass generation emerges as a direct consequence of the underlying gauge-geometric and algebraic structure, rather than as an independent dynamical assumption.

### [81] [Spinning bulk-to-boundary correlators in the massless theories with Poincaré symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06326)
*Jiang Long,Yu-Xuan Wei,Xin-Hao Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过规定未来/过去类光无穷远附近的落条件，对庞加莱不变理论中一般整数自旋 s 算符的体-边界关联函数（bulk-to-boundary correlators）进行分类。基本张量结构由无质量粒子的小群 ISO(2) 确定，并被映射为所有可能的非交叉双线图（non-crossing double-line diagrams）；进一步映射到圆图（circular diagrams）后，所有独立张量结构表现为圈图（loop diagrams）的张量积。通过外推至边界-边界关联函数，发现外推算符属于卡罗尔共形场论（Carrollian conformal field theory, CCFT）中的 Ib 型自旋 s 多重态表示——一种由 Wigner 平移生成元生成的净表示（net representation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Poincaré 不变理论中一般整数自旋算符的体-边界关联函数的结构尚不清晰，需要一个系统性的分类框架。此外，体-边界关联函数与边界-边界关联函数之间的外推关系，以及这种外推在卡罗尔共形场论（CCFT）表示论中的归属，是理解体-边界对应（bulk-to-boundary correspondence）的关键问题。

Method: 在庞加莱不变理论中，通过在未来/过去类光无穷远（future/past null infinity）附近施加合适的落条件（fall-off conditions）来约束体-边界关联函数的行为。利用无质量粒子的小群 ISO(2) 确定基本张量结构；将这些张量结构映射为非交叉双线图，再进一步映射为圆图，从而将独立张量结构表达为圈图的张量积。最后，通过外推将体-边界关联函数转化为边界-边界关联函数，并识别其在卡罗尔共形场论（CCFT）中的表示类型。

Result: 体-边界关联函数可表示为基本张量结构的线性叠加，这些结构由无质量粒子的小群 ISO(2) 完全确定。所有独立张量结构可以映射为非交叉双线图，并进一步映射为圆图，最终表现为圈图的张量积。外推得到的边界-边界关联函数中的算符属于卡罗尔共形场论（CCFT）的 Ib 型自旋 s 多重态表示，该表示由 Wigner 平移生成元生成。

Conclusion: 针对一般整数自旋 s 算符的体-边界关联函数，本文建立了一套基于小群 ISO(2) 和图论映射的系统分类方法。该分类揭示了体-边界与边界-边界关联函数之间的外推结构，并明确了外推算符在卡罗尔共形场论（CCFT）中属于 Ib 型自旋 s 多重态表示。这为理解体-边界对应及其在共形场论表示论中的实现提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We classify the bulk-to-boundary correlators for general integer-spin $s$ operators in a Poincaré-invariant theory by imposing suitable fall-off conditions near future/past null infinity. Any bulk-to-boundary correlator is a linear superposition of a set of basic tensor structures fixed by the little group \text{ISO}(2) of massless particles. We map the independent tensor structures to all possible non-crossing double-line diagrams. A further mapping of the double-line diagrams to circular diagrams shows that all independent tensor structures are tensor products of loop diagrams. By extrapolating the bulk-to-boundary correlators to boundary-to-boundary correlators, we find a rich structure for general spin-$s$ operators. Furthermore, we show that the extrapolated operator lies in a type Ib spin-$s$ multiplet representation of Carrollian conformal field theory (CCFT). This is a net representation that generated by the Wigner translation generators.

</details>


### [82] [Quantum Geometry from Area Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06372)
*Jerzy Kowalski-Glikman,Ludovic Varrin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文构造了因果穹顶（causal-diamond）几何中黑体辐射的爱因斯坦涨落论证的量子统计类似物，通过拉伸视界上的面积密度涨落分析，推导出包含经典项和线性项的边界面积算子热涨落公式，并将线性项解释为几何离散量子的统计特征，为量子面积自由度提供自下而上的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受爱因斯坦利用黑体辐射能量涨落推测光量子存在的经典论证启发，作者试图在因果穹顶（causal-diamond）几何框架下，通过类似的统计涨落分析，为量子几何（quantum geometry）的离散性提供自下而上的证据。

Method: 从闵可夫斯基因果穹顶内拉伸视界（stretched horizon）的相空间出发，对拉伸视界时间上平均的场生成的泊松代数（Poisson algebra）进行量子化；然后计算在类比黑体热态（black-body thermal state）构造的热态中，横向二维球面平均面积密度的涨落。

Result: 在拉伸视界趋近因果穹顶边界的零极限（null limit）下，得到了包含两项的边界面积算子的热涨落公式：一项正比于期望值的平方（经典贡献），另一项呈Verlinde–Zurek标度特征（线性项，对应独立微观组元）。线性项被解读为几何离散量子（discrete quanta of geometry）的统计信号。

Conclusion: 该结果从量子统计涨落的角度支持了面积自由度的量子化本质，并佐证了零面量子几何（null quantum geometry）的embadon图像。

Abstract: We construct a quantum-statistical analogue of Einstein's fluctuation argument for black-body radiation in the context of causal-diamond geometry. Starting from the phase space of a stretched horizon inside a Minkowski causal diamond, we quantize the Poisson algebra generated by the fields averaged over stretched-horizon time. We then compute the fluctuations of the averaged area density of the transverse two-spheres in a thermal state constructed in analogue with the black-body thermal state. In the null limit, where the stretched horizon approaches the causal-diamond boundary, this yields a thermal fluctuation formula of the boundary area operator that contains two terms, in direct analogue with the black-body radiation. The term quadratic in the expectation value is the ``classical'' contribution, while the linear term has the Verlinde--Zurek scaling characteristic of independent microscopic constituents. In direct analogue with Einstein's interpretation of black-body energy fluctuations as evidence for light quanta, we interpret the linear area-fluctuation term as a statistical signature of discrete quanta of geometry. This provides bottom-up evidence for quantum area degrees of freedom and supports the embadon picture of null quantum geometry.

</details>


### [83] [Smooth horizons from topology change in canonical quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06404)
*Venkatesa Chandrasekaran*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过在关系时间演化（relational time evolution）下将拓扑变化引入正则量子化（canonical quantization），解决了JT引力中的防火墙悖论（firewall paradox）。引力哈密顿量通过“裤子对”相互作用作用于黑洞内部，在单内部扇区与连通双内部扇区之间映射。通过视界处的助推边缘模（boost edge modes）及其交叉积代数（crossed product algebra）的协变性，给出了防火墙的精确引力实现。经过Page时间（Page time）演化，连通双内部分支占据主导，其中一支在粘回外部后携带非平凡的单侧助推，构成防火墙；另一支则被引力约束（gravitational constraints）商掉后存活，其上地平线真空测量与早期辐射纯度测量成为同一个狄拉克可观测量（Dirac observable）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决JT引力（JT gravity）中的防火墙悖论，即如何在不违背幺正性（unitarity）的前提下描述黑洞内部在Page时间后的演化。

Method: 将拓扑变化（topology change）纳入正则量子化框架，采用关系时间演化方案。通过扩展相空间描述（extended phase space description）将体积希尔伯特空间（bulk Hilbert space）在事件视界处分裂，引入助推边缘模，构造交叉积代数，并利用引力约束进行商化。

Result: 指出每个拓扑变化跃迁虽指数压低，但Page时间后连通双内部分支占主导。该分支包含两种内部态：一种携带非平凡单侧助推，对应防火墙；另一种为零模，被引力约束存活。存活分支上，地平线真空测量与早期辐射纯度测量成为同一狄拉克可观测量。

Conclusion: 防火墙在引力框架下获得精确的代数实现：它对应于内部边缘模相对于外部且固定物质场的单侧助推，或等价于固定边缘模时内外霍金粒子（Hawking partners）之间的相对相位。Page时间动力学在连通分支上诱导出一个大微分同胚（large diffeomorphism），使内部霍金配偶子的算符代数与解码后的早期辐射算符代数相同。

Abstract: We propose a resolution of the firewall paradox in JT gravity by incorporating topology change into canonical quantization under relational time evolution. The gravitational Hamiltonian acts on the black hole interior through a pair of pants interaction, mapping between a single interior sector and a connected two interior sector. To describe dynamics in the interior while keeping track of the exterior, we pass to an extended phase space description obtained by splitting the bulk Hilbert space across the event horizon. The split introduces boost edge modes at the horizon, which the Hawking modes become gravitationally dressed to. Covariance of the resulting crossed product algebra provides a precise gravitational realization of the firewall: a one sided boost of the interior edge mode relative to the exterior holding the matter fixed, or equivalently, a relative phase between the interior and exterior Hawking partners holding the edge modes fixed. Although each topology changing transition is exponentially suppressed, evolution over a Page time causes the connected two interior branch to dominate. One of these is the naive semiclassical interior, which we show carries a nontrivial one sided boost upon gluing the interior back to the exterior, and hence a firewall. The other interior is shown to be a zero mode of the one sided boost generator. Gluing the interior back to the exterior quotients by the gravitational constraints, which annihilates the firewall branch. On the surviving branch, we show the horizon vacuum measurement and the early radiation purity measurement become the same Dirac observable. Equivalently, we show that Page time dynamics induces a large diffeomorphism on the connected branch under which the operator algebra of the interior Hawking partner and that of the decoded early radiation are identified.

</details>

### [84] [Quantum Circuit Complexity as a Measure of Particle Creation in Bouncing Cosmologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05235)
*Samak Boonpan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量方法，在非奇异性反弹宇宙学背景下，对量子标量场的电路复杂度（circuit complexity）演化进行了精确非微扰研究，发现复杂度在反弹时刻保持有限，反弹后的增长与宇宙学粒子产生（cosmological particle production）密切相关，其中“啁啾”（chirping）贡献充当了时空过渡的几何记忆，量化了粒子创造的信息成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有工作大多采用微扰方法处理反弹宇宙学背景下的量子场复杂度演化，缺乏精确的非微扰分析框架；此外，复杂度与粒子产生之间的定量关系尚未被充分揭示。

Method: 采用Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量（Lewis-Riesenfeld invariant）方法，构建了一个精确的非微扰（non-perturbative）框架，用于描述量子标量场在反弹宇宙学背景中的复杂度演化。

Result: 复杂度在反弹时刻保持有限，主要受时空收缩导致的量子态压缩（squeezing）支配；反弹后复杂度的增长与宇宙学粒子产生之间存在强关联；“啁啾”贡献可作为过渡过程的几何记忆，量化粒子创造的信息成本。

Conclusion: Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量方法为反弹宇宙学中的复杂度研究提供了精确工具；复杂度中的“啁啾”分量是连接时空几何演化与量子信息成本的关键桥梁。

Abstract: We investigate the evolution of circuit complexity for a quantum scalar field in a non-singular bouncing cosmological background. Unlike previous perturbative approaches, we utilize the Lewis-Riesenfeld invariant method to derive an exact non-perturbative framework for the complexity evolution across the bounce. We demonstrate that the complexity remains finite at the bounce, dominated by the squeezing of the quantum state due to spacetime contraction. Crucially, we find that the post-bounce growth of complexity exhibits a strong correlation with cosmological particle production. Our analysis reveals that the "chirping" contribution to complexity acts as a geometric memory of the transition, effectively quantifying the information cost of particle creation in non-trivial spacetime geometries.

Result: 得到状态方程参数满足w ≥ -(D-4)/D（D ≥ 5）；弦性SECs对w施加的普适约束在辐射主导和物质主导时期均成立；分别给出了点粒子属性、宇宙学常数和扩展物体自由度对EoS参数的贡献。

Conclusion: 弦性扩展物体的强能量条件为高维宇宙学中的状态方程参数提供了普适性约束，并将该约束与四维点粒子情形相联系，拓展了传统能量条件的适用范围。

Abstract: We construct the strong energy conditions (SECs) for both massive and massless stringy extended objects in the higher dimensional cosmology (HDC) with cosmological constant $Λ$. Exploiting these conditions, we find the equation of state (EoS) parameters \mbox{$w\geq -(D-4)/D$} for both the massive and massless stringy extended objects in $D$ {$(D\geq 5)$} dimensional cosmology. The stringy SECs impose a universal constraint on $w$ that remains valid across both radiation- and matter-dominated eras. We elucidate the relations between the EoS parameter in the HDC with cosmological constant and that of Hawking--Penrose limit for the massive and massless point particles in the four dimensions. We evaluate the EoS parameters in terms of the contributions from the point particle property, cosmological constant, and extended object degrees of freedom, respectively. We also investigate the weak energy condition for the massive and massless stringy extended objects in the HDC, and those for the massive and massless point particles in the four dimensions,~respectively.

### [86] [Running Vacuum in the expanding Universe: a unified QFT paradigm for Inflation and Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05352)
*Joan Solà Peracaula*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出运行真空模型（RVM），基于弯曲时空中的量子场论（QFT），认为真空能量密度（VED）和引力常数G均随哈勃率H动态演化，从而为暗能量（DE）和早期宇宙暴胀提供统一的理论框架，无需引入暴胀子场，且与DESI观测数据吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统ΛCDM模型中刚性的宇宙学常数Λ已长期面临危机；从量子场论出发，一个随宇宙膨胀而演化的Λ在直觉上更合理，因此需要建立动态真空能量密度的理论基础。

Method: 在弯曲时空量子场论框架下，量子效应导出的真空能量密度ρ_vac是哈勃率H及其时间导数的函数；同时牛顿常数G也随H对数演化；早期宇宙中真空涨落产生高阶项～H⁴，触发快速暴胀（RVM暴胀），无需引入暴胀子场。

Result: 动态真空能量密度在当前时期缓慢演化（δρ_vac ~ O(m_Pl²H²)），为暗能量提供了可能的根本起源；早期宇宙中高阶真空涨落可驱动快速暴胀，且该机制与Starobinsky暴胀不同（后者中H从不恒定）；该框架与DESI测量结果一致，偏好动态暗能量而非刚性Λ项。

Conclusion: RVM提供了一个统一的量子场论框架，将暗能量和暴胀整合为描述宇宙整体的现实理论，其预测的动态真空能量密度受到当前观测数据支持。

Abstract: The concordance $Λ$CDM model, based on a rigid $Λ$-term for the entire cosmic history, has been in crisis for a long time. In our expanding Universe, an evolving $Λ$ with the expansion is intuitively much more reasonable. In the running vacuum model (RVM) framework, based on quantum field theory (QFT) in curved spacetime, quantum effects induce a vacuum energy density (VED) $ρ_{\rm vac}=Λ/(8πG)$ which is a function of the Hubble rate $H$ and its time derivatives, $ρ_{\rm vac}=ρ_{\rm vac}(H, \dot{H},\ddot{H},\dots)$. Currently, $ρ_{\rm vac}$ evolves very slowly with the expansion, $δρ_{\rm vac}\sim {\cal O}(m_{Pl} ^2 H^2)$, and this fact provides a possible fundamental origin of dark energy (DE), conceived as dynamical vacuum energy. In the RVM, Newton's $G$ is also evolving, but much more slowly (logarithmically with $H$): $G=G(\ln H)$. In the very early universe, the vacuum fluctuations induce higher (even) powers, e.g. $\sim H^4$, capable of triggering fast inflation in a very short period, in which $H$ is very large and approximately constant. This is the mechanism of `RVM-inflation'. It does not require an `inflaton' field since inflation is brought about by pure QFT effects on the dynamical background. It differs from Starobinsky's inflation, where $H$ is never constant. Furthermore, the dynamics of $ρ_{\rm vac}(H)$ and $G(H)$ can also have implications on the frequently discussed possibility that the fundamental `constants' of Nature can be mildly evolving with the cosmic expansion. Putting things together, a unified QFT framework of dark energy and inflation ensues as a realistic theory for the description of the universe as a whole on fundamental grounds. In it, dynamical VED is predicted and is much welcomed, since it fits in with current DESI measurements, preferring dynamical DE over a rigid $Λ$ term.

</details>


### [87] [Spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat Berwald vacuum solutions in Finsler gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05427)
*Nicoleta Voicu,Diana - Maria Birla,Christian Pfeifer*

TL;DR: 本文针对SO(3)对称、渐近平坦但非Ricci平坦的Berwald-Finsler时空，求解了Finsler引力真空方程，首次得到了三类非平凡精确球对称真空解，并证明这些解可用于描述紧致天体周围的引力场，超越黎曼几何描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在Finsler几何框架下寻找能够描述紧致天体外部引力场的非Ricci平坦精确解，填补球对称Berwald-Finsler时空中非平凡真空解的研究空白。

Method: 考虑SO(3)对称的Berwald-Finsler时空，施加渐近平坦且因果结构良好的条件，限定出一类可解的时空类别；随后在该类中严格求解Finsler引力真空方程，并利用(α,β)-Finsler结构（由伪黎曼度量和1-形式构造）表征所得解族。

Result: 在所有球对称Berwald时空中，仅有一类同时满足渐近平坦性和良好因果结构；在该类中，Finsler引力真空方程给出三族非Ricci平坦的解系，这是首批非平凡精确球对称真空解，且均为(α,β)-Finsler型。

Conclusion: Finsler几何中存在SO(3)对称、渐近平坦且非Ricci平坦的真空解，这些解有望突破黎曼几何框架，用于描述紧致天体周围的引力场。

Abstract: So-called Berwald-Finsler spacetimes are Finsler spacetimes that are closest to pseudo-Riemannian geometry, as their canonical nonlinear connection defines an affine connection on spacetime. In spherical symmetry, these geometries can be used to describe the gravitational field outside of compact objects. We solve the Finsler gravity vacuum equation for $SO(3)$-symmetric Berwald spacetimes that are asyptotically flat, but not Ricci flat. We find that among all spherically symmetric Berwald spacetimes, only one class is compatible with asymptotic flatness and a well defined causal structure. For this class, we completely solve the Finsler gravity vacuum equation and find three families of non-Ricci flat solutions -- which represent the first non-trivial, exact spherically symmetric vacuum solutions. They are so-called $(α,β)$-Finsler spacetimes that are constructed from a pseudo-Riemannnian metric and a 1-form. In particular, we show, by providing a concrete example, that in Finsler geometry there exist $SO(3)$-symmetric, asymptotically flat vacuum solutions that are not Ricci flat; these solutions are promising candidates to model the gravitational field around compact objects, beyond their Riemannian description.

</details>


### [88] [Curvature conditions for generalized singularity theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05453)
*Jeremías Daín,Gustavo Dotti*

Abstract: We study the curvature conditions introduced in [Class. Quant. Grav. 27, 152002] to predict focal points for trapped spacelike submanifolds in spacetimes of arbitrary dimensions, with the purpose of generalizing Penrose's singularity theorem to compact trapped submanifolds (CTMs) of codimension higher than two. We find that these conditions do not apply in general but may apply for specific CTMs. As a result, higher codimension CTMs may still work as singularity predictors, although the possibility that they intersect the domain of outer communications cannot be ruled out using standard arguments.

</details>


### [89] [Improved unimodular black holes with self-consistent renormalization scale identification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05507)
*Christopher D. Carone*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将重整化尺度（renormalization scale）识别为径向坐标的函数，对单模黑洞（unimodular black hole）度量进行重整化群（renormalization group）改进，并基于最小性和量纲分析（dimensional analysis）的识别方案，得到若干非奇异的单模黑洞度量，并确定了黑洞质量间隙（mass gaps），指出其与文献中其他非奇异黑洞度量的定性相似性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对单模黑洞度量进行重整化群改进，以消除经典广义相对论中黑洞奇点（singularity）问题，并探索非奇异黑洞度量的构造方法。

Method: 将重整化尺度识别为径向坐标的函数，并使其自洽地依赖于改进度量本身的参数；采用基于最小性（minimality）和量纲分析（dimensional analysis）的识别方案来构建非奇异单模黑洞度量。

Result: 得到若干非奇异的单模黑洞度量，并确定了黑洞质量间隙（mass gaps）；这些度量与文献中已有讨论的其他非奇异黑洞度量在定性上具有相似性。

Conclusion: 重整化群改进方法可以系统地构造非奇异单模黑洞度量，且所得结果与已有非奇异黑洞度量在定性层面一致，暗示了该类构造的普适性。

Abstract: We consider the renormalization group improvement of unimodular black hole metrics with an identification of the renormalization scale as a function of the radial coordinate that is self-consistent in that it depends on parameters of the improved metric. Considering identifications that are motivated by minimality and dimensional analysis, we arrive at a number of non-singular unimodular black hole metrics. We determine the black hole mass gaps and note the qualitative similarities to other non-singular black hole metrics that have been discussed in the literature.

</details>


### [90] [Black Bounce Solutions from a Self-Interacting 3-Form Field in General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05508)
*Francisco S. N. Lobo,Manuel E. Rodrigues*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一类由自相互作用3-形式场（3-form field）与标量场（scalar field）耦合广义相对论所支撑的新型黑洞反弹（black-bounce）解。该解光滑插值于黑洞与可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）之间，展示了3-形式框架在正则广义相对论中的数学自洽性与观测可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索3-形式场在广义相对论中能否提供必要的各向异性有效应力，以支撑从黑洞到可穿越虫洞的光滑过渡几何，并希望在不依赖反向重构程序（reconstruction procedure）的前提下，直接从作用量原理导出完整解。

Method: 利用四维中3-形式与1-形式之间的霍奇对偶性（Hodge duality）简化场方程，通过对耦合的爱因斯坦场方程、标量场方程和3-形式场方程进行代数组合与直接积分，获得精确解。

Result: 发现两类解：第一类具有全局幻象标量场（phantom scalar field）和反正切依赖度规函数，在3-形式耦合消失时约化为Schwarzschild-(anti) de Sitter时空；第二类具有常值3-形式拉格朗日量，标量场在反弹附近为幻象，在事件视界外则为典型场，此特征此前主要出现在修正引力理论中。两类解均为全局正则，Kretschmann标量有限，且具有非对称视界结构。

Conclusion: 3-形式黑洞反弹框架在数学上自洽且观测上可行，为在纯广义相对论中实现正则与幻象标量场共存提供了新途径。

Abstract: We construct a new class of black-bounce solutions sourced by a self-interacting 3-form field minimally coupled to general relativity and a scalar field. The 3-form field, which naturally arises in string theory, supergravity, and cosmological models, provides the anisotropic effective stresses required to sustain regular geometries that interpolate smoothly between black holes and traversable wormholes. By exploiting the Hodge duality between a 3-form and a 1-form in four dimensions, we reduce the field equations and obtain exact solutions through the direct integration of the coupled equations of motion. In particular, the solutions are derived from algebraic combinations and manipulations of the Einstein, scalar, and 3-form field equations, starting from a complete action principle, without employing the usual reconstruction procedure in which the metric ansatz is imposed a priori and the matter sector is reconstructed afterwards. This approach reveals two distinct classes of solutions. The first one yields a globally phantom scalar field and a metric function with a characteristic arctangent dependence, reducing to the Schwarzschild-(anti) de Sitter spacetime in the limit of vanishing 3-form coupling. The second class produces a constant 3-form Lagrangian and, remarkably, a partially canonical scalar field, namely phantom only near the bounce and canonical outside the event horizon, a feature previously attainable mainly in modified theories of gravity, but which emerges here within pure general relativity. Both families are globally regular, as confirmed by the finiteness of the Kretschmann scalar, and exhibit an asymmetric horizon structure inherited from the 3-form energy-density distribution. These results demonstrate that the 3-form black-bounce framework is both mathematically consistent and observationally viable.

</details>

Result: 发现两种带有恒定二次标量毛发（constant secondary scalar hair）的标量化极端黑洞，并通过两种方法精确验证了这些解的存在。

This theory is inspired by the bosonic sector of $N=4$ supergravity. Two scalarzied extremal black holes are found with constant secondary scalar hair. We confirm that these are exactly obtained from the standard scalarization and entropy function approach. This may imply that it is not easy to find extremal black holes with primary scalar hair.

### [92] [Asymptotically-flat Black holes in Bumblebee gravity: Exact solutions and Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05801)
*Jinbo Yang,Zhan-Feng Mai,Dicong Liang,Lijing Shao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了静态球对称时空下大黄蜂引力理论（bumblebee gravity theory）的解析解，其中大黄蜂矢量场仅具有非零时间分量。在识别出允许渐近平坦黑洞解的参数空间后，进一步研究了这些黑洞的热力学性质，推导出$Y$荷与$X$势的解析公式。利用解析结果验证了先前数值工作，并发现了多个被遗漏的情况，包括无界荷质比、可穿越虫洞构型、霍金温度的非单调转折行为以及常$Y$热容量的双发散点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在静态球对称时空中，假设大黄蜂矢量场仅保留时间分量，通过解析方法求解场方程，确定允许渐近平坦黑洞解的参数条件。基于解析解，推导满足Smarr关系与热力学第一定律所需的$Y$荷与$X$势的解析表达式。

Result: 解析结果证实了先前数值发现的正确性，并揭示了四种被遗漏的情况：（i）当非最小耦合参数$\xi>2\kappa$时，荷质比无界；（ii）$\xi<0$的过荷解中出现可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）构型；（iii）霍金温度（Hawking temperature）随荷质比变化呈现非单调转折行为；（iv）常$Y$热容量存在两个发散点。

Conclusion: 解析方法有效弥补了纯数值分析的不足，拓展了对大黄蜂引力黑洞相空间与热力学行为的理解。所发现的新奇现象为进一步研究修正引力理论中的黑洞物理提供了重要线索。

Abstract: We construct analytic solutions to the bumblebee gravity theory in static and spherically symmetric spacetimes, where the bumblebee vector field admits only a non-vanishing temporal component. In particular, we identify the parameter space that allows for asymptotically flat black hole solutions. We further investigate the thermodynamic properties of these black holes and obtained the analytic formulas for the $Y$ charge and $X$ potential, which were introduced in the prior work to ensure the Smarr relation and the first law of black hole thermodynamics. Using the new analytic results, we verify the numerical findings reported in early work and uncover multiple cases missed in the previous numerical analysis. These include: (i) an unbounded charge-mass ratio when the non-minimal coupling parameter $ξ$ is larger than $2κ$, (ii) the emergence of a traversable wormhole configuration for overcharged solutions with $ξ<0$, (iii) the non-monotonic turning behavior of the Hawking temperature as a function of the charge-mass ratio, and (iv) the presence of two divergent points in the constant-$Y$ heat capacity.

Result: 环奇点区域应被描述为两个（平坦）圆盘而非一个；通常的世界面表示缺失了r<0区域的多个副本，该区域可表示为共形图中的三角形。

Abstract: The region spaning the ring singularity in the Kerr black hole solution is described here as two (flat) discs rather than one. From this viewpoint it follows that the usual depiction of the worldsheet $θ=π/2$, $φ$ constant (in Boyer-Lindquist coordinates) is missing (multiple copies of) the region $r<0$, representable as a triangle in the usual conformal diagram style.

### [94] [The first decade of gravitational-wave measurements of black hole spins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06209)

TL;DR: 本文综述了引力波探测十年后，通过超过一百例确认事件对恒星级黑洞自旋（spin）的测量进展，系统总结了自旋的物理预言、波形印记、观测约束及天体物理含义，并展望了未来探测器灵敏度提升带来的研究前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋测量长期以来被视为追踪致密双星（compact-object binary）形成与演化的有力工具，因为不同形成通道会在总体层面上产生独特的自旋特征。随着引力波事件目录不断扩大，有必要系统回顾自旋测量的当前进展及其对天体物理的启示。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，首先概述来自孤立双星演化、星团动力学形成、活动星系核（AGN）盘内形成以及层级三合星（hierarchical triples）等主要形成通道对黑洞自旋大小和方向的理论预言；其次描述自旋效应在引力波波形中的印记及单个事件中自旋的可测量性；最后综述当前对自旋大小、方向及有效自旋参数（effective spin parameters）的总体约束，包括与质量和红移的相关性。

Result: 对超过一百例确认引力波事件的自旋测量揭示了恒星级黑洞自旋的新见解；目前已获得自旋大小、方向及有效自旋参数的总体约束，并发现了自旋与质量、红移的相关性。

Conclusion: 本文指出了尚待解决的关键问题与未来展望，强调提高探测器灵敏度将能够对单个事件及整个双黑洞（binary black hole）群体的自旋测量实现更高的精度。

Abstract: A decade after the first direct detection of gravitational waves, the growing catalog of over one hundred confirmed events is revealing new insights into the spins of stellar-mass black holes. Spin measurements have long been heralded as a promising tracer of compact-object binary formation and evolution, as different formation channels predict unique spin signatures on a population level. In this review, we summarize the astrophysics, phenomenology, and current measurements of black hole spins. We begin with an overview of the predictions for black hole spin magnitudes and orientations from leading formation channels--isolated binary evolution, dynamical formation in clusters, formation in AGN disks, and hierarchical triples. We then describe the imprint of spin effects on the gravitational waveform and the measurability of spin in individual events. Finally, we review current population-level constraints on spin magnitudes, orientations, and effective spin parameters, including correlations with mass and redshift, and discuss their astrophysical implications. We conclude by highlighting open questions and future prospects, emphasizing how improved detector sensitivity will enable increasingly precise spin measurements for both individual events and the binary black hole population as a whole.

### [95] [On Cosmological Correlators with Boundary Contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06282)
*Yanjiao Ma,Dong-Gang Wang,Xiangwei Wang,Yi Wang,Wenqi Yu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了准德西特（quasi-de Sitter）时空中宇宙学关联函数（cosmological correlators）的边界贡献（boundary contributions），建立了边界项与场重定义（field redefinitions）之间的对应关系，并在 dS 不变和 boost 破缺两种场景下对 massive-exchange 图进行了具体分析，给出了边界项导致非零可观测量（observables）的判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学关联函数同时受到准德西特时空体相互作用（bulk interactions）和暴胀结束时边界项（boundary terms）的贡献，但边界项通常被认为可忽略或与场重定义（field redefinitions）相关。本文旨在从宇宙学自举（cosmological bootstrap）视角重新审视这一问题，揭示边界项何时会产生非零的可观测效应。

Method: 首先建立边界项与场重定义之间的对应关系，给出边界项导致非零观测贡献的判据；随后在 dS 不变和 boost 破缺两种场景下，针对 massive-exchange 图（massive-exchange diagrams）应用分部积分（IBP）和运动方程（EoM）等技术，对高阶导数交换关联函数进行约化与分类。

Result: 在 dS 等距（isometries）理论中，利用 IBP 和场重定义将导数与非导数交换图相联系，提取了领先边界贡献和红外发散项（IR-divergent pieces），并推导了高阶导数交换关联函数间的递推关系（recursion relations）；在 dS boost 破缺理论中，利用 IBP 和 EoM 将交换图约化为一组独立模板基（basis of independent templates），并在有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）框架下对边界贡献进行了分类。

Conclusion: 本文的结果为系统研究暴胀时空边界物理（boundary physics）提供了新的分析框架和方法论基础，表明边界贡献在特定条件下不可忽略且具有可观测意义。

Abstract: Cosmological correlators receive contributions from both field interactions in the bulk of quasi-de Sitter (dS) spacetime and boundary terms at the end of inflation. While most of the research efforts focus on the former, boundary contributions are normally believed to be negligible or related to field redefinitions that are associated with redundancies of the bulk Lagrangian. In this paper, we revisit this topic in the light of the cosmological bootstrap. We first establish the correspondence between boundary terms and field redefinitions for cosmological correlators. This result provides a set of criteria for determining when boundary terms lead to non-vanishing contributions to cosmological observables. Next, we apply this general understanding to concrete examples of correlators from massive-exchange diagrams, in both dS-invariant and boost-breaking scenarios. For theories with dS isometries, both IBP and field redefinitions are used to relate derivative and non-derivative exchange diagrams, from which the leading boundary contributions and IR-divergent pieces are extracted; we also derive recursion relations among higher-derivative exchange correlators. For theories with broken dS boosts, we use IBP and EoM to reduce exchange diagrams to a basis of independent templates, and then present a classification of the boundary contributions in the general effective field theory framework. These results pave the way for a more systematic investigation on the boundary physics of the inflationary spacetime.

</details>

Abstract: We enlarged the capabilities of the publicly available Mathematica-based tool $\tt GrayHawk$. This second version expands the spectrum of metrics that can be considered in two distinct and disjoined directions. First, it enables a fully numerical computation of the tortoise coordinates integral, allowing the user to account for many metrics for which an analytic computation was impractical. Second, it extends the scattering problem to wormhole solutions. The pool of pre-loaded metrics is enriched, enabling immediate testing of the new features, and the code's modular structure is maintained to facilitate easy modification. This implementation proves $\tt GrayHawk$ adaptability and makes it an even more powerful tool for studying black holes, wormholes, Hawking radiation, and other features involving field propagation on curved manifolds. The codes described in this work are publicly available at \href{https://github.com/marcocalza89/GrayHawk-v2}{\faGithub}.

### [97] [$\tt BlackHawk$ $\tt v3.0$: Hawking Radiation from Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06355)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功扩展了BlackHawk代码的功能，使其能够计算多种新黑洞度量的霍金辐射谱，并提高了计算精度与效率。

Conclusion: BlackHawk v3.0成为一个高度通用的工具，可用于研究多种黑洞模型下的霍金辐射。该代码已在https://blackhawk.hepforge.org/公开提供。

Abstract: We present $\tt BlackHawk$ $\tt v3.0$, a major update of the public code designed to compute Hawking radiation spectra of black holes. Building upon previous versions, this release considerably extends the range of black hole geometries that can be studied by implementing several new spherically symmetric metrics: the Bardeen and Hayward regular black holes, the Simpson-Visser and Peltola-Kunstatter black-bounces, the D'Ambrosio-Rovelli black hole-to-white hole metric, and the Babichev-Charmousis-Lehébel black hole. For each metric, we compute the corresponding Hawking temperatures and greybody factors, enabling the determination of primary Hawking emission spectra for particles of different spins. The greybody factors are obtained through dedicated numerical routines based on the companion code $\tt GrayHawk$. Additionally, $\tt BlackHawk$ $\tt v3.0$ introduces several technical improvements aimed at enhancing precision and efficiency, providing a highly versatile tool. The code is publicly available at https://blackhawk.hepforge.org/

### [98] [Evolution of Realistic Neutron star in the framework of f (Q) gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06371)
*Samprity Das,Surajit Chattopadhyay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在$f(Q)$引力（$f(Q)$ gravity）框架下，基于Krori-Barua度规（Krori-Barua metric）分析了四颗脉冲星作为致密天体（compact objects）的物态性质，发现非度量性（nonmetricity）的线性依赖下各向异性因子为正且单调递增，所有天体的致密性均位于Buchdahl极限（Buchdahl's limit）内，表明这些脉冲星是修改引力背景下的中子星（neutron stars）；通过卡方检验（Chi-Square test）验证了模型质量与观测质量的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在$f(Q)$引力框架下，探索具有非度量性$Q$的引力相互作用对现实致密天体的影响，并检验这些天体在修改引力理论中的物理可行性。

Method: 选取各向异性运动方程并确定$f(Q)$为$Q$的线性函数；采用Krori-Barua度规求解场方程；计算LMC X-4、SMC X-4、Cen X-3和Vela X-1四颗脉冲星的各向异性因子；通过三十个不同的$a$值进行卡方检验，比较模型质量与观测质量。

Result: 各向异性因子为正且单调递增，表明核力可对抗引力吸引；四颗脉冲星的致密性均在Buchdahl极限内，判定其为$f(Q)$修改引力背景下的中子星；表面红移（surface redshift）随时间变化，致密天体保持致密性。

Conclusion: 在$f(Q)$引力框架下，所研究的四颗脉冲星符合中子星特征，模型质量与观测值无显著差异，验证了线性$f(Q)$模型描述致密天体的有效性。

Abstract: This work analyses and evaluates a few realistic compact objects in the presence of a gravitational interaction between two particles with a nonmetricity $Q$. In the $f(Q)$ gravity framework, we have selected the anisotropic equation of motion and have determined $f(Q)$ to be a linear function of nonmetricity $Q$. To evaluate the field equations in our work, we have opted to employ the Krori-Barua metric. We calculated the anisotropic factor for each of the four compact objects and found that the anisotropic component is positive and increases monotonically and interpreted that the nuclear force can oppose the gravitational attraction. At last, the relationship between mass and radius has been determined and illustrated visually. We have noted that the compactness of the pulsars LMC X-4, SMC X-4, Cen X-3, and Vela X-1 is inside the Buchdahl's limit for varying values of $a$. This has led to the interpretation that these pulsars are neutron stars in a modified gravity background of $f(Q)$. In addition, we calculated the model mass and, using thirty distinct choices of $a$, ran the Chi-Square test to see if there was a noticeable difference between the observed and model-generated masses. We have also looked at how the surface redshift has changed over time and whether the compact objects in our model that were previously described are compact.

</details>


### [99] [Detecting Tidal Resonances in Binary Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06376)
*Fabian Gittins,Harsh Narola,Thibeau Wouters,Peter T. H. Pang,Tanja Hinderer,Chris Van Den Broeck*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次使用完全贝叶斯方法研究爱因斯坦望远镜（Einstein Telescope）探测双中子星并合过程中潮汐共振（tidal resonance）的能力，发现其可识别共振模式并敏感至相位移动 ΔΦ≈0.03，且忽略共振会偏置潮汐形变率（tidal deformability）的推断，从而确立潮汐共振作为未来探测器实现星震学（asteroseismology）的可测量途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双中子星因引力波辐射而旋近时，上升的潮汐频率会共振激发振动模式，这些振荡可作为恒星内部结构的震学探针，但引力波干涉仪能否测量这些共振仍待确认。

Method: 采用完全贝叶斯（fully Bayesian）分析方法，模拟一年的观测数据，并对其中200个最强的引力波信号进行统计分析。

Result: 爱因斯坦望远镜能够识别共振模式，对于有利事件可探测到小至 ΔΦ≈0.03 的引力波相位移动；若忽略共振效应，推断的潮汐形变率会出现偏差。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了潮汐共振是未来探测器实现星震学的可测量途径。

Abstract: As a binary neutron star inspirals due to the emission of gravitational waves, the rising tidal frequency resonantly excites vibrational modes. These oscillations are seismological probes of the rich stellar interior, yet it remains to be established whether gravitational-wave interferometers can measure them. Here, we present the first fully Bayesian study of the capability of the Einstein Telescope to detect tidal resonances. We simulate one year of observations and analyse the 200 loudest signals. We find that the Einstein Telescope can identify resonant modes and is sensitive to gravitational-wave phase shifts as small as $ΔΦ\approx 0.03$ for favourable events. We further show that neglecting resonances can bias the inferred tidal deformabilities. These results establish tidal resonances as a measurable route for asteroseismology with future detectors.

</details>


### [100] [Charged black string immersed in a quintessence fluid and string cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06435)
*Leonardo G. Barbosa,Franciele M. da Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的静态解，描述了一个浸入Kiselev型精质流体（quintessence fluid）和弦云（cloud of strings）中的带电黑弦（charged black string）；求解了度规与场方程，对一般精质态参数进行了分析，并在物理相关情况$w_q=-2/3$下给出了显式结果；分析了事件视界结构和Kretschmann标量，验证了能量条件约束，推导了霍金温度（Hawking temperature）和热容（heat capacity）等热力学性质以识别稳定性区间，并研究了零测地线（null geodesics）的光子柱（photon cylinder）。该解通过同时引入精质和弦云参数，推广了已知的带电黑弦时空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有带电黑弦解未同时考虑精质流体和弦云两种背景物质的影响；作者旨在构建一个更一般的静态解，以同时纳入这两种物质场，从而推广已知的带电黑弦时空。

Method: 通过求解度规与耦合场方程，对一般精质态参数（quintessence state parameter）$w_q$进行解析求解，并在物理相关情况$w_q=-2/3$下给出显式度规形式；分析事件视界结构，计算Kretschmann标量以检查曲率奇点，检验能量条件（energy conditions），推导霍金温度和热容进行热力学稳定性分析，并求解零测地线的光子柱。

Result: 给出了浸入Kiselev型精质流体和弦云中的带电黑弦的显静态解；确定了事件视界结构与曲率奇点行为；在能量条件约束下得到了满足热力学稳定性的参数区间；计算了光子柱的半径及其对精质和弦云参数的依赖关系。

Conclusion: 该解作为已知带电黑弦时空的推广，同时引入了精质和弦云两种背景物质，丰富了黑弦时空的解析家族；精质参数和弦云参数共同调控视界结构、热力学稳定性及测地线光学特征，为研究暗能量背景下的弦状引力对象提供了新模型。

Abstract: We present a new static solution describing a charged black string immersed in a Kiselev-type quintessence fluid and a cloud of strings. The metric and field equations are solved for a general quintessence state parameter, with explicit results provided for the physically relevant case $w_q = -2/3$. We analyze the event-horizon structure and the Kretschmann scalar, verify energy-condition constraints, and derive thermodynamic properties including the Hawking temperature and heat capacity to identify stability regimes. Finally, we investigate the photon cylinder for null geodesics. The solution generalizes known charged black-string spacetimes by simultaneously including quintessence and a string-cloud parameter.

### [101] [Short Gravitational-Wave Transients as Probes of Cosmic Domain Walls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06478)
*Tore Boybeyi,Doga Veske,David Maibach*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究测试了GW190521和GW231123这两个引力波事件是否可用拓扑暗物质（TDM）中的宇宙畴壁模型解释。虽然双黑洞（BBH）假设在单个事件中更受贝叶斯因子支持，但两事件共享的TDM参数在联合拟合中具有一致性，且注入测试显示TDM与高自旋BBH信号存在形态简并性（morphological degeneracy），表明多事件参数一致性检验可为畴壁暗物质搜索提供新判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW190521和GW231123被报道为与大质量双黑洞并合（binary black hole coalescence）相一致的短时引力波瞬变信号，但其极高的总质量和自旋大小挑战了标准孤立双星演化模型，因此有必要探索替代解释，特别是拓扑暗物质（topological dark matter, TDM）中宇宙畴壁（cosmic domain walls）的起源假说。

Method: 研究采用物理动机驱动的畴壁模板对LIGO Hanford和Livingston的应变数据进行拟合；分别对两个事件进行独立拟合，并首次对来自同一标量场（scalar field）的畴壁信号进行联合拟合（joint fit），同时在独立噪声实现和不同天区位置上检验共享TDM参数的一致性。此外，还进行了注入测试（injection test）以评估TDM信号在BBH假设下的恢复行为。

Result: BBH假设在单个事件中均被支持，GW231123和GW190521的对数贝叶斯因子（log₁₀ℬ_BBH/TDM）分别为12.2和11.3，但这些值低于在邻近噪声段中注入最大后验BBH波形后典型恢复的数值。联合拟合虽未优于BBH信号，但两事件与同一标量场一致，共享TDM参数在不同噪声实现和天区位置上表现出一致性。注入测试表明，TDM信号在BBH假设下会被系统性恢复为具有大自旋参数的信号，揭示了两者间的形态简并性（morphological degeneracy）。

Conclusion: 多事件参数一致性检验（multi-event parameter consistency test）可为即将到来的观测运行中的畴壁暗物质搜索提供新的判别手段，以应对TDM与高自旋BBH信号之间的形态简并问题。

Abstract: GW190521 and GW231123 have been reported as short-duration gravitational-wave transients consistent with very massive binary black hole (BBH) coalescences whose inferred parameters, i.e., exceptionally high total masses and spin magnitudes, challenge standard isolated binary stellar evolution. We test a topological dark matter (TDM) interpretation invoking cosmic domain walls by fitting a physically motivated domain wall template to the LIGO Hanford and Livingston strain data. The BBH hypothesis is individually favored, with $\log_{10}\mathcal{B}_{\rm BBH/TDM}=12.2$ and $11.3$ for GW231123 and GW190521, respectively. However, these values are lower than those typically recovered from matched maximum a posteriori BBH waveforms injected into nearby noise segments. We further perform, for the first time, a joint fit in which domain wall signals from a single underlying scalar field are constrained simultaneously by both events. Although not favored over BBH signals, we find the two events are consistent with a common scalar field, with shared TDM parameters agreeing across independent noise realizations and sky locations. We further find that injected TDM transients are systematically recovered under the BBH hypothesis with large spin parameters, revealing a morphological degeneracy that could mask genuine domain wall signals. This analysis demonstrates that multi-event parameter consistency tests provide a new discriminant for domain wall dark matter searches in upcoming observing runs.

### [102] [Numerical self-force calculations for scalar particles, formulated in the lab frame](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06487)
*Stamatis Vretinaris,Erik Schnetter,Badri Krishnan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自洽的标量粒子与标量场（包括辐射反作用）相互作用的运动方程推导方法，采用有限离散化尺度、先选态矢量后再推导、在实验室系中显式建立方程等三方面创新，并给出基于有限体积和谱方法的两种离散化方案及一维数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在处理粒子加速产生的自洽辐射反作用（radiation reaction）时存在复杂性和协变性约束带来的推导困难，本文旨在提出一种简化的、适用于数值计算的替代方案。

Method: (1) 引入小而有限的离散化长度尺度 $h$，将粒子视为有限尺寸对象；(2) 在推导运动方程之前选定系统的态矢量（state vector）；(3) 在实验室坐标系中显式建立方程，而非使用显式协变（manifestly covariant）形式。基于此自洽方法得到有效源方法（effective source method），并给出有限体积法和谱方法两种离散化方案。

Result: 一维数值计算结果与解析解呈现极好的一致性（excellent agreement）。

Conclusion: 该自洽方法显著简化了运动方程的推导过程，直接适用于数值计算，并可推广至电动力学或广义相对论领域。

Abstract: We derive equations of motion for scalar particles self-consistently interacting with a scalar field,including the radiation produced by the particles' acceleration. Our approach differs in three key aspects from current methods: (1) we assume a small but finite discretization length scale $h$, which allows us to treat the particle as a small but finite object, (2) we choose the state vector for the system before deriving equations of motion, and (3) we formulate the equations explicitly in the lab frame and not in a manifestly covariant manner. This approach, which is self-consistent, happens to greatly simplify the resulting equations and their derivation, and is directly suitable for numerical calculations. The result is an effective source method which generalizes to electrodynamics or general relativity in a straightforward manner (although we do not consider this here). We then provide two possible discretizations of these equations, based on finite volumes and spectral methods, and show results of one-dimensional calculations. These calculations show excellent agreement with analytic solutions.

</details>

### [103] [Hydrogen-induced lattice cohesion weakening favors atomic displacement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05325)
*Liang Gao,Yiran Mao,Markus Wilde,Xiaoou Yi,Cong Li,Shiwei Wang,Thomas Schwarz-Selinger,Jan Coenen,Richard Kembleton,Sebastijan Brezinsek,Christian Linsmeier,Guanghong Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 摘要发现，金属中的晶格溶解氢（lattice-dissolved hydrogen, LDH）通过削弱晶格内聚强度（lattice cohesion），即使在亚阈值应力（sub-threshold stress）下也能促进原子位移和位错运动，从而为氢致局部塑性（hydrogen-enhanced localized plasticity, HELP）机制提供了原子尺度的物理解释，并通过低能氢等离子体实验定量验证了这一效应，建立了解读氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）的新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解原子位移（atomic displacement）作为金属中各种变形与损伤（从辐照缺陷产生到应力驱动位错运动）的基础过程，其背后的核心控制因素是原子间的内聚强度（interatomic cohesion strength）。本文旨在阐明晶格溶解氢如何通过削弱内聚强度来影响这一过程，并揭示其与氢脆现象的关联。

Method: 通过识别金属中在直接氢暴露下形成的晶格溶解氢（lattice-dissolved hydrogen, LDH），定性分析其对晶格内聚的削弱效应；进一步在低能氢等离子体暴露的金属表面进行定量验证——尽管入射离子动量不足以直接造成位移损伤，但大量缺陷仍被观察到，从而独立于缺陷捕获氢（defect-trapped H）量化了LDH的内聚削弱作用。

Result: 证实了晶格溶解氢能够有效削弱晶格内聚，从而在亚阈值应力（sub-threshold stress）范围内促进原子位移和位错运动，为氢致局部塑性（hydrogen-enhanced localized plasticity, HELP）提供了原子尺度的物理机制。低能氢等离子体实验定量验证了氢诱导的晶格内聚削弱效应。

Conclusion: 通过首次独立于缺陷捕获氢定量表征晶格溶解氢的内聚削弱效应，建立了解读氢脆（hydrogen embrittlement）的新范式（new paradigm），为理解氢致局部塑性提供了原子层面的透明物理机制。

Abstract: Atomic displacement -- the fundamental process underlying diverse deformation and damage phenomena in metals, from irradiation defect production to stress-driven dislocation motion -- is governed by interatomic cohesion strength. Here, lattice-dissolved hydrogen (LDH) occurring in metals under direct hydrogen exposure is identified to effectively weaken lattice cohesion, and thereby facilitating atomic displacement and dislocation movement upon plastic deformation in sub-threshold stress regime. This atomic-scale insight provides a physically transparent mechanism for hydrogen-enhanced localized plasticity implicated in hydrogen embrittlement. We quantitatively verify the hydrogen-induced lattice cohesion weakening effect on metal surfaces exposed to low-energy hydrogen plasma, where massive defects are generated despite the absence of sufficient ion momentum for direct displacement damage. By unprecedentedly quantifying the cohesion-weakening effect of LDH independently from defect-trapped H, we establish a new paradigm to understand hydrogen embrittlement.

</details>


### [104] [Interplay of non-local transport and local scattering during electron thermalization and spatial equilibration in laser-excited metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05457)
*Markus Uehlein,Tobias Held,Christopher Seibel,Sebastian T. Weber,Baerbel Rethfeld*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过玻尔兹曼输运方程的能量空间重新表述，统一描述了非局域输运与局域散射的相互作用，揭示了输运过程加速表面热化但延缓整个电子系统完全平衡的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超快激光激发金属会在空间和能量分布上同时产生电子非平衡态，其动力学由非局域输运（non-local transport）与热电子局域散射（local scattering）共同主导，但目前缺乏对这两个过程联合的微观描述。

Method: 对玻尔兹曼输运方程（Boltzmann transport equation）在能量空间中进行了重新表述，通过完整的碰撞积分（full collision integrals）一致地描述空间平衡化与散射过程。

Result: 输运通过移除非热载流子加速了辐照表面观测到的表观热化过程，但同时这种空间重新分布延缓了整个电子系统的完全平衡化。在前后表面处，主导过程随空间位置和能量窗口而不同。

Conclusion: 该工作深化了对光学厚激光驱动系统中电子非平衡过程相互作用的理解，对未来电子学应用具有相关启示。

Abstract: Ultrafast laser excitation of metals induces electronic nonequilibrium both in space and locally in the energy distribution. The subsequent dynamics are governed by the interplay between non-local transport and local scattering of hot electrons, yet combined microscopic descriptions of these processes remain sparse. Here, we disentangle the influence of these processes on thermalization using a reformulation of the Boltzmann transport equation in energy space that consistently describes both spatial equilibration and scattering through full collision integrals. Our results reveal that transport accelerates the apparent thermalization observed at the irradiated surface by removing athermal carriers, while the same spatial redistribution delays complete equilibration of the full electron system. We analyze the experimentally accessible energy-dependent dynamics at the front and back surface and find that the dominant process varies, depending on both position and on the energetic window. Overall, our work improves the understanding of the interplay of electronic nonequilibrium processes occurring in optically thick laser-driven systems with relevant implications for future electronic applications.

</details>


### [105] [Strong Optical-Optical Avoided Crossings Suppress Thermal Conductivity in Ga-Substituted TlInTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05803)
*Sayan Paul,Swapan K Pati*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算和线性化维格纳输运方程（LWTE），证明了在TlIn$_{0.5}$Ga$_{0.5}$Te$_2$中，光学-光学声子间的避免交叉（avoided crossing）能有效抑制晶格热导率（$κ_l$）。原始TlInTe$_2$中光学声子贡献了63%的$κ_l$，而经Ga替代引入对称性匹配后，光学声子分支形成避免交叉，显著降低群速度（$v_g$），使光学声子贡献降至44%，$κ_l$从0.568降至0.482 Wm$^{-1}$K$^{-1}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究广泛关注声学与光学声子之间避免交叉对晶格热导率（$κ_l$）的抑制作用，但光学声子之间的避免交叉效应因被认为对热输运贡献较弱而长期未获充分探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，验证光学-光学避免交叉能否有效抑制$κ_l$。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合线性化维格纳输运方程（linearized Wigner transport equation, LWTE）进行热输运模拟；通过不可约表示（irreducible representation）分析声子对称性，解释避免交叉产生的机制；采用模式平均输运分析（mode-averaged transport analysis）区分群速度和非简谐散射的贡献。

Result: 在TlIn$_{0.5}$Ga$_{0.5}$Te$_2$中，50% Ga替代使原始TlInTe$_2$中不同对称性表示的光学声子交叉点转变为相同对称性的避免交叉，形成能隙打开。这一变化显著抑制了光学声子群速度（$v_g$），使光学声子对$κ_l$的贡献从63%降至44%，300 K下$κ_l$从0.568降至0.482 Wm$^{-1}$K$^{-1}$。模式平均输运分析表明，$κ_l$抑制主要源于群速度降低，非简谐散射增强为次要因素。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了对称性调控的光学-光学避免交叉（symmetry-modified optical-optical avoided crossing）作为抑制光学声子主导热输运体系$κ_l$的有效策略，拓展了通过声子避免交叉降低晶格热导率的机制范围。

Abstract: In crystalline solids, avoided crossing between acoustic and optical phonons is widely recognized as an effective mechanism for suppressing lattice thermal conductivity ($κ_l$). However, the role of avoided crossings among optical phonons remains largely unexplored due to their weak contribution to heat transport. Here, using first-principles calculations combined with the linearized Wigner transport equation (LWTE), we demonstrate that optical-optical avoided crossings can effectively reduce ($κ_l$) in TlIn$_{0.5}$Ga$_{0.5}$Te$_2$. Pristine TlInTe$_2$ exhibits strong optical phonon-dominated heat transport, where optical phonons contribute nearly 63% of $κ_l$. The phonon dispersion of TlInTe$_2$ shows several crossing points in the optical region, which evolve into avoided crossings after 50% Ga substitution. Irreducible representation analysis reveals that the crossing phonon branches in TlInTe$_2$ belong to different symmetry representations, whereas the corresponding branches in TlIn$_{0.5}$Ga$_{0.5}$Te$_2$ possess the same symmetry representation, which enables phonon modes to couple and results in gap opening at the crossing points. These avoided crossings significantly suppress the optical phonon group velocity, thereby reducing the optical phonon contribution from 63% to 44% and lowering $κ_l$ from 0.568 to 0.482 Wm$^{-1}$K$^{-1}$ at 300 K. Mode-averaged transport analysis further confirms that the suppression of $κ_l$ is primarily governed by reduced phonon group velocity ($v_g$), while enhanced anharmonic scattering provides an additional secondary contribution. Our results establish symmetry-modified optical-optical avoided crossing as an effective route to suppress optical phonon transport and reduce $κ_l$ in systems where optical phonons significantly contribute to heat transport.

</details>


### [106] [The KNN rollercoaster: from bulk ceramics to phase engineered wafer-scale thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05974)
*Giulia Pavese,Federico Orlando,Fabio Melzi,Walter Piazzi,Andrea Pescarolo,Federico Maspero,Marco Asa,Riccardo Gianola,Andrea Picco,Andrea Serafini,Kui Yao,Silvia Picozzi,Laura Castoldi,Miguel-Ángel Badillo-Ávila,Riccardo Bertacco*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在8英寸硅晶圆上系统生长Mn掺杂K₁₋ₓNaₓNbO₃薄膜，系统改变Na含量进行表征。利用密度泛函理论（DFT）模拟从理论上支撑实验观察的结构与性能增强机制。

Result: 富钠（Na-rich, >70 at.%）组分可有效抑制焦绿石相形成和化学偏析，促进完全(001)面外取向的致密柱状生长。所得薄膜的剩余极化达14 μC/cm²，压电系数d₃₃,f = 79 pm/V，e₃₁,f = 10 C/m²。

Conclusion: 薄膜的最优化学计量比与块体等摩尔标准根本不同，需采用富钠组分以克服衬底约束。应变驱动的结构重取向至低对称单斜相（monoclinic phase）是性能增强的核心机制。该工作为KNN在微系统（microsystems）中的晶圆级集成建立了清晰的技术路径。

Abstract: Since the initial disclosure of the extraordinary piezoelectric coefficients of Potassium sodium niobate (KNN) in near-equimolar bulk ceramics, its development trajectory has resembled a rollercoaster, with its integration into microelectronics severely lagging due to thermodynamic stability issues and poor planar process compatibility. In this work, we revisit the bulk-derived phase diagram for the specific case of thin films integrated on silicon. By systematically investigating Mn-doped K1-xNaxNbO3 films grown on 8-inch wafers, we demonstrate that the optimal stoichiometry for thin films fundamentally diverges from the bulk equimolar standard. A Na-rich composition (> 70 at.%) is required to overcome substrate-induced constraints, effectively suppressing pyrochlore formation and chemical phase segregation while promoting dense columnar growth with a complete (001) out-of-plane polar orientation. Consequently, Na-rich films deliver outstanding functional properties, reaching remanent polarizations up to 14 uC cm-2, with piezoelectric coefficients of d33f= 79 pm/V and e31f = 10 C/m2. Supported by Density Functional Theory simulations, we correlate this enhancement with improved stability and a strain-driven structural reorientation toward a lower-symmetry monoclinic phase with tilted polarization. By redefining the phase engineering rules for wafer-scale thin films, our results establish a clear route toward KNN integration in microsystems.

### [107] [Resolving room temperature microscale fracture and plasticity of iron oxides along the cascade of iron ore reduction via nanoindentation and microcantilever bending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06001)
*Shreehard Sahu,James P. Best,Gerhard Dehm,Anwesha Kanjilal*

Method: 采用纳米压痕（nanoindentation）和微悬臂梁断裂测试（micro-cantilever fracture testing）对单晶赤铁矿（hematite）、磁铁矿（magnetite）和方铁矿（Wustite）进行室温塑性（plasticity）与断裂行为研究；断裂韧性（fracture toughness）测量使用带缺口微悬臂梁（notched microcantilevers），分别沿低指数晶面（low index）和高指数晶面（high index）取向进行测试。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了氧化铁相全面的力学性能数据集，可应用于材料模型（material models），以预测氢基直接还原（hydrogen-based direct reduction）过程中的断裂与磨损行为。

Abstract: Understanding the fundamental mechanical behaviour of iron oxide phases is essential for controlling attrition and fracture during iron ore reduction process, particularly in hydrogen-based direct reduction systems. Hematite exhibited the highest hardness, H and elastic modulus, E (H=18.5 GPa, E=281 GPa), followed by magnetite (H=8.7 GPa, E=165 GPa) and Wustite (H=7.5 GPa, E=145 GPa), reflecting differences in slip activity along the iron oxide reduction sequence. Furthermore, fracture toughness was measured using notched microcantilevers for all three iron oxide phases, aligned along low index and high index crystallographic planes, respectively. For the low index-oriented case hematite showed increased fracture toughness owing to crack deviation and faceting while magnetite and Wustite exhibited single plane cleavage fracture. Distinct changes in the deformation behavior in terms of plasticity and cracking of the three iron oxides were evident from both methods. Further investigation of a magnetite-gangue interface, particularly relevant to low-concentration ores, revealed significantly reduced fracture toughness compared to the magnetite phase. Overall, these results provide a comprehensive set of mechanical properties of iron oxides with potential application in material models for predicting fracture and attrition during hydrogen-based direct reduction.

Abstract: Long-lived dark excitons in monolayer WSe2 present promising candidates for carrying spin and valley information, but their optical access and spin manipulation have conventionally required the use of strong external magnetic fields. Abstract: We investigate the structural, electronic, and magnetic properties of bilayer Janus 1T-MnSSe using first-principles calculations. ### [110] [Endowing variational phase-field fracture models with custom strength criteria](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06169)

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在广义标准材料（generalized standard materials）变分框架下，通过让耗散势（dissipation potential）依赖于材料当前状态，将任意弹性域（elastic domain）纳入相场断裂模型（phase-field fracture models）的新策略，从而在保持问题变分结构的同时，使弹性退化与强度准则成为两个独立可控的方面。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该方法让耗散势依赖于材料的当前状态，在广义标准材料的变分框架内运作。弹性退化（elastic degradation）与强度准则（strength criterion）被设计为两个独立且可控的方面，从而在不牺牲变分结构的前提下，将任意弹性域纳入相场断裂模型。

Result: 通过简单且具有代表性的模型进行了详细讨论，验证了该方法的有效性。展示了在应变空间与应力空间中弹性域的演化过程。数值模拟揭示了在多种多轴加载条件下、针对不同解析强度曲面（analytical strength surfaces）的裂纹成核过程。

Abstract: By now, several approaches have been proposed to endow phase-field fracture models with the ability to describe crack nucleation under multiaxial stress states. These include techniques for splitting the free energy, direct modifications of the phase-field driving or resisting forces that sacrifice the variational structure of the problem, and the introduction of additional internal variables, such as plastic strains or other nonlinear strains. In this paper, we propose a fundamentally different strategy for incorporating arbitrary elastic domains into phase-field fracture models, formulated within the variational framework of generalized standard materials. The proposed approach relies on letting the dissipation potential depend on the current state of the material. In this way, the variational structure of the problem is preserved, while elastic degradation and the strength criterion remain two distinct and independently controllable aspects of the material response. Simple yet representative models are presented and thoroughly discussed to demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed methodology. The resulting evolution of the elastic domain is investigated in both strain and stress spaces. Moreover, numerical simulations demonstrate a range of crack nucleation processes under multiaxial loading conditions for various analytical strength surfaces. This work paves the way for future developments and applications in several directions.

### [112] [PolyGraphPy: A unified Python framework for atomistic simulation and machine learning-driven polymer design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06415)
*João G. C. S. Duarte,Shruti Venkatram,Morgan Cencer,Traian Dumitricǎ,Ketson R. M. dos Santos*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: PolyGraphPy是一个开源Python框架，通过整合原子模拟（atomistic simulations）与机器学习（machine learning），实现聚合物的高效性能预测和导向设计，包含自动化密度泛函紧束缚（DFTB）计算、贝叶斯图神经网络（Bayesian GNN）以及两种生成模型（SELFIES-GPT和遗传算法），在丙烯酸酯数据集上展现了降低计算成本、加速数据驱动聚合物信息学的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物（polymers）因其可定制的化学组成和结构而应用广泛，但其设计空间极为庞大，受单体类别、共聚物构型（copolymer configurations）、链长、化学计量比及材料性能等多种因素共同制约。传统探索方法效率低下，亟需高效的计算方法来推动聚合物科学中的数据驱动研究。

Method: PolyGraphPy集成了三个核心模块：1）自动化的密度泛函紧束缚（Density Functional Tight Binding, DFTB）计算，用于构建单体、均聚物和交替共聚物的结构化数据集；2）基于贝叶斯图神经网络（Bayesian Graph Neural Networks, Bayesian GNNs）的性能预测模型，利用随机图表示（stochastic graph representations）预测目标性能（如静态极化率）并提供不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification）；3）两种互补的从头设计生成模型：基于SELFIES的生成式预训练变换器（SELFIES-based Generative Pretrained Transformer, GPT）和基于BRICS图碎片化的遗传算法（Genetic Algorithm, GA）。

Result: 在丙烯酸酯（acrylates）数据集上的实验表明，PolyGraphPy提供了一个高度可定制的端到端流水线（end-to-end pipeline），显著降低了计算成本，并加速了数据驱动的聚合物信息学（data-driven polymer informatics）流程。

Conclusion: PolyGraphPy作为开源工具，通过结合原子模拟与机器学习，为聚合物材料的高效性能预测和导向设计提供了可行方案，推动了计算聚合物科学的发展。

Abstract: Polymers are indispensable materials with applications ranging from electronics to medicine owing to their versatility, which can be tailored by adjusting their chemical composition and architecture. The design space for these compounds is vast and governed by factors such as monomer classes, copolymer configurations (e.g., linear, branched, random, and alternating), chain size, stoichiometry, and material properties (e.g., density, refractive index, solubility, and Poisson's ratio). Exploring this space requires efficient computational methodologies for polymer science. To address this challenge, we introduce PolyGraphPy, an open-source Python framework that integrates atomistic simulations with machine learning for accurate property prediction and property-guided polymer design. The framework automates Density Functional Tight Binding calculations to efficiently construct structured datasets for monomers, homopolymers, and alternating copolymers. For property prediction, PolyGraphPy employs Bayesian Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) with stochastic graph representations to predict target properties, such as static polarizability, while providing robust uncertainty quantification. Furthermore, the platform incorporates two complementary generative models for the de novo design of targeted molecules: a SELFIES-based Generative Pretrained Transformer (GPT) and a Genetic Algorithm (GA) based on BRICS graph fragmentation. Demonstrated on a dataset of acrylates, PolyGraphPy provides a highly customizable end-to-end pipeline that reduces computational costs and accelerates data-driven polymer informatics.

</details>

Abstract: A recent non-perturbative formulation of $2n$ dimensional chiral gauge theories relies on realizing chiral fermions on the $2n$ dimensional boundary of a $2n+1$ dimensional disk manifold. It also requires extending boundary gauge configurations into the interior of the disk using some flow prescription that preserves 2n dimensional gauge invariance. ### [114] [Gauge field flow for chiral gauge theories on a slab](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05306)
*Jinlong Dang,Rohith Karur,Srimoyee Sen*

TL;DR: 本文在格点规范理论中实现了基于畴壁费米子（domain wall fermions）和梯度流（gradient flow）的手征规范理论（chiral gauge theories）构造方案，并提出了新的EOM流（equation of motion flow）方法，通过数值验证了格点上流守恒（current conservation）与反常流入（anomaly inflow）机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手征规范理论在格点上的构建是一个长期难题。本文旨在在格点（lattice）上数值实现一种已有的理论方案：利用$2n+1$维欧氏空间中的畴壁费米子，结合梯度流将规范场（gauge fields）延拓到额外维度，从而解除反畴壁（anti-wall）上的镜像费米子（mirror fermions）耦合。

Method: 针对$n=1$（即$2+1$维）情形，在存在$2n$维背景规范场（background gauge fields）的条件下，实现了畴壁费米子方案。此外，提出并实现了一种新的规范场流方案（EOM flow），其中规范场在远离畴壁处满足$2n+1$维运动方程。两种方案均将规范场与费米子耦合，并在格点上检验流守恒与反常流入。

Result: 在格点数值实现中，两种方案（梯度流与EOM流）均成功耦合了规范场与费米子，并演示了流守恒与反常流入如何在格点上成立。

Conclusion: 本文通过具体数值实现验证了基于畴壁费米子和梯度流构造手征规范理论的可行性，并提出了EOM流作为替代方案。这为格点规范理论中处理手征费米子（chiral fermions）和反常（anomalies）提供了新的数值工具。

Abstract: The proposal to formulate chiral gauge theories using domain wall fermions on $2n+1$ dimensional Euclidean lattice with a slab geometry involves $2n$ dimensional dynamical gauge fields residing on one of the domain walls. The gauge fields are extended into the extra dimension using gradient flow decoupling the mirror fermions on the anti-wall. We implement this construction on the lattice for $n=1$ in the presence of $2n$ dimensional background gauge fields. We also formulate and implement an additional gauge field flow proposal, where the gauge fields satisfy $2n+1$ dimensional equation of motion away from the domain wall, known as the EOM (equation of motion) flow. In both cases, we couple the gauge fields to fermions and demonstrate how current conservation and anomaly inflow work on the lattice.

### [115] [Methods for Inferring Interaction Potentials from Cross-Linking Mass Spectrometry Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05541)
*Börries von Seggern,Mohsen Sadeghi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个从交联质谱（XL-MS）数据中参数化粗粒化相互作用势的框架，通过建立与逆Henderson问题的联系并改进多种优化算法，在均匀流体和三相分离系统中均实现了高精度参数反演，为将XL-MS实验数据转化为粗粒化蛋白质模型提供了系统路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交联质谱（cross-linking mass spectrometry, XL-MS）是探测蛋白质内部结构和蛋白质-蛋白质相互作用的有力定量技术，但缺乏系统方法将这类数据适配到粗粒化相互作用粒子模型（coarse-grained interacting particle models）中。现有方法直接拟合径向分布函数（radial distribution functions, RDFs），但许多可观测量（如配位数）作为RDF的泛函（functional）无法被唯一反演。

Method: 建立了该问题与逆Henderson问题（inverse Henderson problem）之间的联系，并适配了迭代玻尔兹曼反演（Iterative Boltzmann Inversion）和迭代蒙特卡洛（Iterative Monte Carlo）等算法进行数值求解。推导了精确梯度和低密度极限梯度近似，提出了两种基于预测-校正框架（predictor-corrector framework）的新算法。在生物现实的十组分测试系统上评估了多种优化算法。

Result: 在均匀流体中，所有方法均实现了出色的效率和精度。在具有挑战性的三相系统（three-phase system）中，Adam、采用低密度导数的梯度下降法以及使用精确梯度的牛顿法（Newton's method）均能可靠地恢复正确参数。

Conclusion: 这些结果为从XL-MS实验到粗粒化蛋白质模型建立了清晰路径，尤其适用于相分离（phase separation）调控生物学功能的系统，有望推动生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）和蛋白质聚集（protein aggregation）的新研究。

Abstract: Cross-linking mass spectrometry (XL-MS) has emerged as a powerful quantitative technique for probing intra-protein structural information as well as protein-protein interactions at an unprecedented scale. XL-MS data yield information on the pairwise spatial proximity of proteins through inter-molecular linkers. However, systematic methods for adapting such data for coarse-grained interacting particle models remain limited. Predominant focus is put on directly fitting radial distribution functions (RDFs), while numerous observables, e.g. coordination numbers, which are functionals of the RDF, cannot be uniquely inverted. In this work, we develop a framework for parameterizing interaction potentials from such observables in potentially phase-separated mixtures, as encountered in XL-MS results. We establish a connection between this problem and the inverse Henderson problem and adapt algorithms such as Iterative Boltzmann Inversion and Iterative Monte Carlo to its numerical solution. We derive exact and low-density limit gradient approximations and propose two new algorithms based on an adaptation of the predictor-corrector~framework. In total, we evaluate several optimization algorithms on biologically realistic ten-component test systems. We demonstrate that for homogeneous fluids, all methods achieve exceptional efficiency and accuracy. Critically, we further demonstrate successful parametrization in a challenging three-phase system. Here, three algorithms, namely Adam and gradient descent employing the low-density derivative as well as Newton's method with the exact gradient, reliably recover the correct parameters. These results establish a clear pathway from XL-MS experiments to coarse-grained protein models for systems where phase separation governs biological function, potentially enabling new investigations of biomolecular condensates and protein aggregation.
