### [116] [Nambu Nonequilibrium Thermodynamics and the Lyapunov Structure of Open Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05231)
*So Katagiri*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过一个开放活塞模型（open-piston model），证明了在开放非平衡系统中，子系统热力学熵并非李雅普诺夫函数（Lyapunov function），而是引入了一个新的耗散势 $S_{NB}$，该量在可逆Nambu流（Nambu flow）下守恒，且不可逆动力学可表达为由其生成的正半定梯度流（positive-semidefinite gradient flow），从而为不可逆弛豫提供了单调递增的动力学量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放非平衡系统中，子系统热力学熵在弛豫过程中可能暂时下降，不满足李雅普诺夫函数条件，因此需要寻找一个能够组织不可逆弛豫（irreversible relaxation）的恰当热力学量。

Method: 构建了一个同时与压力库（pressure reservoir）和热库（heat bath）耦合的显式开放活塞模型；可逆部分由扩展能量和子系统熵生成的Nambu旋转流（Nambu rotational flow）描述，不可逆部分由耗散势 $S_{NB}$ 生成的梯度流（gradient flow）描述。

Result: 在绝热可逆极限下，Nambu括号产生守恒曲面交线上的振荡活塞运动；耦合热库并加入摩擦后，子系统熵 $S$ 呈现非单调振荡，而 $S_{NB}=S-H_{1}/T_{b}$ 在所提出的正半定耗散结构下单调递增。

Conclusion: $S_{NB}$ 的单调性并非源于将其等同于热力学熵，而是源于两个几何条件：可逆Nambu流保持 $S_{NB}$ 守恒，且不可逆动力学可写为由 $S_{NB}$ 生成的正半定梯度流。该模型提供了一个最小宏观实现，能清晰分离热力学熵、耗散势、可逆时间序与不可逆弛豫。

Abstract: In open nonequilibrium systems, the thermodynamic entropy of a subsystem is not generally a Lyapunov function. Even during relaxation toward equilibrium, it may decrease temporarily because of exchanges with external reservoirs. This raises a basic question: what thermodynamic quantity, if any, organizes irreversible relaxation in an open system?
  We address this question using an explicit open-piston model coupled to both a pressure reservoir and a heat bath. The reversible sector is formulated as a Nambu rotational flow generated by the extended energy and the subsystem entropy, while the irreversible sector is written as a gradient flow generated by a dissipation potential $S_{NB}$. In the adiabatic reversible limit, the Nambu bracket produces the oscillatory piston motion on the intersection of conserved level surfaces. After coupling to a heat bath and adding friction, the subsystem entropy $S$ can exhibit nonmonotonic oscillations, whereas $S_{NB}=S-H_{1}/T_{b}$ increases monotonically under the proposed positive-semidefinite dissipative structure.
  We show that this monotonicity is not a consequence of identifying $S_{NB}$ with thermodynamic entropy. Rather, it follows from two geometric conditions: the reversible Nambu flow preserves $S_{NB}$, and the irreversible dynamics can be written as a positive-semidefinite gradient flow generated by $S_{NB}$. The open-piston model therefore provides a minimal macroscopic realization in which thermodynamic entropy, dissipation potential, reversible temporal order, and irreversible relaxation can be separated explicitly.

</details>


### [117] [Opinion dynamics on social proximity disordered networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05349)
*Fellipe Aranha,Giuliano G. Porciúncula,Adauto J. F. de Souza,Paulo R. A. Campos,André L. M. Vilela*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究探讨基于空间邻近性的 Gabriel 图网络对舆论动力学的影响，发现该模型表现出与二维伊辛普适类相容的二阶相变，表明空间约束的平面交互拓扑在临界动力学分析中保留了空间的维度性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解局部社会压力如何塑造集体意见形成在社会学、政治学、金融学和科技领域具有重要意义，而复杂网络是研究这一过程的有力框架。然而，当前主流网络模型（如随机、无标度和小世界网络）忽略了欧几里得几何近邻性和连续交互的作用，因此有必要探索基于空间嵌入的邻近交互网络（如 Gabriel 图）对舆论动力学的影响。

Method: 采用 Gabriel 图作为空间嵌入网络，通过几何无序参数（geometric disorder parameter）随机扰动智能体坐标，实现从正方形晶格到空间随机网络的过渡。舆论动力学通过社会压力运作，并引入非从众性（nonconformity）水平来影响意见分歧。通过磁化强度（magnetization）、磁化率（susceptibility）和 Binder 四阶累积量（Binder's fourth-order cumulant）分析全局社会共识的形成与瓦解，并使用体积缩放（volumetric scaling）方法提供适用于规则和异质交互拓扑的临界性参考框架。

Result: 模型表现出二阶相变（second-order phase transitions），其行为依赖于几何无序和非从众性水平。标准临界指数（critical exponents）与二维伊辛普适类（two-dimensional Ising universality class）兼容。

Conclusion: 空间约束的、平面的且全局连接的交互拓扑在临界动力学分析中保留了空间的维度性。

Abstract: Understanding how local social pressure shapes collective opinion formation is essential in modern society, with implications in sociology, politics, finance, and technology. Complex networks are a powerful framework for investigating these processes and for representing social interactions in emergent phenomena, and canonical models such as random, scale-free, and small-world networks remain most relevant when Euclidean geometric proximity and contiguous interactions are not the dominant organizing factors. Our investigation explores the effects of Gabriel graphs, a spatially embedded network that utilizes proximity-based interactions, on social opinion dynamics. Using a geometric disorder parameter that randomly displaces agent coordinates, we transition from square lattices of social interactions to spatial random networks that preserve local constraints while introducing strong topological heterogeneity. Opinion dynamics operate through social pressure, with a level of nonconformity that affects dissent among opinions. We analyze magnetization, susceptibility, and Binder's fourth-order cumulant to characterize the emergence and breakdown of global social consensus. The model exhibits second-order phase transitions whose behavior depends on both geometric disorder and nonconformity levels. We use volumetric scaling and provide a reference frame appropriate for characterizing criticality in regular and heterogeneous interaction topologies. We find that the standard critical exponents remain compatible with the two-dimensional Ising universality class. Furthermore, the results suggest that spatially constrained, planar, and globally connected interaction topologies preserve the dimensionality of space in critical dynamics analysis.

</details>


### [118] [Dissipation-coherence tradeoff for stochastic oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05498)
*Jie Gu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了一个针对自主噪声振荡中每周期熵产生（entropy production per oscillation period）的更弱但严格的下界，该下界保留了Oberreiter-Barato-Seifert (OBS)猜想的结构，但引入了一个模态均匀性因子（mode-uniformity factor），并证明当主导振荡模（dominant oscillatory mode）局域化时，仅基于特征值的预因子会失效。论文还给出了从低维数据估算该因子的路线，并在平移不变马尔可夫跳过程（translation-invariant Markov jump processes）中退化为OBS形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Oberreiter、Barato和Seifert提出了一个引人注目的猜想，认为在生化与介观系统的自主噪声振荡中，每个振荡周期的熵产生存在一个以最慢振荡模态的相干数（coherence number）为下界的普适下限。该猜想的严格性及其适用范围需要进一步验证和扩展。

Method: 通过引入一个在稳态内积（steady-state inner product）下衡量振荡本征模（oscillatory eigenmode）在状态间分布均匀程度的模态均匀性因子（mode-uniformity factor），推导出一个保留OBS结构但更弱且严格的熵产生下界。并给出了在单模态主导（single-mode dominance）和测量信息充分条件下从低维数据估算该因子的证明性路线。

Result: 明确指出了仅基于特征值的预因子在主导振荡模局域化时可能失效。在圆环上的平移不变马尔可夫跳过程中，对称性保护使得模态均匀性因子η=1，因此精细化的下界退化为OBS形式。圆上的漂移-扩散极限（drift--diffusion limit）可以饱和该下界。

Conclusion: 该工作严格化了OBS猜想，揭示了其特征值仅依赖形式的局限性，并通过模态均匀性因子给出了更精确的约束。同时提供了从低维数据估算该因子的可行路径，为实验验证提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Autonomous noisy oscillations in biochemical and mesoscopic systems require nonequilibrium driving and therefore dissipation. A striking conjecture by Oberreiter, Barato, and Seifert (OBS) proposes a universal lower bound on the entropy produced per oscillation period in terms of the coherence number of the slowest oscillatory mode. Here we derive a weaker but rigorous lower bound that preserves the OBS structure while introducing a mode-uniformity factor that quantifies how evenly the oscillatory eigenmode is distributed across states in the steady-state inner product. The result makes explicit that an eigenvalue-only prefactor can fail when the dominant oscillatory mode is localized. We also outline a proof-of-principle route for estimating this factor from low-dimensional data under single-mode dominance and sufficiently informative measurements, and derive an eigenvector-free corollary using only the smallest stationary probability. Translation-invariant Markov jump processes on a ring provide a symmetry-protected class with $η=1$, so the refinement reduces to the OBS form; the drift--diffusion limit on a circle saturates the bound.

</details>


### [119] [Polylogarithmic Structure of Bragg Diffraction in Finite-Coherence Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05886)
*Evangelos G. Filothodoros*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 提出一种基于加权多平面干涉模型的对数（polylogarithmic）结构，用于描述布拉格衍射（Bragg diffraction），将散射振幅表示为多对数生成函数，并建立了衍射理论与复分析（complex analysis）之间的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统衍射模型在处理无序或部分相干（partially coherent）材料时，通常需要额外的唯象展宽假设（phenomenological broadening assumptions），缺乏一个能够统一描述峰位、峰宽和线形的紧凑解析框架。

Method: 基于加权多平面干涉模型（weighted multi-plane interference model）构建多对数结构，散射振幅表达为多对数生成函数 $F(θ) = \mathrm{Li}_m\left(e^{iθ_{\mathrm{eff}} - ε}\right)$，其中 $ε$ 为有限相干长度（finite coherence length）。经典布拉格条件对应于多对数自变量趋近其分支点（branch point）$z=1$ 的极限情形。

Result: 该模型能够恢复理想晶体（ideal crystals）的标准布拉格定律（Bragg law），同时捕获有限相干长度、无序（disorder）和非均匀晶格相干性（non-uniform lattice coherence）导致的衍射偏离。布拉格峰对应多对数的边界奇点（boundary singularities）。

Conclusion: 提出了一个紧凑的解析框架，建立了衍射理论与复分析之间的联系，对于传统模型需要额外唯象假设的无序或部分相干材料可能尤为适用。

Abstract: We develop a polylogarithmic structure for Bragg diffraction based on a weighted multi-plane interference model. Within this kind of construction, the scattering amplitude is expressed as a polylogarithmic generating function. By introducing extra contributions with power-law and the usual exponential decay, it takes the form $F(θ) = \mathrm{Li}_m\left(e^{iθ_{\mathrm{eff}} - ε}\right)$, where $ε$ is a finite coherence length. In the limit where $ε\rightarrow 0$, the argument of the polylogarithm approaches the unit circle and the classical Bragg condition corresponds to the approach of the polylogarithm argument toward its branch point $z=1$. This formulation provides a compact analytical framework for describing diffraction line shapes within a generalized correlation model in which peak positions, widths, and line shapes arise from a single analytic structure. Although we are able to recover the standard Bragg law for ideal crystals, the polylogarithm model captures deviations due to finite correlation length, disorder and non-uniform lattice coherence. We show that if Bragg peaks correspond to boundary singularities of the polylogarithm, a connection between diffraction theory and complex analysis arise. The proposed theoretical model may be particularly relevant for disordered or partially coherent materials, where conventional diffraction models often require additional phenomenological broadening assumptions.

</details>


### [120] [A granular Büttiker-Landauer motor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05913)
*Olivier Devauchelle,Predrag Popović,Piotr Szymczak,Anaïs Abramian,Arnaud Lazarus*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过宏观实验系统首次实现了Büttiker和Landauer的理论预测：在非均匀温度场中，粒子会聚集在低温区域；在存在势能力（potential force）且温度不均匀时，仅靠噪声即可驱动稳态粒子流。实验验证了这些现象违背经典菲克定律（Fick's law），并与理论定量预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统扩散理论（菲克定律）预言随机游走者（random walker）会沿浓度梯度向下扩散并趋于均匀分布，但在某些实验（如振动弹性板上的Chladni图形）中观察到粒子在弱涨落区域聚集，这与菲克定律相矛盾。Büttiker和Landauer曾从理论上提出非均匀温度场可导致粒子低温聚集及噪声驱动的稳态电流，但缺乏实验验证。

Method: 采用宏观实验系统模拟非均匀温度场中的粒子行为，实验设计参照Büttiker的理论框架，以可观测的宏观系统复现其理论预测的两种现象：温度梯度下的粒子聚集，以及势能力与非均匀温度耦合下的噪声驱动稳态电流。

Result: 实验成功观察到粒子在低温区域聚集的现象，并证实了在非均匀温度场与势能力共同作用下，仅依靠噪声即可驱动稳态电流。实验结果与Büttiker的定量预测吻合。

Conclusion: 该宏观实验为Büttiker和Landauer关于非均匀温度场中反常扩散行为（anomalous diffusion behavior）的理论提供了首次实验验证，表明噪声在适当条件下可充当驱动力而非仅仅导致无序，拓展了对非平衡统计力学（non-equilibrium statistical mechanics）中输运现象的理解。

Abstract: Random walkers usually diffuse according to Fick's law. On average, they move down the gradient of their concentration and, in the absence of external force, tend to distribute themselves uniformly. In some experiments, however, this familiar notion is at odds with observation. Sand grains, for instance, gather along the nodal lines of a vibrated elastic plate to form a Chladni figure, thus accumulating where fluctuations are weak -- a fact that escapes the reach of Fick's law. On theoretical grounds, Büttiker [Zeitschrift für Physik B, 68, 1987] and Landauer [J Stat Phys, 53, 1988] proposed that particles submitted to a non-uniform temperature field would indeed gather where the temperature is low. They also predicted that, in the presence of a potential force, a non-uniform temperature could drive a steady current of particles, powered only by noise. Here, we present an experimental realization of these phenomena in a macroscopic system, which confirms the quantitative predictions of Büttiker.

</details>


### [121] [Thermodynamics of bouncing grains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05930)
*Olivier Devauchelle,Predrag Popović,Piotr Szymczak,Anaïs Abramian,Arnaud Lazarus*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 通过实验研究非共振振动平板上沙粒的扩散行为，发现其与经典分子扩散类似，可定义温度并满足涨落-耗散定理和麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼统计；但在温度梯度下，扩散不再服从菲克定律，实验支持一种新的输运关系，并提出了相应热通量表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非共振振动平板上颗粒扩散的物理机制，尤其是其与经典分子扩散的异同，以及非均匀温度场下微观动力学对宏观行为的修正作用。

Method: 采用异质的非共振平板进行实验，观察振动沙粒的扩散行为，并与经典分子扩散理论（如涨落-耗散定理、麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼统计）进行对比；在温度非均匀条件下检验菲克定律（Fick's law）的适用性及一种新提出的输运关系。

Result: 在均匀温度下，振动颗粒的扩散与经典分子扩散一致，可定义温度并服从涨落-耗散定理（fluctuation-dissipation theorem）和麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼统计（Maxwell-Boltzmann statistics）；但当温度在平板上变化时，菲克定律失效，实验支持一种新的输运关系；基于该关系进一步推导了非平衡稳态下的热通量表达式并得到实验验证。

Conclusion: 振动颗粒体系在均匀温度下与经典热力学框架兼容，但在非均匀温度下表现出偏离经典扩散定律的微观效应；新输运关系及相应的热通量表达式可较好地描述Chladni实验中的扩散现象。

Abstract: When a horizontal plate vibrates strongly enough, it causes small particles such as sand grains to continually bounce on it and, over time, to diffuse across its surface. This phenomenon is the cause of the well-known Chladni figure, which is drawn by a higher density of grains gathering along the nodal lines of a resonating elastic plate. Using a heterogeneous, non-resonating plate, we investigate experimentally this type of diffusion. We find that, for the most part, is it comparable to classical molecular diffusion. We can define a temperature for the bouncing grains, and the system then obeys the fluctuation-dissipation theorem. We also recover Maxwell-Boltzmann statistics at equilibrium, when temperature is uniform. However, when temperature varies across the vibrating plate, the microscopic details of the grains' dynamics affect their macroscopic behavior: Fick's law, for instance, no longer applies. Instead, our experiments support a new transport relation that was recently proposed to represent diffusion in Chladni's experiment. Finally, we propose an expression for the heat flux associated to the non-equilibrium steady state predicted by this new relation, and test it against observations.

</details>


### [122] [Hidden periodicities allow the prediction of locked particle motions on quasicrystalline surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06026)
*Seemant Mishra,Artem Ryabov,Philipp Maass*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了准晶表面（quasicrystalline surface）上粒子在时间周期驱动力（time-periodic forcing）下的运动，发现粒子轨迹虽非周期，但其平均方向和速度由隐藏的周期势（hidden periodic potentials）决定，并表现出方向锁定（directional locking）和速度锁定（speed locking）现象，且运动不与驱动力同步化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准晶表面因具有长程有序（long-range order）但缺乏平移周期性（translational periodicity），其上的粒子运动呈现奇特特征，尤其在时间周期驱动力下，运动方向可能偏离平均驱动方向。这促使研究者探索准晶势中粒子运动的锁定机制及其背后的物理规律。

Method: 研究采用由平面波叠加生成的具有准晶最小点（minima）图案的表面势模型，分析粒子在该势场中受时间周期力驱动下的运动轨迹、平均方向和速度，并揭示隐藏的周期势在其中的决定作用。

Result: 粒子在准晶表面势中的轨迹是非周期的；平均方向和速度由隐藏的周期势的晶格向量（lattice vectors）决定；方向锁定和速度锁定由这些晶格向量定义的特征速度（characteristic velocities）决定；粒子运动不与驱动力同步化，且即使在方向锁定状态下，平均速度也可能保持非锁定状态。

Conclusion: 准晶表面上的粒子运动虽然非周期，但可通过隐藏的周期势理解其平均行为。这些发现通过一个可直接用于实验实现的模型得到验证，为准晶体系中的输运现象提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Motion of particles across quasicrystalline surfaces exhibits peculiar features due to the presence of long-range order without translational periodicity. Under time-periodic forcing, this motion can become locked in directions thatn deviate strongly from the mean driving direction. We show that for surface potentials with a quasicrystalline pattern of minima generated by a superposition of plane waves, particle trajectories are nonperiodic, yet their mean direction and speed are determined by hidden periodic potentials. The lattice vectors of these underlying potentials define characteristic velocities that dictate both directional and speed locking. The particle motion does not synchronize with the driving, and it is possible for the mean speed to remain nonlocked even in directionally locked states. These findings are demonstrated using a model directly amenable to experimental realization.

</details>

Motivation: 该研究有两个目标：一是揭示液体二元模型中固体状分子聚集与晶格激发的相互作用能够表征常态液体宏观行为与其介观物理过程之间的联系；二是在介观尺度上通过二元性识别时间方向。

Method: 论文基于液体的二元模型（Dual Model of Liquids），分析固体状分子团簇与晶格激发（即弹性能量量子）之间的相互作用。该方法将宏观行为与介观过程联系起来，并考察该相互作用在时间相关及耗散过程中的方向性。

Conclusion: 液体的二元模型能够有效桥接宏观与介观尺度，并在介观尺度上识别出时间箭头，为理解液体中的时间相关和耗散过程提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: This manuscripts has two goals. The first goal is to show that the interaction in the Dual Model of Liquids between the solidlike molecule aggregates and the lattice excitations is appropriate to represent the link between the behaviour at macroscopic scale of normal liquids and the physical processes characterizing those systems at mesoscopic scale. The second goal is to show that the duality allows identifying a time arrow on the mesoscopic scale in liquids. The interaction of quanta of elastic energy with the molecular clusters introduces a privileged direction, which is relevant in time dependent and dissipative macroscopic processes, although the interaction remains temporally reversible

</details>


### [124] [A closed system setting for quantum thermalisation in free fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06362)
*Purvaash Panduranghan-Udhayashankar,Filiberto Ares,Pasquale Calabrese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究在封闭量子系统中模拟边界耦合热浴的温度淬火过程，以自由费米子模型（XX链和横场Ising链）为例，利用广义流体动力学（generalised hydrodynamics）解析计算了Frobenius距离，完整刻画了热化过程，并发现该设定下不存在Mpemba效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在封闭量子系统中模拟系统与边界耦合热浴相互作用的场景，研究热化（thermalisation）及Mpemba效应（Mpemba effect）是否可能出现，以理解非平衡量子弛豫的基本机制。

Method: 采用三分量几何结构：有限链初始处于有限温度，两侧突然连接两个同质半无限链，后者处于不同温度作为热浴；全系统在均匀哈密顿量下幺正演化。利用自由费米子模型的Gaussian动力学性质，将Frobenius距离精确表示为两点关联函数，并结合广义流体动力学在流体动力学极限下导出解析预测。

Result: 在XX链（保持U(1)粒子数对称性）和横场Ising链（破坏该对称性）两种模型中，均未观察到Mpemba效应；Frobenius距离在流体动力学极限下得到完整解析刻画。

Conclusion: 该边界驱动热化协议（boundary-driven thermalisation protocol）中的弛豫过程可被完全解析表征，且不存在反常的加速平衡现象；识别了一类可完全解析分析且无Mpemba效应的热化方案。

Abstract: We study thermalisation and the possible occurrence of the Mpemba effect in a closed quantum setting that mimics the interaction of a system with thermal reservoirs coupled only at its boundaries. Specifically, we consider a tripartite geometry in which a finite chain, initially prepared at a finite temperature, is suddenly connected on both sides to two semi-infinite chains of the same nature held at a different temperature. These outer chains act as thermal baths, while the full system evolves unitarily under a homogeneous Hamiltonian. This setup provides a simple quantum realisation of a temperature quench and closely resembles the original scenario in which the classical Mpemba effect was first observed. We focus on two paradigmatic free-fermion models, the XX chain and the transverse-field Ising chain, which respectively preserve and break the global $U(1)$ particle-number symmetry. As a probe of relaxation, we consider the Frobenius distance between the time-evolved reduced density matrix of the central subsystem and its stationary state, which is the thermal state at the bath temperature. Exploiting the free-fermionic structure of both models, the dynamics remains Gaussian and the Frobenius distance can be expressed exactly in terms of two-point correlation functions. Combining this representation with generalised hydrodynamics, we derive analytical predictions for the Frobenius distance in the hydrodynamic limit, providing a complete characterisation of the thermalisation process. Using these results, we investigate the possible occurrence of the Mpemba effect. We find that, despite the genuine non-equilibrium dynamics displayed by the system, no Mpemba effect arises in this setting. Our analysis identifies a broad class of boundary-driven thermalisation protocols in which relaxation is fully characterised analytically and exhibits no anomalous acceleration of equilibration.

</details>

### [125] [Equivariant Quantum Cohomology of Grassmannians via the Clifford algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06352)
*Christian Korff,Mikhail Vasilev*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文构造了格拉斯曼流形（Grassmannians）的显式等变量子Satake映射，将其环面等变量子上同调（torus-equivariant quantum cohomology）表示为射影空间（projective space）的上同调，并利用由此产生的Clifford代数结构，通过Wick定理导出了等变Gromov-Witten不变量（equivariant Gromov-Witten invariants）的新递推关系，从而给出了组合证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格拉斯曼流形的等变量子上同调计算复杂，现有的方法尚缺乏系统且高效的代数结构来统一处理其递推关系与组合性质。

Method: 构造显式的等变量子Satake映射（equivariant quantum Satake map），将格拉斯曼流形的上同调约化到射影空间；利用射影空间上同调的外代数与Clifford代数的典范等同，从几何（push-pull映射）和代数（shuffle积）两种视角描述该作用。

Result: 基于Clifford代数结构，利用Wick定理导出了等变Gromov-Witten不变量的一组新递推关系；为等变量子Pieri规则（equivariant quantum Pieri rules）提供了组合证明，并将部分结果推广到了量子三重Schubert演算（quantum triple Schubert calculus）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的Clifford代数框架为格拉斯曼流形的等变量子上同调计算提供了统一且高效的代数方法，并展示了其在组合Schubert演算中的广泛应用潜力。

Abstract: We construct an explicit equivariant quantum Satake map for Grassmannians, which enables us to express their torus-equivariant quantum cohomology in terms of that of projective space. We then consider the exterior algebra of the latter, which admits a canonical identification with a Clifford algebra. We describe the resulting action in several complementary ways: first, from a geometric perspective via push-pull maps, and second, in terms of the shuffle product, which also arises in the simplest cohomological Hall algebra associated with the $A_1$-quiver. Exploiting the Clifford algebra structure, we derive new recurrence relations among equivariant Gromov-Witten invariants, yielding a new method for their computation in terms of Wick's Theorem. As an application, we provide combinatorial proofs of Graham positivity for both equivariant quantum Pieri rules, and in one case extend these results to quantum triple Schubert calculus.

</details>

### [126] [Detectability of secondary images from flares near Sgr A* with mock GRAVITY data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06134)
*Fengting Xie,Qing-Hua Zhu,Xin Li*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟GRAVITY观测数据，研究围绕Sgr A*轨道耀斑的二次像是否可探测。贝叶斯模型拟合表明，仅靠增大样本量不足以区分二次像信号；只有同时将样本量提升一个数量级并将天体测量不确定性降低至当前的40%，才能实现稳健探测（|ΔBIC| > 7.9）。二次像的探测是迈向探测高阶像和光子环的关键第一步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRAVITY合作组观测到的近红外耀斑轨道运动编码了吸积物质动力学与背景时空几何的信息。耀斑质心轨迹包含主像（primary image）、二次像（secondary image）及高阶像（higher-order image）的贡献，可能揭示时空几何的独特特征。本研究旨在评估这些尚未分辨的二次像信号是否能够在未来GRAVITY观测中从统计上被区分和探测。

Method: 通过模拟数据（mock data）仿照未来GRAVITY观测，分别构建两种模型：一种仅考虑主像轨迹贡献的质心；另一种则包含主像与二次像的流量加权贡献。采用贝叶斯框架（Bayesian framework）对这两种模型拟合模拟数据，并通过贝叶斯信息准则差值（|ΔBIC|）量化二次像信号在统计上可区分的条件。

Result: 仅将样本量提升一个数量级不足以提供区分二次像的强证据。只有当样本量提高一个数量级且天体测量不确定性（astrometric uncertainties）降低至当前GRAVITY天体测量数据不确定性的40%时，才能实现稳健探测（|ΔBIC| > 7.9）。

Conclusion: 二次像来源于强场区域（strong-field regime）的引力透镜效应（gravitational lensing），与由吸积流物理主导的主像不同。探测二次像是迈向探测高阶像和光子环（photon rings）的关键第一步，其实现依赖于未来观测中样本量与精度的协同提升。

Abstract: The orbital motion of near-infrared flares reported by the GRAVITY collaboration encodes information about both the dynamics of accretion matter and the underlying spacetime geometry. The centroid track of these flares, which corresponds to the flux-weighted center of light, incorporates contributions from primary, secondary and higher-order images. Thus, it potentially indicates distinctive signatures of the spacetime geometry, even when these individual multiple images remain unresolved. In this study, we explore the detectability of the secondary images from flares orbiting Sgr A* through mock data simulating future GRAVITY observations. Specifically, we compare the model in which the centroid coincides with the track of the primary images with another model in which the centroid incorporates flux-weighted contributions from both the primary and secondary images. Fitting these models to the mock data based on Bayesian framework, we quantify the conditions under which the signature of secondary images can be statistically distinguishable. We demonstrate that increasing the sample size by an order of magnitude alone could not yield strong evidence for distinguishing the secondary image. Robust detectability ($|Δ\text{BIC}| >7.9$) is achieved when both with the improved sample size and astrometric uncertainties reduced to 40\% of current uncertainties of GRAVITY astrometric data. Unlike the primary image, which is dominated by accretion flow physics, the secondary images originate from gravitational lensing in the strong-field regime. Their detection is an essential first step toward probing higher-order images and the photon rings.

Conclusion: 若该异常信号被更多数据以更高显著性确认，则需引入新物理；本文模型为此提供了一个可行的候选解释，并给出了若干可在近期接受检验的预言。

Abstract: The CMS collaboration has reported a measurement of $Υ$ decays to ditaus using $61.9~{\rm fb}^{-1}$ of scouting data. If interpreted as the decay of $Υ(1S,2S,3S)$, the measured ditau rate is more than ten times that seen in the dimuon final states at the $\sim 3 σ$ level, and is likewise inconsistent with the branching ratios measured at $B$-factories. If confirmed with more data and at higher significance, such a violation of lepton flavor universality would necessitate new physics. In this Letter, we present a simple model with a light pseudoscalar coincidentally near the $Υ(1S)$ mass, which mixes with two Higgs doublets in the alignment limit. Such a particle naturally decays primarily to taus and evades all existing experimental constraints, while implying a number of predictions that can be tested in the near future.

Motivation: 未来实验（杰斐逊实验室CLAS12/SoLID及电子-离子对撞机EIC的ePIC）即将提供高精度SIDIS双强子数据，评估这些数据对横向性PDFs和张量荷不确定性的约束能力，是当前理论及唯象研究的迫切需求。

Method: 针对质子靶（CLAS12和ePIC）和$^3$He靶（SoLID和ePIC）生成赝数据（pseudo-data），将这些数据纳入已有的JAMDiFF全局分析（global analysis）框架，联合现有双强子实验数据进行重拟合。

Result: 杰斐逊实验室未来数据将显著降低中等至大夸克动量分数$x$区间横向性PDFs的不确定性；EIC数据则可约束整个$x$范围，首次实验检验横向性PDFs的预测小$x$行为。在张量荷不确定性缩减方面，将结果与格点QCD（lattice QCD）比较，揭示了二者之间可能出现兼容或张力的具体情景。

Conclusion: 未来Jefferson Lab和EIC的SIDIS双强子测量将大幅提升对横向性PDFs及核子张量荷的约束能力，并能为与格点QCD预言的一致性提供实验检验。

Abstract: We assess the impact of future measurements of dihadron production in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering from the CLAS12 and proposed SoLID experiments at Jefferson Lab, as well as from the ePIC experiment at the future Electron-Ion Collider (EIC), on the transversity parton distribution functions (PDFs) and the corresponding tensor charges of the nucleon. To this end, we generate pseudo-data for these experiments for a proton target (CLAS12 and ePIC) and a $^3$He target (SoLID and ePIC), and we include these pseudo-data in the JAMDiFF global analysis of existing experimental dihadron data. We find that future data from Jefferson Lab will significantly reduce uncertainties in the transversity PDFs in the region of intermediate-to-large quark momentum fractions $x$, while the EIC will provide strong constraints across the entire range of $x$, allowing for the first experimental test of the predicted small-$x$ behavior of the transversity PDFs. In discussing the reduction of uncertainties in the tensor charges, we also compare the results from the data analyses with those from lattice QCD, highlighting scenarios in which compatibility or tension between the two would arise.

### [129] [The Future of Lepton Flavor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05291)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选取五类流行的轻子味模型（leptonic flavor model）作为分析对象：质量求和规则（mass sum rules）、狄拉克型和马约拉纳型中微子的一重和双重纹理零点（texture zeros）、带电轻子修正（charged lepton corrections）、模对称性（modular symmetries）以及约束顺序主导（constrained sequential dominance）。将这些模型的理论预测与未来实验的预期测量数据建立对应关系，分析相关性（correlations）、简并性（degeneracies）和区分能力（discrimination capabilities）。

Result: 未来测量将精确确定中微子质量顺序（mass ordering）、$θ_{23}$八分圆（octant）、CP破坏量$δ$，并显著提升$θ_{12}$等振荡参数的精度；结合宇宙学数据集或β衰变端点谱测量获得的绝对中微子质量标度信息，将极大减少可行轻子味模型数量，并允许对各种模型进行有效区分。

Abstract: The flavor puzzle remains one of the biggest open questions in particle theory to date and upcoming results from neutrino experiments will have a large impact on its potential solution in the future. While some classes of leptonic flavor models are difficult to constrain with current data, this will change in the coming years as several yet unknown quantities, like the neutrino mass ordering and the octant of $θ_{23}$, will be determined, and the CP-violating quantity $δ$ will be measured with some precision. In addition, significant improvements in the precision of the other oscillation parameters, notably $θ_{12}$, is also expected to impact our understanding of flavor. Together with anticipated improvements on the absolute neutrino mass scale determination from the combination of cosmological data sets or beta decay endpoint spectrum measurements, upcoming experiments will lead to a refined picture of our understanding of flavor in the lepton sector. In this paper, we show exactly how flavor model predictions relate to expected measurements. Five popular classes of leptonic flavor model predictions are considered: mass sum rules, one and two texture-zeros for both Dirac and Majorana neutrinos, charged lepton corrections, modular symmetries, and constrained sequential dominance. We discuss correlations, degeneracies, and discrimination capabilities in the context of the expected measurements from upcoming experiments. We also highlight how different flavor model predictions can be differentiated and the roles each upcoming observable has on flavor model predictions. We anticipate that the precision targeted in future measurements will be sufficient to dramatically reduce the number of viable leptonic flavor models, will allow us to disentangle them, and could hopefully begin to shed light on the answer to the flavor puzzle.

Abstract: Paleodetectors have been proposed as a new approach to direct detection of weakly interacting massive particles (WIMPs), through the search for damage tracks in ancient minerals induced by WIMP-nucleon scattering. However, for inelastic dark matter such as the Higgsino, existing paleodetector targets lack sufficiently heavy nuclei to overcome the kinematic threshold for scattering. We propose heavy-element paleodetectors as a new probe of inelastic dark matter, using ancient, radiopure minerals containing heavy elements such as lead. We identify brine precipitates from deep geothermal aquifers as a possible geological source of such minerals. Additionally, paleodetectors are uniquely sensitive to the history of the dark matter high-velocity tail, including a possible fast population induced by the Large Magellanic Cloud's close approach 50 Myr ago. Such a scenario would favor younger minerals than usually assumed in the paleodetector literature. This method can probe Higgsino mass splittings up to $δ\simeq 920$ keV. Due to the large Higgsino-nucleon cross section, we find that even suboptimal mineral samples with ordinary radioactivity from depths of only 2 km can probe new parameter space, thus partially relaxing the stringent requirements on radiopurity and depth that constitute two significant challenges for the paleodetector program.

Method: 采用更高阶（higher-order）计算方法分析信号-背景干涉效应，研究聚焦于共振区域，并分别计算了 $gg \to H \to \gamma\gamma$（双光子道）和 $gg \to H \to Z\gamma$ 两个过程。

Conclusion: 干涉效应在两个通道中均表现为相消（destructive），且对 $Z\gamma$ 通道的修正幅度更大，表明在精确检验标准模型（Standard Model）时有必要将此类干涉效应纳入考量。

Abstract: In this contribution we summarize recent progress in higher-order computations of signal-background interference effects in Higgs boson production via gluon fusion. The focus is on the resonance region, where interference terms are most significant relative to the pure signal contribution when the Higgs boson decay is loop-induced. We present results for the well-studied $gg \to H \to γγ$ process and for the rare $gg \to H \to Zγ$ mode. In both cases, the interference is destructive, reducing the resonant Higgs boson production rate by about 1.6\% in the diphoton channel and by roughly 3\% in the $Zγ$ decay mode.

Main category: hep-ph

Method: 利用规范阿贝尔味对称性$U(1)_F$通过弗罗加特-尼尔森机制（Froggatt-Nielsen mechanism）实现自然保护，产生具有单位畴壁数（unit domain wall number）的意外高品质味轴子（accidental high-quality flavored axion），并分析其宇宙弦网络（cosmic-string networks）演化与衰变对引力波谱的影响。

Conclusion: 引力波谱中的平台-谷结构为高品质味轴子暗物质模型提供了独特而有力的探针，可与低能味实验（low-energy flavor experiments）互补，共同检验该理论框架。

Abstract: Axions, arising from an anomalous global Peccei-Quinn symmetry $U(1)_{\text{PQ}}$, offer a compelling solution to the strong CP problem but are vulnerable to Planck-suppressed operators. Gauged abelian flavor symmetries $U(1)_F$, invoked to explain the flavor hierarchies via the Froggatt-Nielsen mechanism, can naturally shield the axion from such effects, yielding an accidental high-quality flavored axion with unit domain wall number. Such constructions predict two complementary signatures: (i) flavor-changing neutral currents from $K\toπa$ decays, typically associated with high flavor scales $Λ_{\text{FN}}\gtrsim f_a$, and (ii) stochastic Gravitational Waves (GWs) sourced by the evolution and decay of gauged flavonic and axionic cosmic-string networks. In addition, global axionic strings can efficiently radiate axions, potentially accounting for the observed dark matter relic abundance. We show that the resulting characteristic plateau--valley structure in the GW spectrum provides a distinctive and powerful probe of high-quality flavored axion dark matter models, complementary to low-energy flavor experiments.

Abstract: In this work, we study a compact hexaquark configuration motivated by the same quark content as $D^{+} D^{-} K^+$ using QCD sum rules, where the $D D K$ system has been extensively studied within theoretical frameworks of few-body hadronic dynamics and coupled-channel interactions. The state is constructed from three color-octet quark--antiquark clusters coupled to an overall color singlet. ### [134] [Vector charmonium(-like) states in the energy range of 4.1-4.6 GeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06180)

TL;DR: 本文针对4.1-4.6 GeV能量区域矢量类粲偶素（vector charmonium(-like)）谱学中长期存在的矛盾，建立了一个统一的耦合道（coupled-channel）理论框架。该框架包含重夸克自旋对称性（heavy-quark spin symmetry）约束的开粲道、可选裸极点以及Z_c道末态相互作用，通过对BESIII多个截面的联合拟合证明，即便纯动力学方案也能捕捉所有分布的主要特征，表明观测到的线形异常主要由强耦合道效应与动力学产生的极点所主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建一个统一的耦合道框架，专用于该能区的1⁻⁻共振态（resonances）。框架纳入S波开粲道(D̄D₁, D̄*D₁, D*D̄₂*)、由重夸克自旋对称性约束、可选的夸克模型裸极点（bare poles，可能对应ψ(4160)与ψ(4415)），以及Z_c道中与三体末态相关的末态相互作用（final-state interaction）。基于此框架建立多个基准模型（benchmark models），对BESIII六个截面(e⁺e⁻→J/ψπ⁺π⁻, h_cπ⁺π⁻, D̄D̄*π, D*D̄*π, J/ψη, χ_c₀ω)及含Z_c(3900)和Z_c(4020)结构的不变质量分布进行联合拟合。

Result: 即使纯动力学方案（无裸极点）也能捕获所有分析分布的主要特征。引入紧凑裸态（bare compact states）可定量改善拟合质量，但不改变核心结论。

Conclusion: 该能区测量到的线形（line shapes）反常行为可被理解为强耦合道效应与动力学产生极点（dynamically generated poles）所致，无需依赖纯夸克模型态的常规解释。

Abstract: The spectrum of vector charmonium(-like) states in the 4.1-4.6 GeV energy region exhibits a long-standing tension. While the inclusive $R$-value indicates the presence of only vector charmonia that are usually interpreted as conventional states, exclusive $e^+e^-$ cross sections reveal additional structures whose parameters strongly depend on the observed final states when fitted with Breit-Wigner functions. This puzzling pattern suggests that coupled-channel and threshold effects play an essential role. In this work, we develop a unified coupled-channel framework relevant for the $1^{--}$ resonances in the considered energy region. The framework incorporates the $S$-wave open-charm channels $D\bar{D}_1$, $D^*\bar{D}_1$, and $D^*\bar{D}_2^*$, constrained by heavy-quark spin symmetry, optional bare poles corresponding to quark-model states which may be associated with the $ψ(4160)$ and the $ψ(4415)$, and final-state interaction in the $Z_c$ channels relevant for the three-body final states. We employ several benchmark models based on the constructed framework to perform simultaneous fits to the BESIII data for the cross sections of $e^+e^-\to J/ψπ^+π^-$, $h_cπ^+π^-$, $D\bar{D}^*π$, $D^*\bar{D}^*π$, $J/ψη$, and $χ_{c0}ω$, together with the available invariant-mass distributions that exhibit the $Z_c(3900)$ and $Z_c(4020)$ structures. The models differ in the number of bare seed states and the fitting strategy. We show that even the purely dynamical scheme captures the gross features of all the analyzed distributions. We therefore conclude that the nontrivial behavior of the measured line shapes in the studied energy range can be understood in terms of strong coupled-channel effects with dynamically generated poles. The inclusion of bare compact states leads to a quantitative improvement of the fit quality but does not alter this conclusion.

Motivation: 研究电弱规范玻色子的四顶点耦合（quartic gauge couplings）既能检验标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的预言，也能探索超出SM的新物理信号；现有研究对同号W±W±产生中的反常四规范耦合（anomalous quartic gauge couplings）尚缺乏基于偏振和自旋关联效应的系统分析。

Method: 在SM有效场论（SM Effective Field Theory, SM EFT）框架下，利用角不对称性（angular asymmetries）提取偏振与自旋关联效应，并结合传统运动学可观测量（如WW系统的横质量分布），进行联合约束分析；同时通过施加不变质量截断（invariant-mass cut-off）考察幺正性（unitarity）影响。

Result: 自旋关联不对称性（spin-correlation asymmetries）对反常WWWW相互作用的灵敏度与WW系统横质量分布相当；通过识别最小高灵敏度不对称性集合，可用较少可观测量捕获对Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）的主要约束；联合角不对称性与运动学信息可得到比单一方法更优的限制；引入不变质量截断后确定了幺正性安全的反常耦合参数区域。

Conclusion: 联合角不对称性与运动学可观测量可显著提升对反常四规范耦合的约束能力；幺正性条件通过对WW系统施加质量截断得以控制，从而划定可靠的参数空间。

Abstract: The study of quartic couplings of electroweak gauge bosons not only provides a test of the Standard Model (SM) predictions, but also can look for signals of new physics beyond the SM. We present a comprehensive study of anomalous quartic gauge couplings in same-sign $W^\pm W^\pm$ production via vector boson scattering at the LHC. The analysis is carried out within the framework of the SM Effective Field Theory, exploiting polarization and spin-correlation effects encoded in angular asymmetries in addition to conventional kinematic observables. We demonstrate that spin-correlation asymmetries provide sensitivity to anomalous $WWWW$ interactions that is comparable to that obtained from the transverse mass distribution of the $WW$ system. By identifying a minimal set of the most sensitive asymmetries, we show that the dominant constraints on the Wilson coefficients can be captured with a reduced number of observables. A combined analysis of angular asymmetries and kinematic information leads to improved limits compared to either approach alone. The impact of unitarity considerations is also examined by imposing invariant-mass cut-offs on the $WW$ system, allowing us to determine unitarity-safe regions for the anomalous couplings.

</details>


### [136] [Big Axions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05276)
*Hannah Banks,Marius Kongsore,Neal Weiner*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“大轴子（big axions）”模型：一种在理论空间（theory space）中通过非局域化U(1)对称性网络自发集体破缺而产生的南部-戈德斯通模式（Nambu-Goldstone mode）。该模型自然实现高品质偶然全局对称性，可容纳暴胀前与暴胀后两类宇宙学历史，并展现出丰富的拓扑结构，能够衔接普通佩切-奎因轴子（Peccei-Quinn axion）与源自额外维度规范场的轴子。作者还识别出一类最小可行的现象学子类——“小大轴子（little big axions）”，证明其能为量子色动力学中的强电荷-宇称问题（strong CP problem）提供鲁棒解，同时可能解释部分或全部暗物质（dark matter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轴子模型通常面临品质问题（quality problem）——即全局对称性会受到量子引力效应的破坏。本文旨在通过理论空间中的非局域化对称性破缺机制，自然实现高品质的偶然全局对称性，从而解决这一根本性理论难题。

Method: 作者引入“大轴子”概念，其关键机制是：在理论空间中非局域化（delocalized）的多个U(1)对称性构成网络，通过集体自发破缺（collective spontaneous breaking）产生一个南部-戈德斯通模式。该方法将普通轴子与来自额外维度规范场的轴子统一在同一个理论框架之下。

Result: 模型展示了丰富的拓扑结构，能够在普通佩切-奎因轴子与源自额外维度规范场的轴子之间进行插值（interpolate）。同时识别出“小大轴子”这一最小可行现象学子类，该子类既可解决强CP问题，又有潜力构成部分或全部暗物质。

Conclusion: 大轴子模型为高品质偶然全局对称性提供了一种自然实现方式，并具有兼容两种宇宙学历史（暴胀前与暴胀后）的理论灵活性。其中“小大轴子”子类是一个现象学上可行的最小模型，同时解决强CP问题与暗物质候选者两大核心问题。

Abstract: We introduce big axions: axion models in which a Nambu-Goldstone mode emerges from the collective spontaneous breaking of a network of U(1) symmetries delocalized in theory space. Big axions naturally realize high-quality accidental global symmetries, admit both pre- and post-inflationary cosmological histories, and exhibit rich topological structures that interpolate between ordinary Peccei-Quinn axions and axions which descend from extra-dimensional gauge fields. We identify a minimal phenomenologically viable subclass, little big axions, and demonstrate that they provide a robust solution to the strong charge-parity problem in quantum chromodynamics while potentially accounting for some or all of the dark matter of the universe.

</details>


### [137] [Bulk viscosity of a binary mixture: the role of the intra-species interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06105)
*Gabriele Parisi,Vincenzo Nugara,Shams Ul Arfeen,Salvatore Plumari,Vincenzo Greco*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在 Chapman-Enskog 框架下，将混合流体体粘滞系数（bulk viscosity）从一阶展开改进至二阶，显著改善了与 Green-Kubo 形式及相对论玻尔兹曼方程数值解的一致性，尤其修正了一阶结果在组分质量相近时的物理缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 体粘滞系数 ζ 是现代物理学多个领域的关键输运系数，但二元混合物的 ζ 计算涉及多时间尺度微观过程的复杂相互作用。已有 Chapman-Enskog 一阶结果无法复现相关物理特征，尤其当两种组分质量相近时偏差明显，因此需要更高阶的解析改进。

Method: 在 Chapman-Enskog（CE）框架下，基于玻尔兹曼分布函数（Boltzmann distribution function）的级数展开，将混合流体的体粘滞系数 ζ 推导至二阶（2nd order）。随后将其与基于相对论玻尔兹曼方程（Relativistic Boltzmann equation）数值解的 Green-Kubo 形式（Green-Kubo formalism）结果进行对比验证。

Result: 二阶结果编码了一阶结果所缺失的多种物理性质；在某些特定条件下，二阶结果与一阶结果在定性及定量上均存在显著差异。与 Green-Kubo 基准的比较表明，从一阶转向二阶 CE 结果后，一致性显著提高。

Conclusion: 将 Chapman-Enskog 展开提升至二阶能够有效弥补一阶结果在混合物体粘滞系数计算中的不足，为更准确地描述复合流体系统的输运行为提供了改进的解析途径。

Abstract: The bulk viscosity $ζ$ is a transport coefficient which is of central importance for various areas of modern physics. In particular, its determination for a mixture of more than one fluid is challenging, since it involves a complex interplay of multiple microscopic processes that operate on different time scales. Within the Chapman-Enskog framework, based on a series expansion of the Boltzmann distribution function, many previous works have derived the 1$^{\text{st}}$ order result for the $ζ$ of a mixture. However, such a result fails to reproduce relevant physical features of the system, especially when the masses of the two components are similar. In this work we improve the 1$^{\text{st}}$ order Chapman-Enskog result by deriving the $ζ$ at the 2$^{\text{nd}}$ order in the expansion. We show that this improved formula encodes many physical properties that the 1$^{\text{st}}$ order result misses: under specific conditions, the 2$^{\text{nd}}$ order result can be qualitatively and quantitatively very different from the 1$^{\text{st}}$ order one. Moreover, this result is compared against the $ζ$ evaluated within the Green-Kubo formalism, by means of a numerical solution of the Relativistic Boltzmann equation. The agreement with respect to this benchmark is significantly improved when moving from the 1$^{\text{st}}$ to the 2$^{\text{nd}}$ order CE result.

</details>


### [138] [Spin-orbit correlation of quarks within quarkonium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06263)
*Tianyang Hu,Xianghui Cao,Siqi Xu,Weijie Du,Qin-Tao Song,Yang Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究建立了自旋-轨道关联（spin-orbit correlation, SOC）的场论定义与非微扰光前动力学（light-front dynamics）量子多体框架之间的联系，展示了如何从宇称奇能量-动量张量（parity-odd energy-momentum tensor, EMT）的强子矩阵元中提取SOC，并首次计算了粲偶素（charmonium）和B_c介子的横向与纵向SOC分布，揭示了丰富的部分子（partonic）动力学信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋-轨道关联（SOC）为探测强子的内部自旋结构提供了独特的探针，即使在总角动量为零的系统中该观测量也可非零。然而，其场论定义与可计算的非微扰框架之间的具体联系尚待建立，且该观测量在部分子图像（partonic picture）中的直接提取路径尚未明确。

Method: 将SOC的形式化场论定义与基于光前动力学（light-front dynamics）的非微扰量子多体框架相连接；从宇称奇能量-动量张量（P-odd EMT）的强子矩阵元中直接提取SOC；在部分子图像下计算该观测量。

Result: 计算了粲偶素（charmonium）和B_c介子的横向与纵向SOC分布；结果与基于克莱布施-高登分解（Clebsch-Gordan decomposition）的粗略估计一致。

Conclusion: SOC观测量能提供关于部分子动力学（partonic dynamics）的丰富、非平凡信息。

Abstract: The spin-orbit correlation (SOC) provides a unique probe into the internal spin structure of hadrons. Defined via the parity-odd (P-odd) energy-momentum tensor (EMT), this observable can remain non-vanishing even in systems where the total angular momentum is zero. In this study, we connect the formal field-theoretical definition of the SOC to a non-perturbative quantum many-body framework utilizing light-front dynamics. Furthermore, we show how the SOC can be extracted directly from the hadronic matrix elements of the P-odd EMT, establishing a pathway to access this observable within the partonic picture. As a practical application, we compute the transverse and longitudinal SOC distributions for charmonium and $B_c$ mesons. While our findings align with rough estimates based on the Clebsch-Gordan decomposition, we demonstrate that these observables yield rich, non-trivial information regarding partonic dynamics.

</details>


### [139] [Diffusion of multiple conserved charges from entropy production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06283)
*Samapan Bhadury,Arpan Das,Sandeep Chatterjee,Hiranmaya Mishra*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于查普曼-恩斯科格（Chapman-Enskog）方法，在动理学理论框架下推导了包含重子数（B）、电荷（Q）和奇异数（S）多个守恒荷的耗散性相对论流体动力学方程，得到了从一阶到二阶的耗散方程以及扩散矩阵元（κ_{qq'}），并估算了这些输运系数随温度和化学势的变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重离子碰撞初始态中非均匀的重子阻止（baryon stopping）会产生多组分扩散动力学，需要包含多个守恒荷的耗散性相对论流体动力学描述以及对扩散矩阵元的定量理解。

Method: 采用动理学理论（kinetic theory）框架，利用查普曼-恩斯科格（CE）方法求解相对论玻尔兹曼方程（relativistic Boltzmann equation），碰撞项采用松弛时间近似（relaxation-time approximation）且松弛时间与动量无关。基于玻尔兹曼H定理（Boltzmann's H-theorem）和熵产生条件，对非平衡分布函数在局部平衡附近进行一阶和二阶梯度展开。

Result: 导出了包含剪切黏度（η）、体黏度（ζ）以及扩散矩阵元（κ_{qq'}）的输运系数，其中扩散矩阵元包含B、Q、S三个守恒荷之间的对角和非对角元素。估算了(2+1)味夸克-胶子等离子体中扩散矩阵元的温度（T）和化学势依赖关系，并给出了比值κ_{qq'}T/η在宽温度及化学势范围内的数值结果。

Conclusion: 扩散矩阵元κ_{qq'}对于描述多组分扩散动力学至关重要；通过比值κ_{qq'}T/η可以评估扩散矩阵元相对于其他输运系数的相对重要性，这为重离子碰撞中多守恒荷耗散流体动力学模拟提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We derive dissipative relativistic hydrodynamic equations in the presence of multiple conserved charges, i.e., baryon number ($B$), electric charge ($Q$), and strangeness ($S$), using the Chapman-Enskog (CE) method within the kinetic theory approach. The relativistic Boltzmann equation is solved within the relaxation-time approximation with a momentum-independent relaxation time in the collision term. We derive both first-order (Navier-Stokes limit) and second-order dissipative hydrodynamic equations. Within the kinetic theory framework, using the Boltzmann's H-theorem, and by demanding that for a dissipative system, the entropy must be produced, we find different transport coefficients at the first-order and second-order gradient expansion of the out-of-equilibrium distribution function around the local equilibrium. Apart from the well-known transport coefficients, the shear ($η$) and the bulk ($ζ$) viscosities , we also find the diffusion matrix elements ($κ_{qq^{\prime}}$) for the conserved charges $B$, $Q$ and $S$. The diffusion matrix elements ($κ_{qq^{\prime}}$) are important to model the multi-component diffusion dynamics sourced by inhomogeneous baryon stopping in the initial state of heavy-ion collisions. We estimate the temperature ($T$) and chemical potential dependence of diagonal and off-diagonal elements of the diffusion matrix elements for the (2+1) flavor quark-gluon plasma. We further estimate the ratio $κ_{qq^{\prime}}T/η$ for a wide range of temperature and chemical potentials to show the relative importance of the diffusion matrix elements compared to other transport coefficients.

### [140] [Transcranial FUS Therapy and Monitoring using Nonlinear Acoustics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05628)
*Pradosh Pritam Dash*

Main category: physics.med-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一套基于声学全息图（acoustic hologram）的创新框架，用于解决经颅超声（transcranial ultrasound, TUS）在临床应用中因颅骨复杂性导致的焦点畸变和衰减问题。框架包括频域拓扑优化方法实现高保真聚焦、基于非线性参量阵（parametric array, PA）效应的非侵入式配准策略，以及利用PA效应监测脑室扩张作为颅内压变化的非侵入式代理指标。此外，还展示了一个体外聚焦超声神经调控平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚焦超声（focused ultrasound, FUS）具有无创调控神经活动和深脑递送的巨大临床潜力，然而经颅超声（TUS）的临床进展受限于颅骨复杂性引起的焦点畸变和衰减；现有相控阵校正方案成本高昂且持续依赖磁共振成像（magnetic resonance imaging, MRI），阻碍了广泛学术研究和临床转化。

Method: 提出了一个三部分组成的创新框架：(1) 一种新颖的频域拓扑优化方法，通过考虑体积波传播效应克服了传统纯相位设计在兆赫兹（megahertz）频段的失效，实现高保真聚焦；(2) 一种非侵入式配准策略，利用非线性参量阵列（parametric array, PA）效应实现精确透镜对准，无需MRI等成像模态；(3) 利用PA效应作为监测脑室扩张的非侵入式工具，作为脑积水颅内压变化的代理指标。此外，还构建了一个体外聚焦超声神经调控平台。

Result: 频域拓扑优化方法在高频段实现了优于传统纯相位设计的聚焦精度；非侵入式PA配准策略成功实现了精确透镜对准；PA效应可有效作为脑室扩张的非侵入式监测手段，反映颅内压变化。体外神经调控平台验证了基于声学的治疗发现能力。

Conclusion: 该研究为构建可及、高精度的经颅超声系统提供了可行路径，有助于推动其学术研究和临床转化。声学全息图框架在降低成本、消除对MRI依赖方面具有显著优势，PA效应在颅内压监测中的潜在应用拓展了超声的临床功能。

Abstract: Focused ultrasound (FUS) offers a promising, non-invasive method for modulating neural activity and delivering therapies deep within the brain with immense clinical potential. However, progress in developing transcranial ultrasound (TUS) for clinical applications has been hindered by several factors. The complexity of the human skull causes focal aberrations and attenuation, thereby presenting a major obstacle to the precise targeting of ultrasound waves. Although phased arrays can correct for these aberrations, their high cost and continuous reliance on magnetic resonance imaging (MRI) pose significant obstacles for widespread academic research and clinical translation. To address these challenges, this thesis proposes an innovative framework for the design, registration, and clinical application of acoustic holograms. First, we introduce a novel frequency-domain topology optimization method that overcomes the breakdown of traditional phase-only designs in the megahertz regime by accounting for volumetric wave-propagation effects, thereby achieving high-fidelity focusing. Second, we present a non-invasive registration strategy that utilizes the nonlinear parametric array (PA) effect to enable precise lens alignment without requiring any imaging modalities, such as MRI. Finally, we demonstrate the utility of this nonlinear parametric array (PA) effect as a tool for monitoring ventricular dilation as a non-invasive proxy for intracranial pressure changes in hydrocephalus. Collectively, these developments provide a path toward accessible, high-precision transcranial ultrasound systems for research and clinical use. In addition, we demonstrate a novel platform for in vitro focused ultrasound neuromodulation that leverages acoustics to advance therapeutic discovery.

### [141] [xCPS: an xAct package for covariant phase space, Noether charges, and entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05204)
*Juan Margalef-Bentabol*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: xCPS 是一个基于 xAct 的张量代数软件包，用于在场论的协变相空间形式（covariant phase space formalism）中进行符号计算。它能够从通用拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）自动推导运动方程、辛流（symplectic currents），判定无穷小变换是否为 Noether 对称性（Noether symmetry）并计算相应的 Noether 荷，还能判定张量表达式是否为散度（divergence）并寻找其散度势（divergence potential）。该包通过实现具有分级超交换楔积（graded supercommutative wedge product）和垂直算子（vertical operators）的垂直外微积分（vertical exterior calculus），支持规范理论和高阶导数引力模型的高效计算，包括热力学量（如 Wald 熵）的推导。xCPS 以 GPL 许可证开源发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在场论的协变相空间形式体系中，许多符号计算（如运动方程推导、对称性分析、散度判定等）手动执行繁琐且易错，现有工具缺乏对此形式体系的系统自动化支持。因此，开发 xCPS 旨在填补这一空白，为理论物理学家提供一个高效、自动化的符号计算工具。

Method: xCPS 基于 xAct 张量代数框架，从通用拉格朗日量出发，自动化执行协变相空间形式中的关键计算。它通过引入分级超交换楔积和垂直算子实现垂直外微积分，从而支持规范理论和包含高阶导数的引力理论。

Result: xCPS 能够自动推导运动方程和辛流，系统判定无穷小变换是否为 Noether 对称性并计算 Noether 荷，以及判定张量表达式是否为散度并寻找其散度势。该包还能高效处理规范理论和高阶导数引力模型，例如推导 Wald 熵等热力学量。

Conclusion: xCPS 作为一个开源软件包，为协变相空间形式中的符号计算提供了系统化自动化支持，特别适用于规范理论和复杂引力理论的研究，降低了手动计算的复杂度。

Abstract: xCPS is an xAct tensor algebra package for symbolic computations within the covariant phase space formalism of field theories. From a generic Lagrangian, xCPS automates the derivation of equations of motion and symplectic currents. It systematically determines whether an infinitesimal transformation in the space of fields is a Noether symmetry and computes the associated Noether charge. Additionally, xCPS can in many cases determine whether a tensorial expression is a divergence and, if so, find its divergence potential. By implementing vertical exterior calculus through a graded, supercommutative wedge product and vertical operators, the package enables efficient computations in gauge theories and higher-derivative models of gravity, including the derivation of thermodynamic quantities like Wald's entropy. xCPS is open-source under the GPL license and available at https://github.com/juanmargalef.

</details>


### [142] [The Score Hamiltonian: Mapping Diffusion Models to Adiabatic Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05217)
*Peter Halmos,Boris Hanin*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文发现了基于分数的扩散模型（score-based diffusion models）采样与薛定谔算子的基态绝热输运（adiabatic transport of ground states）之间的精确对应关系，其中薛定谔算子由学习到的分数的量子势（quantum potential）构造，称为分数哈密顿量（Score Hamiltonian）。通过含时势的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equations）的绝热定理，推导了新的密度重建界（density reconstruction bounds）和原理性退火调度（principled annealing schedules）。发现采样的根本极限由分数匹配误差平方与分数哈密顿量谱间隙（spectral gap）——即数据密度的庞加莱常数倒数（inverse Poincaré constant）——的比值决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示基于分数的扩散模型采样与量子绝热过程之间的深层理论联系，为采样算法的精度与效率提供严格的数学化约束和物理原理性指导。

Method: 建立了基于分数的扩散模型采样与一类基于学习分数的量子势构造的薛定谔算子的基态绝热输运之间的精确对应关系；利用含时势的福克-普朗克方程的绝热定理推导密度重建界和退火调度。

Result: 推导出新的密度重建界和原理性退火调度；明确了采样的理论下限由分数匹配误差平方与数据密度的庞加莱常数倒数之比决定。

Conclusion: 基于分数的扩散模型采样问题可以等价转化为基态绝热输运问题，其性能上限由数据密度的谱几何属性（庞加莱常数）与分数匹配误差共同约束。

Abstract: We exhibit an exact correspondence between sampling with score-based diffusion models and adiabatic transport of ground states for a family of Schrödinger operators we call Score Hamiltonians, built from the learned score's quantum potential. We obtain novel density reconstruction bounds and principled annealing schedules via adiabatic theorems for Fokker-Planck equations with time-varying potentials. We find the fundamental limit of sampling is set by the ratio of squared score-matching error to Score Hamiltonian spectral gap - the inverse Poincaré constant of the data density.

</details>


### [143] [Universal deformations and universal residual stresses in incompressible isotropic Cauchy elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05416)
*Arash Yavari*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了不可压缩各向同性柯西弹性固体（incompressible isotropic Cauchy elastic solids）在残余应力（residual stress）存在下的普适变形（universal deformations），证明了残余应力不会扩大普适变形的空间，并推导了六类已知普适变形对应的普适残余应力场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 残余应力广泛存在于各类固体材料中，但现有理论对残余应力下弹性体的普适变形认识不足。本文旨在不假设残余应力具体来源的前提下，系统研究残余应力对不可压缩各向同性柯西弹性固体中普适变形的影响。

Method: 基于柯西应力（Cauchy stress）作为应变和残余应力的各向同性张量值函数（isotropic tensor-valued function）的本构表示，推导了含残余应力的不可压缩各向同性柯西弹性固体的普适性约束条件（universality constraints）。假设残余应力场与对应普适变形具有相同对称性，将普适性约束简化为可显式求解的常微分方程系统。

Result: 证明了六类已知普适变形集合与无残余应力时的不可压缩各向同性弹性体完全相同，残余应力不会扩大普适变形的空间。针对每类普适变形，求解并刻画了对应的普适残余应力场。

Conclusion: 残余应力不改变不可压缩各向同性柯西弹性固体的普适变形类别，但可以通过普适性约束确定与之兼容的残余应力场分布。这一结果有助于理解残余应力对材料变形行为的影响。

Abstract: We study universal deformations in incompressible isotropic Cauchy elastic solids with residual stress, without assuming any specific origin for the residual stress. Starting from the constitutive representation of the Cauchy stress as an isotropic tensor-valued function of strain and residual stress, we derive the universality constraints for residually-stressed incompressible isotropic Cauchy elastic solids. We show that for the six known families of universal deformations the set of universal deformations is identical to that of incompressible isotropic elasticity in the absence of residual stress. We also show that residual stress does not enlarge the space of universal deformations. We then determine the universal residual stress fields corresponding to the six known families of universal deformations. Assuming that the residual stress field has the same symmetry as the corresponding universal deformation, the universality constraints reduce to systems of ordinary differential equations that can be solved explicitly. The resulting universal residual stress fields are characterized and discussed for each family.

Method: 论文提出两组关于 Gaussian 量子细胞自动机（GQCA）的条件，分别可独立保证热化；中间步骤是证明了一个量子多体版本的 Riemann-Lebesgue 引理（quantum many-body generalization of the Riemann-Lebesgue lemma），该引理对局部 Weyl 算符（local Weyl operators）的期望值给出了依赖于其支撑集（support）和状态粒子密度的上界。

Result: 在平移不变的 GQCA 作用下，满足所提条件时，任何局部正规且粒子密度一致有界的态，在局部 Weyl 代数（local Weyl algebra）上都会热化到无限温度态（infinite temperature state）。

Conclusion: 平移不变 Gaussian 量子细胞自动机在特定条件下可以作为玻色子系统热化到无限温度的一种机制。量子多体 Riemann-Lebesgue 引理为此提供了关键的分析工具。

Abstract: We study the long-time dynamics of many-body bosonic lattice systems under translation-invariant Gaussian quantum cellular automata. We formulate two sets of conditions on GQCAs which separately guarantee thermalization of any state on the local Weyl algebra to the infinite temperature state, whenever the state is locally normal and has uniformly bounded particle density. Our main intermediate result is a quantum many-body generalization of the classic Riemann-Lebesgue lemma which is a bound on expectation values of local Weyl operators involving their support and the state's particle density.

Abstract: Despite significant advancements in parameterizations of boundary layer processes, forecasting, and nowcasting low-level clouds using numerical models remain challenging. ### [146] [Liouville-Preserving Hamiltonian Scattering on Finite Metric Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05973)
*Philip Hierhager*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究如何在度量图（metric graph）上通过补全顶点处的能量保持同构（energy-preserving Borel isomorphism）来定义确定性的经典运动，并证明该动力学系统具有可测的全局单参数变换群、能量守恒以及由边上的Liouville测度诱导的商测度不变性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 度量图上每条边具有力学哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）时，通过分支顶点的经典运动仅由能量守恒无法确定出射方向。本文旨在通过补充顶点处的确定性规则（即能量保持的Borel同构），将这一缺失的顶点数据补全，从而建立全局确定的经典动力学。

Method: 在每个顶点处规定一个能量保持的Borel同构（energy-preserving Borel isomorphism），将入射边界余切向量（incoming boundary covector）映射到出射边界余切向量。相空间（phase space）定义为识别入射线与出射线的可测商空间。通过排除有限个顶点势能值V(v)，将边上的Hamilton方程与顶点规则拼接，构造全局的单参数变换群。采用边上的Liouville测度（Liouville measure）dq dp诱导商测度，利用连续正则能量窗口上的均匀无Zeno估计（uniform no-Zeno estimate）以及速度方向顶点置换对横向Liouville通量r dr的保持性质证明不变性。

Result: 补全顶点数据后，边上的Hamilton方程与顶点规则共同定义了一个全局的单参数保测变换群（one-parameter group of bimeasurable transformations），该群保持能量守恒以及由边Liouville测度诱导的商测度不变。若顶点规则与动量反转（momentum reversal）相容，则该商动力学是可逆的（reversible）。在满足通常正则值条件的正则能量面上，诱导的时间参数化测度也是不变的。

Conclusion: 通过在顶点处补充能量保持的Borel同构，度量图上的哈密顿系统可以具有确定性的全局动力学，且该动力学保持能量和商Liouville测度不变。该结论不依赖于商空间上的光滑辛结构（smooth symplectic structure），证明基于边上的Liouville不变性及其横向通量保持性质。

Abstract: A metric graph with a mechanical Hamiltonian on each edge does not, by itself, define a deterministic classical motion through a branching vertex: conservation of energy fixes only the outgoing speed, not the outgoing edge-end. We study the deterministic problem obtained after this missing vertex datum is supplied. On each edge $e$, with coordinate $q\in[0,\ell_e]$, the Hamiltonian is $H_e(q,p)=p^2/2+V_e(q)$, where $V$is continuous on the graph and $C^2$ on every edge. At each vertex we prescribe an energy-preserving Borel isomorphism from incoming to outgoing nonzero boundary covectors. The resulting phase space is the measurable quotient that identifies each incoming boundary covector with its prescribed outgoing one. After excluding the finitely many energy levels $V(v)$, the edgewise Hamilton equations and the vertex laws concatenate to a global one-parameter group of bimeasurable transformations. The group preserves energy and the quotient measure induced by the edgewise Liouville measures $dq\,dp$. The proof uses no smooth symplectic structure on the quotient; the invariance follows from ordinary edgewise Liouville invariance, a uniform no-Zeno estimate on compact regular energy windows, and preservation of the transverse Liouville flux $r\,dr$ by the speedwise vertex permutations. If the vertex laws are compatible with momentum reversal, then the quotient dynamics is reversible. On regular energy surfaces satisfying the usual regular-value condition, the induced time-parametrization measure is invariant as well.

</details>

### [147] [GEMINI: Generalized Ensnarlment Measure from Incomplete-linkage of Network-network Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05153)
*Yu Tian,Chinmayi Subramanya,Carl D. Modes*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文引入GEMINI算子，基于不完全高斯链接积分（incomplete Gauss linking integral）直接刻画空间嵌入网络（spatially embedded networks）中边与边之间的拓扑与几何关联，为复杂生物网络的结构-功能关系提供一种通用的量化分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间嵌入网络在物理与生物系统中广泛存在，但由于其架构复杂性，以往难以进行约化建模或有效表征，使得结构-功能关系（structure-function relationships）的研究长期受阻。现有方法虽能将网络分解为树状与环状子结构，但缺乏在完整网络语境下同时量化拓扑（topology）与几何（geometry）特征的工具。

Method: 提出GEMINI算子，这是一种同时具有拓扑感知和几何感知能力的算符。该算子基于不完全形式的高斯链接积分（Gauss linking integral）构建边-边关联（edge-edge association）信息，当边集合形成链接组合时能保持拓扑敏感性。

Result: 在合成格子（synthetic lattices）和小鼠大脑血管网络数据上的验证表明，GEMINI能够系统性地捕获并分类复杂结构组织（structural organizations），有效区分不同空间网络的架构模式。

Conclusion: GEMINI为真实数据中的空间网络分析提供了一种通用方法，适用于拓扑与几何共同决定功能的场景，从而为理解复杂网络组织关键的大量生物学实例中的结构-功能关系开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Spatially embedded networks are central to many physical and biological systems, where geometry and connectivity jointly shape structure and function. Examples abound across the scales of biological organization, from network-like membrane-bound organelles in the cell to mesoscale tissue organization of multiple distinct flow networks in organs and beyond. In each of these cases, the complexity of the architectures has heretofore frustrated our ability to link mechanism or regulation of these structures to reduced modeling or even relevant characterization, putting structure-function relationships largely out of reach. Complex, functional spatial networks can be decomposed into tree-like and cyclic substructures, but we still lack both an understanding of how these elements intertwine to give rise to function, and the tools to holistically quantify both the topological and geometric aspects of these features in their full network context. To close this gap, we here introduce GEMINI, a topology and geometry aware operator that directly characterizes incomplete linking and more general spatial associations between edges in spatially embedded network architectures. GEMINI contains information on edge-edge association through an incomplete version of the Gauss linking integral which simultaneously endows it with topological sensitivity when collections of edges form linked assemblages. Validation on both synthetic lattices and on mouse brain vasculature data demonstrates that GEMINI systematically captures and classifies the complexity of structural organizations. Our results provide a general approach for analyzing spatial networks in realistic data, where topology and geometry together determine function, thus opening the door to a more complete understanding of structure-function relationships across a broad set of biological examples where complex network organization is key.

</details>


### [148] [Newton's Identity in Finite-Bead Fermionic Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05442)
*A. Chaudhary,J. Valenzuela*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 针对谐波势阱（harmonic trap）中的无相互作用费米子（non-interacting fermions），该研究从路径积分（path integral）的行列式约化形式出发，推导出任意虚时切片数下配分函数（partition function）的精确递推关系。通过识别该递推与牛顿恒等式（Newton's identity）的直接对应，利用分拆理论（theory of partitions）的封闭形式结果导出一维n费米子有限虚时切片配分函数的精确表达式，并据此解析计算了热力学能量、哈密顿量能量（Hamiltonian energy）及比热（specific heat）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有连续极限下的递推关系不适用于离散时间配分函数（discrete time partition functions），因此需要建立可直接用于任意虚时切片数和任意短时传播子（short-time propagator）选择的精确递推关系，以弥补有限虚时切片情形下解析计算的空白。

Method: 从路径积分的收缩行列式形式（contracted determinant form）出发，直接推导出有限虚时切片数的精确递推关系；将该递推与牛顿恒等式建立对应，进而应用分拆理论的封闭形式结果，得到一维n费米子有限虚时切片配分函数的解析表达式。

Result: 对于任意粒子数n、虚时切片数N、虚时间步长τ及任意短时传播子选择，均能解析计算热力学能量、哈密顿量能量和比热。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种无需连续极限的有限虚时切片解析方法，为路径积分蒙特卡罗（path integral Monte Carlo）中离散时间效应的精确处理提供了理论依据。

Abstract: For non-interacting fermions in a harmonic trap, the partition function at any discrete number of imaginary time slices (or beads) and for any choice of short-time propagator admits an exact recursion relation derived directly from the contracted determinant form of the path integral. This finite-bead recursion is distinct from earlier continuum-limit recursions, which do not apply to the discrete time partition functions. By identifying a direct correspondence between this recursion and Newton's identity, application of a closed-form result from the theory of partitions provides an exact expression for the one-dimensional $n$-fermion finite-bead partition function. From this, the Thermodynamic and Hamiltonian energies and specific heats are analytically calculated for any $n$, $N$, $τ$, and propagator choice.

Conclusion: 本工作为平面波场中的半经典辐射反冲提供了完整的解析框架，在保持方程可积性的前提下成功引入了量子修正，有助于理解强场量子电动力学（strong-field quantum electrodynamics）中的电子动力学。

Abstract: We analyze electron dynamics in a plane electromagnetic wave using the Landau-Lifshitz equation with a quantum radiation reaction correction modeled by a Gaunt factor. In this geometry, the quantum parameter $χ$ depends solely on the lightfront momentum, allowing the modified equation of motion to retain the integrable structure of the classical problem. We derive an exact solution for the energy evolution and the four-velocity, which reduces to the known classical result in the appropriate limit. The results provide an analytical and deterministic description of semiclassical radiation reaction in plane-wave fields.

### [150] [Coupled simulation of plasma-surface interactions during early stages of vacuum arcing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05893)
*Roni Koitermaa,Andreas Kyritsakis,Tauno Tiirats,Flyura Djurabekova,Veronika Zadin*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个全耦合模拟框架，将原子尺度阴极动力学与真空电弧（vacuum arcing）早期阶段的等离子体形成相连接，揭示了铜纳米凸起（Cu nanoprotrusions）热失控的两条路径：直接焦耳加热驱动不稳定性与一种新颖的纳米颗粒辅助机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 模型将分子动力学（molecular dynamics）、有限元电热计算（finite element electrothermal calculations）、电子发射（electron emission）与粒子云网格（particle-in-cell）等离子体模拟相结合，通过表面与等离子体域之间的动态粒子传递实现全耦合。

Result: 对铜纳米凸起的模拟识别出两条热失控（thermal runaway）路径：一是直接的焦耳加热驱动不稳定性，二是纳米颗粒辅助机制——脱落的纳米颗粒产生中性蒸气后被电离。

Conclusion: 该全耦合模拟方法能够揭示真空电弧早期阶段中原子尺度阴极动力学与等离子体形成之间的复杂相互作用，并发现了一种此前未知的纳米颗粒辅助热失控路径。

Abstract: We describe fully coupled simulations that bridge atomistic cathode dynamics and plasma formation during the earliest stages of vacuum arcing. The model combines molecular dynamics, finite element electrothermal calculations, electron emission and particle-in-cell plasma simulations via dynamic transfer of particles between the surface and plasma domains. Simulations of Cu nanoprotrusions reveal two routes to thermal runaway: direct Joule heating-driven instability and a novel nanoparticle-assisted mechanism, where detached nanoparticles generate neutral vapor that becomes ionized.

</details>

### [151] [A universal and efficient hybrid digital-analog fermionic quantum simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05517)
*Hao-Tian Wei,Kaden R. A. Hazzard*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一个通用框架，利用费米子超冷原子平台进行量子模拟，证明变分算法能够在现有硬件上模拟远超硬件原生哈密顿量的多体系统，并对无能隙目标哈密顿量的基态性质实现多项式时间的量子模拟，相比经典精确对角化算法提供指数级加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前量子模拟硬件受限于其原生哈密顿量（native Hamiltonian），无法直接模拟超出其设计范围的物理系统。本文旨在建立一种通用框架，利用现有费米子超冷原子平台上的变分算法，实现对更广泛多体系统的高效量子模拟。

Method: 论文提出一种通用框架，利用费米子超冷原子（fermionic ultracold atom）平台结合变分算法（variational algorithm）进行量子模拟。通过分析证明，针对一大类无能隙目标哈密顿量（gapless target Hamiltonian）的局域观测量（local observables），量子模拟时间随逆相对误差的多项式增长，并提供了数值证据与理论论证。

Result: 量子模拟时间满足 $T\sim O(\mathrm{poly}(1/ε))$（含对数修正），相比朴素经典算法（如精确对角化）实现指数级加速（exponential speedup）。在三个不同模型中提供了数值证据：排斥性哈伯德模型（repulsive Hubbard model）、含最近邻吸引相互作用的哈伯德模型（引入配对现象）、以及霍夫施塔特-哈伯德模型（Hofstadter-Hubbard model，引入规范场与分数量子霍尔效应）。

Conclusion: 该工作表明，利用当前费米子平台可以进行远超硬件原生模型的量子模拟，为在现有硬件上实现更复杂多体系统的量子模拟提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We present a universal framework to harness fermionic ultracold atom platforms for quantum simulation, showing how variational algorithms on existing hardware can simulate many-body systems well beyond the hardware's native Hamiltonian. Our analysis provides evidence that one can quantum simulate the ground-state properties of a broad class of gapless target Hamiltonians of local observables in a quantum evolution time that grows polynomially with the inverse relative error, $T\sim O(\mathrm{poly}(1/ε))$ up to logarithmic corrections, offering an exponential speedup over na{ï}ve classical algorithms such as exact diagonalization. We provide numerical evidence and theoretical argument that this holds for energy density, density-density, and spin-spin correlations in three qualitatively distinct models -- the repulsive Hubbard model; a Hubbard model augmented with nearest-neighbor attractive interactions, which introduces the phenomenon of pairing; and the Hofstadter-Hubbard model, which introduces a gauge field and fractional quantum Hall physics. This work demonstrates quantum simulation using current fermionic platforms far beyond the models natively implemented in the hardware.

</details>


### [152] [Charge-Conjugation Violation and Population Asymmetry in Bipartite Fermionic Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06138)
*Di Xiao,Xue-Ting Fang,Lushuai Cao,Zhong-Kun Hu,Peter Schmelcher*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本论文通过二分费米子晶格中的子晶格扭结（sublattice kink）建立了一种内禀电荷共轭对称性破坏（intrinsic CCV）机制，其根源在于哈密顿量的图拓扑性质（graph-topological nature），并导致构型种群不对称以及隐叶状特征（hidden leaf-like structure）的能谱结构，该不对称性还可通过淬火动力学中的真空不稳定性（vacuum-instability）产生不平衡的子晶格扭结生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷共轭对称性破坏（charge conjugation violation, CCV）是粒子物理的核心概念，也出现在量子多体系统的准粒子中，但通常依赖于系统中嵌入的外在对称性破缺。一个悬而未决的问题是：内禀CCV机制如何产生，以及其宏观后果是什么。

Method: 在二分费米子晶格中建立子晶格扭结作为展现内禀CCV的具体构型。该内禀CCV基于底层哈密顿量的图拓扑性质，不涉及任何显式对称性破缺。

Result: 内禀CCV导致不同构型的种群不对称性（population asymmetry），并在本征能谱中留下隐叶状结构。种群不对称性还通过淬火动力学中的真空不稳定性触发不平衡的子晶格扭结产生。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了图拓扑（graph topology）作为内禀CCV的微观起源，种群不对称性是其宏观后果，所提出的构型非常适合于通过冷原子量子模拟器（cold-atom quantum simulators）进行实验实现。

Abstract: Charge conjugation violation (CCV) is a central concept in particle physics and appears also for quasiparticles in quantum many-body systems, which typically relies on an embedded external symmetry breaking to the underlying system. An open question is how an intrinsic CCV mechanism could emerge and what its macroscopic consequences would be. We establish sublattice kinks in bipartite fermionic lattices as a concrete setup showing intrinsic CCV. The intrinsic CCV of the sublattice kink is based on the graph-topological nature of the underlying Hamiltonian, with no explicit symmetry breaking taking place. It leads to a population asymmetry of different configurations and imprints a hidden leaf-like structure in the eigenenergy spectrum. The population asymmetry also leads to an imbalanced sublattice-kink production triggered by the vacuum-instability in the quench dynamics. Our work demonstrates the graph topology as the microscopic origin of intrinsic CCV, with the population asymmetry as the macroscopic consequence, of which the proposed setup is highly amenable to experimental implementation via cold-atom quantum simulators.

</details>

### [153] [Observation of Strong $φ$-meson Directed Flow at High Baryon Density](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05694)
*The STAR Collaboration*

Main category: nucl-ex

TL;DR: STAR实验在RHIC上的金金对撞中首次观测到φ介子的大定向流，其大小与重子相当但远大于轻介子，表明φ介子主要通过高重重子共振态产生并受重子集体运动影响，为理解稠密QCD物质中的重子共振产生和奇异强子输运提供了新约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在重离子碰撞中，定向流（directed flow, $v_1$）对碰撞早期集体动力学敏感，而φ介子因其长寿命和弱相互作用，被视为探测稠密重子阶段集体动力学的理想探针。此前尚缺乏对φ介子定向流在中等能量区（高重子密度区域）的观测数据。

Method: 利用STAR实验在RHIC上采集的Au+Au对撞数据，测量了质心系能量$\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=3.0$–4.5 GeV（固定靶模式）和$\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=7.7$ GeV（对撞模式）下的φ介子定向流系数$v_1$，并与质子、Λ重子及$K^0_S$介子的结果进行对比，同时与强子输运（hadronic transport）计算结果进行比较。

Result: 首次观测到中等中心度Au+Au碰撞中φ介子具有显著的定向流；其$v_1$大小与质子和Λ重子相当，在最低能量下比$K^0_S$介子大3倍以上；中快度斜率$dv_1/dy$展现出与重子相似而不同于轻介子的强烈能量依赖性。

Conclusion: φ介子的定向流行为支持其通过高重重子共振态产生并受重子集体运动以及重子平均场相互作用（baryonic mean-field interactions）影响的图像。该结果为约束重子共振产生机制和奇异强子在稠密QCD物质中的输运动力学提供了新的实验依据。

Abstract: We report the first observation of a large directed flow ($v_1$) of $φ$ mesons in mid-central Au+Au collisions at $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=3.0$-4.5 GeV, together with the $\sqrt{s_{\mathrm{NN}}}=7.7$ GeV collider-energy result for the collision-energy dependence, measured by the STAR experiment at RHIC. Despite its mesonic nature, the $φ$-meson $v_{1}$ exhibits a magnitude comparable to that of protons and $Λ$ baryons, and is significantly larger (by a factor of $\gtrsim3$) than that of $K^0_S$ mesons at the lowest energies. The midrapidity slope $dv_1/dy$ shows a pronounced energy dependence similar to that observed for protons and $Λ$ baryons, in contrast to lighter mesons, in the high-baryon-density region. Comparisons with hadronic transport calculations indicate that the observed $φ$-meson directed flow is consistent with production via high-mass baryon resonances and the collective motion of baryons influenced by baryonic mean-field interactions. Due to its long lifetime and relatively weak effective $φ$-$N$ interaction, the $φ$ meson can retain sensitivity to collective dynamics established during the dense baryonic stage of the collision. These results provide new experimental constraints on baryon-resonance production and strange-hadron transport dynamics in dense QCD matter.

### [154] [BV construction of SUSY vertex algebras from SUSY factorization algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05706)
*Shintarou Yanagida*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文通过超对称（supersymmetric, SUSY）增强 Costello–Gwilliam 因子化代数（factorization algebras），在超 Riemann 面上构造了 $N=1$ SUSY 顶点代数，并证明了 SUSY 版本的提取定理（extraction theorem）。作为应用，在 BV 形式化中研究了全纯 sigma 模型，对于线性靶空间得到了自由 $bc$-$βγ$ 系统，对于一般复靶空间则识别出所得 SUSY 顶点代数与手征 de Rham 复形（chiral de Rham complex）等价；进一步表明，Ricci 平坦 Kähler 和 hyperkähler 靶空间分别诱导出 $N=2$ 和 $N=4$ 超对称增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将 Costello–Gwilliam 因子化代数框架推广到超对称情形，以在超 Riemann 面上系统构造超对称顶点代数（SUSY vertex algebra），并建立从几何数据到超对称代数的严格提取程序。

Method: 定义定义在嵌入 SUSY 圆盘上的 SUSY 因子化代数并施加自然对称条件，证明 SUSY 版本的 Costello–Gwilliam 提取定理，随后将结果应用于 BV 形式化（BV formalism）下的全纯 sigma 模型。

Result: 对线性靶空间，得到自由 $bc$-$βγ$ 系统并恢复其 SUSY 顶点代数结构；对一般复靶空间，证明通过坐标变换得到的 SUSY 顶点代数与手征 de Rham 复形同构；对 Ricci 平坦 Kähler 和 hyperkähler 靶空间，分别得到 $N=2$ 和 $N=4$ 超对称增强结构。

Conclusion: 建立了超对称因子化代数与 SUSY 顶点代数之间的严格对应，统一了若干已知超对称代数的几何构造，并为更一般的超对称量子场论（SUSY QFT）的代数形式化提供了框架。

Abstract: We construct $N=1$ supersymmetric (SUSY) vertex algebras from supersymmetric enhancements of Costello--Gwilliam factorization algebras on super Riemann surfaces. Introducing SUSY factorization algebras defined on embedded SUSY disks together with natural symmetry conditions, we prove a SUSY analogue of the Costello--Gwilliam extraction theorem. As an application, we study the holomorphic sigma model in the BV formalism. For a linear target, we obtain the free $bc$-$βγ$ system and recover its structure as a SUSY vertex algebra. For general complex targets, we describe the descent of the theory under coordinate changes and identify the resulting SUSY vertex algebra with the chiral de Rham complex. We further show that Ricci-flat Kähler and hyperkähler targets give rise to $N=2$ and $N=4$ supersymmetric enhancements introduced by Ben-Zvi--Heluani--Szczesny.

### [155] [Balanced tensor categories of representations of fixed-points conformal nets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06402)
*Adrià Marín-Salvador*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本论文证明，对于任意（未必有理的）共形网 (conformal net) $\mathcal{A}$，其上有限群 $G$ 的忠实作用导出的 $G$-交叉平衡 $\mathrm{W}^*$-张量范畴 (balanced $\mathrm{W}^*$-tensor category) $\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A})$ 的 $G$-等变范畴 (equivariantization) 与不动点共形网 $\mathcal{A}^G$ 的表示范畴 $\text{Rep}(\mathcal{A}^G)$ 之间存在平衡 $\mathrm{W}^*$-张量范畴等价，从而将先前对有理 (rational) 情况的编织张量范畴等价推广到非有理情形，并涵盖了平衡结构 (balance) 的对应关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将有理共形网 (rational conformal net) 情形下已知的编织张量范畴等价 $(\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A}))^G \cong \text{Rep}(\mathcal{A}^G)$（以局域化自同态语言表述于 arXiv:math/0403322）推广至非有理 (non-rational) 共形网情形，并纳入平衡结构 (balance) 的等价关系。

Method: 利用 arXiv:2606.03623 中引入的 $G$-交叉平衡 $\mathrm{W}^*$-张量范畴 (balanced $\mathrm{W}^*$-tensor category) $\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A})$ 框架，研究其 $G$-等变范畴 (equivariantization) 与不动点共形网表示范畴之间的等价性。

Result: 建立了 $(\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A}))^G \cong \text{Rep}(\mathcal{A}^G)$ 这一平衡 $\mathrm{W}^*$-张量范畴等价，该结果对非有理共形网也成立，并且包含平衡结构 (balance) 的对应。

Conclusion: 成功将有限群作用下的共形场论中 $G$-等变化与不动点子代数表示范畴之间的等价关系从有理情形推广到一般非有理情形，同时完善了平衡结构的对应性。

Abstract: Let $\mathcal{A}$ be a (not necessarily rational) conformal net with a faithful action of a finite group $G$. Let $\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A})$ be the $G$-crossed balanced $\mathrm{W}^*$-tensor category of $G$-twisted representations of $\mathcal{A}$ as introduced in arXiv:2606.03623. We show that there is an equivalence of balanced $\mathrm{W}^*$-tensor categories $(\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A}))^G\cong \text{Rep}(\mathcal{A}^G)$ between the $G$-equivariantization of $\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A})$ and the category of representations of the fixed-points conformal net $\mathcal{A}^G$. This generalizes to the non-rational case the equivalence of braided tensor categories $(\text{Rep}^G(\mathcal{A}))^G\cong \text{Rep}(\mathcal{A}^G)$ for $\mathcal{A}$ rational appearing (in the language of localized endomorphisms) in arXiv:math/0403322, and it also includes the balances.

### [156] [Quantitative eigenvector universality for generalized Wigner matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06419)
*Lucas Benigni*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的方法，用于研究广义Wigner矩阵的特征向量普适性（eigenvector universality），主要结果包括谱内任意位置的特征向量投影的渐近正态性，以及特征向量最大条目的定量下界。在光滑条目情形下，进一步得到了显式数量的特征向量投影的联合正态性，以及在Kolmogorov距离下的显式收敛速度。该方法基于对Dyson向量流（Dyson vector flow）的新分析，不依赖于特征向量矩流（eigenvector moment flow）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 特征向量普适性（eigenvector universality）是随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）的核心问题之一，其研究对于理解高维数据统计性质、量子混沌等领域具有重要意义。现有方法（如特征向量矩流）在处理某些情形时存在局限性，因此需要发展新的分析框架来克服这些限制。

Method: 提出了一种基于Dyson向量流（Dyson vector flow）的新分析方法，该方法不依赖传统的特征向量矩流（eigenvector moment flow），从而为特征向量普适性提供了新的技术途径。

Result: 1) 获得了谱内任意位置特征向量投影（eigenvector projections）的渐近正态性（asymptotic normality）；2) 给出了特征向量最大条目的定量下界；3) 在光滑条目情形下，得到了显式增长数量的特征向量投影的联合正态性（joint normality）；4) 在Kolmogorov距离（Kolmogorov distance）下获得了显式的收敛速度（explicit rate of convergence）。

Conclusion: 该工作为广义Wigner矩阵的特征向量普适性提供了一种不依赖于特征向量矩流的新方法，不仅扩展了已有结果的适用范围，还在光滑条目情形下给出了更精细的定量结果（如联合正态性和显式收敛速度），推动了随机矩阵理论中特征向量普适性的研究进展。

Abstract: We present a novel approach to eigenvector universality for generalized Wigner matrices. Our main consequences are asymptotic normality of joint eigenvector projections everywhere in the spectrum as well as a quantitative lower bound on the largest entry of an eigenvector. In the case of smooth entries, we are able to obtain joint normality of an explicit growing number of eigenvector projections, and we are also able to obtain an explicit rate of convergence in Kolmogorov distance. This is based on a new analysis of the Dyson vector flow which does not rely on the eigenvector moment flow.
