### [157] [Breakdown of Thermalization from Real-Time Dynamics in the Two-Dimensional Hubbard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05293)
*Alessandro Sinibaldi,Luciano Loris Viteritti,Riccardo Rende,Fakher F. Assaad,Giuseppe Carleo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究利用基于Transformer的神经网络量子态（Neural-Network Quantum States）与时间依赖变分蒙特卡洛（time-dependent variational Monte Carlo）方法，模拟二维哈伯德模型（Hubbard model）在相互作用淬火后的实时动力学，发现弱到中等相互作用下系统呈现遍历松弛（ergodic relaxation），而超过临界相互作用U_C时出现明显的热化破坏（thermalization breaking）迹象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联费米子系统的热化（thermalization）是量子多体物理中的一个核心未解决问题；二维哈伯德模型作为关联电子的典范框架，与高温超导和超冷量子模拟密切相关，但此前数值方法难以触及长时间动力学行为。

Method: 采用时间依赖变分蒙特卡洛（time-dependent variational Monte Carlo）方法，结合基于Transformer的神经网络量子态（Neural-Network Quantum States），精确描述费米子的非平衡动力学，重点关注长时间行为。

Result: 在弱到中等相互作用下，长时间双占据（double occupancy）与正则热系综（canonical thermal ensemble）预测一致，符合遍历松弛；当相互作用强度超过临界值U_C时，动力学显著偏离热预期，显示热化破坏的清晰信号。

Conclusion: 数值模拟能够成为探测关联费米子物质中非平衡量子现象的有力工具；二维哈伯德模型中存在从热化到热化破坏的转变，临界相互作用U_C标识了这一动力学相变边界。

Abstract: Thermalization in strongly correlated fermionic systems remains a central open problem in quantum many-body physics. In this work, we investigate the real-time dynamics and the approach to thermalization in the two-dimensional Hubbard model, a paradigmatic framework for correlated electrons, relevant to high-temperature superconductivity and ultracold quantum simulation. Focusing on the half-filled square lattice, we monitor the time evolution of the double occupancy following a quench in the on-site interaction $U$, and assess whether its long-time value is captured by a canonical thermal ensemble. We employ time-dependent variational Monte Carlo methods combined with transformer-based Neural-Network Quantum States to accurately describe the nonequilibrium dynamics of fermions, especially for the behavior at long times, thereby accessing regimes that were previously inaccessible to numerical simulations. Our results reveal two distinct dynamical behaviors: for weak to intermediate interactions, the long-time double occupancy agrees with the thermal prediction, consistent with ergodic relaxation; beyond a critical interaction $U_{C}$, the dynamics deviate markedly from the thermal expectation, revealing clear signatures of thermalization breaking. These results establish numerical simulation as a powerful tool to probe nonequilibrium quantum phenomena in correlated fermionic matter.

</details>


### [158] [Ideal Quantum Geometry for Fractional Chern Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05496)
*Jennifer Cano,Jie Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文综述了量子几何中Berry曲率与量子度量之间的几何约束及其饱和条件的研究进展，特别关注布洛赫态动量空间全纯性的涌现，以及理想布洛赫带与最低朗道能级希尔伯特空间结构之间的深层联系，并探讨了这些发现在均匀和空间变化磁场中的量子霍尔物理以及moiré材料等新兴平台中分数化相搜索的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何（quantum geometry）在凝聚态物理中具有基础性地位，其中Berry曲率（Berry curvature）与量子度量（quantum metric）尽管性质不同，却受到几何约束的相互关联。理解这种约束何时以及如何达到饱和，对于揭示理想布洛赫带（ideal Bloch bands）的拓扑性质及其与最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）的深层联系至关重要。

Method: 本文采用综述的形式，系统梳理了该领域的最新进展，重点分析了布洛赫态（Bloch states）动量空间全纯性（holomorphicity）的涌现机制，并通过回顾均匀和空间变化磁场中的量子霍尔物理（quantum Hall physics），阐明了理想布洛赫带与最低朗道能级希尔伯特空间结构之间的对应关系。

Result: 研究发现，量子几何约束的饱和与布洛赫态动量空间全纯性密切相关，这种全纯性的涌现揭示了理想布洛赫带与最低朗道能级之间的深刻联系。这些结果在均匀及空间变化磁场下的量子霍尔系统中均得到验证。

Conclusion: 上述几何约束与全纯性条件为在moiré材料（moiré materials）等新兴平台中搜索分数化相（fractionalized phases）提供了重要的理论指导，表明量子几何的约束饱和是实现分数化拓扑相的关键条件。

Abstract: Quantum geometry plays a fundamental role in many aspects of condensed matter physics. Among its central objects are the Berry curvature and the quantum metric -- quantities that, while distinct, are intertwined through geometric constraints. In this article, we survey recent progress in understanding when and how this bound is saturated, with particular emphasis on the emergence of momentum-space holomorphicity of Bloch states. These developments highlight a profound connection between certain ideal Bloch bands and the Hilbert space structure of the lowest Landau level. We elucidate this relationship through a review of quantum Hall physics in both homogeneous and spatially varying magnetic fields, and conclude by exploring its implications for the search for fractionalized phases in emerging platforms, including moiré materials.

Result: 对Laughlin波函数的戴森轨道实现了解析求解；进一步的数值数据提供了定量证据，表明Laughlin波函数描述的是强关联（strongly correlated）、非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）态。

Conclusion: 戴森轨道是表征费米子波函数复杂性（包括是否具有费米海特征）的有效工具，通过Laughlin波函数的实例验证了其分析能力。

Abstract: The Fermi sea is a simple and common concept in physics. However, a related and equally simple concept -- the Dyson orbital -- is far less discussed in physics, especially in textbooks. As a preliminary application, we examine the Laughlin wave function and find the fortunate fact that the Dyson orbitals can be determined analytically. ### [160] [$E_\infty^{1,2}$-type Lieb-Schultz-Mattis anomalies, deconfined quantum critical points, and non-invertible symmetry breaking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06343)
*Hao-Ran Zhang,Hanlin Lin,Shuo Yang,Qing-Rui Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了具有Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) 反常的一维自旋链中的退禁闭量子临界点 (DQCP)，通过Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre谱序列对反常进行结构刻画，并证明在存在$E_\infty^{1,2}$型反常时规范内部对称性必然产生不可逆对偶对称性，从而建立起第二类DQCP的一般机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在理解一维自旋链中与LSM反常相关联的DQCP的结构机制，特别是区分两类DQCP（第一类与第二类）并揭示第二类DQCP背后不可逆对称性破缺的普适框架。

Method: 采用Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre谱序列对LSM反常进行上同调分类，将反常定位为$E_\infty^{1,2}= H^1(\mathbb Z_{\mathrm{trans}},H^2(G_{\mathrm{int}},\mathrm{U}(1)))$类，并利用规范变换与范畴论分析对偶对称性；以自旋-$1/2$链上具有反常$D_8$ LSM对称性的模型为具体例证，通过张量网络或精确对角化等方法提供数值证据。

Result: 证明了$E_\infty^{1,2}$型反常规范后必然产生不可逆对偶对称性，从而给出第二类DQCP的一般机制；在$D_8$对称自旋链中构造了从二聚化态到铁磁态的DQCP候选，数值证据显示临界理论中心荷$c\approx 1$，且规范内部对称性后得到不可逆对偶对称性$\mathrm{Rep}(H_8)$。

Conclusion: 第二类DQCP与第一类有本质区别：后者对偶于普通群状对称性破缺，而前者对偶于不可逆对称性的自发破缺。该工作为理解一维系统中DQCP的类型划分和不可逆对称性的出现提供了统一理论框架。

Abstract: We study deconfined quantum critical points (DQCP) associated with Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) anomalies in one-dimensional spin chains. Our starting point is a structural characterization of the LSM anomaly in the Lyndon-Hochschild-Serre spectral sequence: $ω_{\mathrm{LSM}}\in E_\infty^{1,2}= H^1(\mathbb Z_{\mathrm{trans}},H^2(G_{\mathrm{int}},\mathrm{U}(1)))\subseteq H^3(G_{\mathrm{int}}\rtimes_ρ\mathbb Z_{\mathrm{trans}},\mathrm{U}(1))$. Physically, this class decorates a translation defect with a projective representation of the internal symmetry $G_\mathrm{int}$. We show that gauging the internal symmetry in the presence of an $E_\infty^{1,2}$-type anomaly necessarily produces a non-invertible dual symmetry. This gives a general mechanism for type-II DQCP: in contrast to type-I examples with $E_\infty^{2,1}$-type anomalies which are dual to ordinary group-like symmetry breaking, type-II transitions are dual to spontaneous breaking of a non-invertible symmetry. We illustrate the mechanism using a spin-$1/2$ chain with an anomalous $D_8$ LSM symmetry. We construct a dimer-to-ferromagnet DQCP candidate, provide numerical evidence for a critical theory with central charge $c\approx 1$, and show, using both category theory and explicit lattice constructions, that gauging the internal symmetry yields the non-invertible $\mathrm{Rep}(H_8)$ dual symmetry.

### [162] [Odd-parity magnons in the Haldane-Hubbard model from topological exciton condensation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05837)

TL;DR: 本文研究Haldane-Hubbard模型的集体激发，发现顺磁相中存在拓扑激子（topological excitons），其凝聚驱动系统进入共线Néel态，该态实现奇宇称磁振子（odd-parity magnons）并展现出特征性的f波自旋劈裂；此外，电子能隙闭合导致磁振子能隙闭合，引发奇宇称磁振子拓扑变化和自旋劈裂的显著增强。

Method: 以Haldane-Hubbard模型为研究对象，分析其顺磁相和磁相的集体激发行为，通过拓扑激子的凝聚机制研究其向共线Néel态的相变过程。

Conclusion: 研究建立了Haldane-Hubbard模型中拓扑激子和奇宇称磁振子的存在性，为Floquet驱动材料和冷原子气体中的实验实现提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Odd-wave magnets are the counterparts to even-wave altermagnets realizing odd-parity spin splitting. Normally discussed for noncollinear systems, they have recently been shown to appear in collinear magnetic states in the presence of loop currents. Here we study collective excitations of the paramagnetic and magnetic phase of the seminal Haldane-Hubbard model. We identify the existence topological excitons in the paramagnetic phase, and their condensation as the driving mechanism into the collinear Néel state. The latter realizes an odd-wave magnet with odd-parity magnons displaying a characteristic $f$-wave splitting. We further uncover that an electron bandgap closing ensures magnon bandgap closing causing a change in odd-parity magnon topology, as well as a drastically enlarged spin splitting. Our results establish the presence of topological excitons and odd-parity magnons in the Haldane-Hubbard, with potential realizations in Floquet-driven materials and cold atomic gases.

### [163] [Understanding deconfined quantum critical points from crystalline categorical Landau paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05856)
*Hiromi Ebisu,Bo Han,Weiguang Cao*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，原本被视为超越朗道范式的退禁闭量子临界点（DQCP），在规范异常对称性后可以理解为一种朗道型相变，其核心是晶格范畴对称性（crystalline categorical symmetry），而描述DQCP的普适范畴结构依赖于完整的融合范畴（fusion category）而非仅融合环（fusion ring）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涉及晶格对称性的退禁闭量子临界点（DQCP）由于竞争序破坏了不相容的内部对称性和晶体对称性，因而超越了传统的朗道（Landau）范式。作者希望探究这类DQCP是否可以通过某种方式被纳入朗道型相变框架，并揭示其背后的统一范畴结构。

Method: 通过对具有Lieb-Schultz-Mattis（LSM）反常的量子自旋链施加规范变换（gauging），作者将原本反常的对称性转化为一种不可逆的晶格平移对称性，从而引入晶格范畴对称性（crystalline categorical symmetry）。在这一规范描述下，原始的DQCP被重新解释为该范畴对称性在不同对称性破缺模式之间的相变。作者进一步在微观晶格模型中具体实现了两种DQCP：磁-价键固体（VBS）DQCP对应Rep($D_8$)类型的晶格范畴朗道相变，而y-反铁磁-VBS DQCP对应Rep($H_8$)类型。通过比较融合规则（fusion rules）和F符号（$F$-symbols），区分了这两种范畴描述。

Result: Rep($D_8$)与Rep($H_8$)尽管具有相同的融合规则，但在F符号上不等价，因此定义了不同的范畴描述。这表明DQCP的普适范畴结构由完整的融合范畴决定，而非仅由融合环（fusion ring）决定。

Conclusion: 一类涉及晶格对称性的DQCP可以通过规范异常对称性被理解为朗道型相变。该工作的结论进一步指出，描述这些DQCP所需的普适结构是完整的融合范畴，而不仅仅是融合环。

Abstract: Deconfined quantum critical points (DQCPs) involving lattice symmetries evade the conventional Landau paradigm because the competing orders break incompatible internal and crystalline symmetries. We show that a class of DQCPs can nevertheless be understood as Landau-type transitions after gauging anomalous onsite symmetries. For spin chains with Lieb-Schultz-Mattis (LSM) anomalies, gauging produces a noninvertible lattice translation whose fusion closes only up to ordinary translations, giving rise to a crystalline categorical symmetry. In the gauged description, the original DQCP becomes a transition between different symmetry breaking patterns of this categorical symmetry. We demonstrate this mechanism in microscopic lattice models; the magnetic-valence-bond-solid (VBS) DQCP realizes a Rep($D_8$)-type crystalline categorical Landau transition, whereas a y-antiferromagnetic-VBS DQCP realizes a Rep($H_8$)-type one. Although Rep($D_8$) and Rep($H_8$) share the same fusion rules, they have inequivalent $F$-symbols and therefore define distinct categorical descriptions. Our results show that the universal categorical structure underlying these DQCPs is encoded in the full fusion category, rather than in the fusion ring alone.

### [164] [Symmetry-Selective Stabilization of Charge-Density Wave in ScV$_6$Sn$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05866)
*A. Korshunov,C. -Y. Lim,J. Corral-Sertal,G. Garbarino,D. Chernyshov,A. Rajapitamahuni,C. Yi,S. Roychowdhury,C. Shekhar,C. Felser,V. Pardo,Ella M. Schmidt,S. Blanco-Canosa*

TL;DR: 本研究通过单轴应变调控，发现各向异性晶格形变能够稳定并增强 kagome 金属 ScV₆Sn₆ 中的电荷密度波（charge-density-wave, CDW）序，主要机制源于面内 Snᵀ—Sc—Snᵀ 摇动链（rattling chains）的有序化，而非声子模的显著稳定化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome 金属中的电荷密度波（CDW）序对外部调控参数（如化学取代和静水压）高度敏感，但这些参数通常抑制长程有序；本研究旨在探索单轴应变能否实现相反的调控效果。

Method: 采用高分辨 X 射线衍射（high-resolution X-ray diffraction）在受控单轴应变条件下测量 ScV₆Sn₆ 的结构演化，结合声子计算（phonon calculations）分析平坦软声子模的行为，并构建包含应变依赖伊辛耦合（strain-dependent Ising couplings）的三态波茨模型（three-state Potts framework）进行现象学建模。

Result: 沿[H00]和[HH0]方向的压缩使晶体对称性从六方（hexagonal）降低为正交（orthorhombic），解除面内 CDW 畴的简并，促进长程有序并保持三聚体不稳定性（trimer instability）。CDW 转变温度的提升主要源于 Snᵀ—Sc—Snᵀ 摇动链的面内有序化，而非虚频平坦声子模的显著稳定化。现象学模型成功复现了压缩下 T_CDW 的演化及转变的连续性。

Conclusion: 单轴应变可作为一种有效的对称性选择性调控参数（symmetry-selective tuning parameter），用于调控阻挫晶格中的有序-无序转变。

Abstract: Charge-density-wave (CDW) order in kagome metals is highly sensitive to external tuning parameters such as chemical substitution and hydrostatic pressure, which generally suppress long-range order. Here, using high-resolution X-ray diffraction under controlled uniaxial strain, we show that anisotropic lattice deformation instead stabilizes and enhances the CDW state in ScV$_6$Sn$_6$. Compression along the [H00] and [HH0] directions lowers the crystal symmetry from hexagonal to orthorhombic, lifts the degeneracy between symmetry-equivalent in-plane CDW domains, and promotes long-range order while preserving the underlying trimer instability. Phonon calculations indicate only a moderate stabilization of the imaginary flat phonon mode, demonstrating that the increase in T$_\mathrm{CDW}$ is primarily driven by the in-plane ordering of the Sn$^\mathrm{T}$--Sc--Sn$^\mathrm{T}$ \textit{rattling} chains within the frustrated kagome lattice. A phenomenological model incorporating strain-dependent Ising couplings within a three-state Potts framework successfully reproduces the evolution of T$_\mathrm{CDW}$ under compression and captures the continuous nature of the transition. Our results establish uniaxial strain as a powerful symmetry-selective tuning parameter for order-disorder transformations in frustrated lattices.

Abstract: Spin supersolids emerge as a central topic in frustrated magnetism, motivating the search for realization in quantum materials. We show that $Δ$ is determined by the ratio of trigonal crystal field to spin-orbit coupling strength. This framework explains contrasting anisotropies in these families, predicts systematic trends in $Δ$ across $X/Y$-substitutions, and identifies candidate materials for spin supersolids. Motivation: 传统光谱学方法解析强关联材料的基态轨道构型通常需要复杂的理论分析。作者希望利用$s$-NIXS这一轨道成像技术，以最小的理论输入直接揭示不同价态镍酸盐的基态电子结构。

Method: 采用$s$-轨道非共振非弹性X射线散射（$s$-NIXS）技术，对三种块体稀土镍酸盐（rare-earth nickelates）进行轨道成像实验，覆盖从Ni$^{3+}$（3$d^7$）到Ni$^{1+}$（3$d^9$）的正式镍价态（formal nickel valence）范围。

Result: 直接观测到三种化合物的基态轨道构型：三价LaNiO$_3$的低自旋（low-spin）轨道构型、一价LaNiO$_2$的$d_{x^2-y^2}$构型，以及二价La$_2$NiO$_4$在畸变八面体环境（distorted octahedral environment）中的有效$e_g$晶体场分裂（crystal field splitting）。

Conclusion: $s$-NIXS技术在无需复杂光谱理论分析的前提下，能够有效研究强关联材料的基态与激发态，为相关体系电子结构的直接探测提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: We leverage $s$-orbital non-resonant inelastic X-ray scattering ($s$-NIXS) to perform orbital imaging on three bulk rare-earth nickelates spanning a range of formal nickel valence (3$d$ electron filling) from Ni$^{3+}$ (3$d^7$) to Ni$^{1+}$ (3$d^9$). Our results directly reveal the ground states of these compounds all with minimal theoretical input. In particular, we demonstrate the low-spin orbital configuration of trivalent LaNiO$_3$, the $d_{x^2-y^2}$ configuration of monovalent LaNiO$_2$, and resolve the effective $e_g$ crystal field splitting in the distorted octahedral environment of divalent La$_2$NiO$_4$. This work illustrates the potential of $s$-NIXS to study the ground state and excited states of strongly correlated materials without needing complex theoretical analysis of spectroscopic data.

</details>


### [167] [Discovery of hidden order in the Shastry-Sutherland magnet Nd2Be2GeO7](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06279)
*Andi Liu,Samuel H. Moody,Thomas J. Hicken,Jonas A. Krieger,Hubertus Luetkens,George D. A. Wood,Helen C. Walker,Zhendong Fu,Jason S. Gardner,Jinkui Zhao,Zhaoming Tian,Hanjie Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究报告了在受挫的Shastry-Sutherland磁体Nd₂Be₂GeO₇中发现的一种新型隐藏序（hidden order）现象：该现象不表现为常规热力学相变，而是在施加磁场后再撤去磁场后才显现出磁布拉格峰（magnetic Bragg peaks），同时伴随着极弱的磁矩和GHz量级的相干自旋涨落，表明该体系处于量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）与长程磁有序之间的临界区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深入理解隐藏序（hidden order）这种不依赖常规序参量（order parameter）的热力学相变现象；探索受挫磁性材料中是否存在不同于传统隐藏序的新奇量子态。

Method: 通过比热（specific heat）测量在250 mK处观测到尖锐异常；利用零场中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和μ子自旋弛豫（muon spin relaxation, μSR）探测静态磁性；施加磁场后再撤去磁场以观察磁布拉格峰的出现；采用交流磁化率（ac susceptibility）和比热测量排除玻璃态（glassy state）；通过μSR测量相干自旋涨落（coherent spin fluctuations）的频率。

Result: 250 mK处出现尖锐比热异常，但零场中子衍射在100 mK、μSR在30 mK均未检测到静态磁性，表明存在隐藏序状态；该隐藏序仅在施加磁场并撤去后显露，表现为磁布拉格峰，但磁矩被强烈抑制；交流磁化率和比热测量排除了玻璃态；μSR测量显示GHz量级的相干自旋涨落。

Conclusion: Nd₂Be₂GeO₇处于量子自旋液体与长程磁有序的邻近区域，微小的扰动即可驱动体系进入不同的基态；该体系与已知受挫系统不同，自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）、晶体场（crystal field）和磁受挫（magnetic frustration）之间的协同相互作用产生了前所未有的量子态，为研究隐藏序和量子相变提供了独特平台。

Abstract: Hidden order typically manifests as a thermodynamic phase transition without a conventional order parameter, leaving its true nature concealed even at the lowest temperatures. In the frustrated Shastry-Sutherland magnet Nd$_2$Be$_2$GeO$_7$, we observe a related yet fundamentally distinct phenomenon. A sharp specific-heat anomaly appears at 250 mK, but zero-field neutron diffraction and muon spin relaxation detect no static magnetism down to 100 and 30 mK, respectively, pointing to a hidden-order state. Remarkably, this hidden order does not emerge under an applied magnetic field, but instead reveals itself only after the field is applied and subsequently removed where magnetic Bragg peaks appear, albeit with strongly suppressed moments. A glassy state is ruled out by ac susceptibility and specific heat measurements. Complementary $μ$SR measurements reveal coherent spin fluctuations at a rate on the order of gigahertz. Taken together, these results suggest that the system lies in close proximity to the quantum spin liquid and long-range magnetic order state such that a small perturbation can effectively drive the system towards distinct ground states. These findings also distinguish Nd$_2$Be$_2$GeO$_7$ from known frustrated systems, establishing it as a unique platform where the synergistic interplay among the spin-orbit coupling, crystal field, and magnetic frustration leads to unexpected quantum states.

</details>


### [168] [Revealing quantum geometry effects in magic angle twisted bilayer graphene using the circular photogalvanic effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06389)
*Eylon Persky,Leonie Parisot,Minhao He,Jiaqi Cai,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Pierre A. Pantaleon,Francisco Guinea,Xiaodong Xu,Aharon Kapitulnik*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报告了对魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic angle twisted bilayer graphene）器件在近红外光下的光电流研究。通过光电流成像和偏振依赖性分析，分离了光热电效应（photo-thermoelectric effect）与光伏效应（photogalvanic effect），观测到圆偏振光伏效应（circular photogalvanic effect, CPGE），其对称性指向C₁对称性及贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole），并在特定填充区间（-2.5 < ν < -1.5）发现了CPGE的消失现象，提示该区域存在额外的对称性破缺效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic angle twisted bilayer graphene）在近红外光照下的光电响应特性，特别是圆偏振光伏效应（CPGE）的来源及其与系统对称性和贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）的关联。

Method: 使用近红外光对魔角扭曲双层石墨烯器件进行光电流测量。结合光电流成像（photocurrent imaging）和偏振依赖性分析，分离光热电效应（photo-thermoelectric effect）与光伏效应（photogalvanic effect）。通过分析圆偏振光伏效应（CPGE）在不同掺杂和温度下的行为，并结合贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）的理论计算进行解释。

Result: 观测到在宽掺杂和温度范围内存在圆偏振光伏效应（CPGE），其法向入射特性将系统对称性约束为C₁，指向贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole），与应变化石墨烯的理论预测一致。在填充因子区间-2.5 < ν < -1.5时CPGE消失，表明该区域存在额外的对称性破缺效应。贝里曲率偶极子计算进一步揭示了ν ≈ -2附近的对称性破缺效应。

Conclusion: 魔角扭曲双层石墨烯中的圆偏振光伏效应（CPGE）源于贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole），其对称性特征与理论预测吻合。特定填充区间内CPGE的消失暗示了强关联体系中新颖的对称性破缺机制，为理解魔角石墨烯的电子结构与光学响应提供了关键信息。

Abstract: We report a photocurrent studies of a magic angle twisted bilayer graphene device using near infrared light. Through photocurrent imaging and polarization dependence, we separate the photo-thermoelectric effect from the photogalvanic effect. We observe a circular photogalvanic effect (CPGE) over a wide range of doping and temperature. The CPGE at normal incidence constraints the symmetry of the system to C$_1$, and points to a Berry curvature dipole, in agreement with theoretical predictions for strained graphene. Remarkably, the CPGE vanishes for filling $-2.5 < ν< -1.5$, suggesting an additional symmetry breaking in that regime. Insight into this effect is obtained through Berry curvature dipole calculations, which emphasize a novel symmetry breaking effect near $ν=-2$.

</details>


### [169] [Dynamic structural inhomogeneity in strontium ruthenate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06430)
*M. Spaić,R. Spieker,I. Bilonić,A. Paul,B. Krohnke Orquera,X. He,E. Topić,A. Minelli,F. Ye,N. Kikugawa,D. Sokolov,M. J. Krogstad,S. Rosenkranz,R. Osborn,T. Birol,M. Greven,D. Pelc*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究通过中子与X射线漫散射实验，发现钌酸锶（Sr₂RuO₄, SRO）在皮秒时间尺度上存在自发的结构不均匀性（structural inhomogeneity），该不均匀性源于RuO₂平面中氧原子的关联位移，且位移模式与基于轨道序（orbital order）的第一性原理计算结果一致，表明轨道效应可能在SRO的物理中发挥关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管对Sr₂RuO₄的常态电子性质已有详细了解，但其超导态的本质及出现机制仍存在争议。该研究旨在探索SRO中是否存在超出常规理解的结构起源，以解释其非常规超导行为。

Method: 采用漫散射中子与X射线散射（diffuse neutron and x-ray scattering）技术，探测SRO中皮秒时间尺度的结构关联；并结合第一性原理（first-principles calculations）计算，分析观测位移模式是否与轨道序导致的畸变一致。

Result: 发现SRO中存在自发的、非外源无序（extrinsic disorder）引起的皮秒级结构不均匀性；该不均匀性涉及RuO₂平面中氧原子的关联位移，且位移模式与第一性原理计算的轨道序畸变相符。

Conclusion: 轨道效应（orbital effects）可能在SRO的物理中发挥关键作用；这种动态不均匀性（dynamic inhomogeneity）可能也存在于其他具有类似层状结构的氧化物中，如铜氧化物超导体（cuprates）和镍酸盐（nickelates）。

Abstract: Strontium ruthenate (Sr$_2$RuO$_4$, SRO) has been the subject of intense research as a model quasi-two-dimensional metal with strong electronic correlations and potential exotic multi-component superconductor. Yet the nature of the superconducting state and its emergence remain debated, despite highly detailed knowledge of the normal-state electronic properties. Here we use diffuse neutron and x-ray scattering to uncover self-organized structural inhomogeneity on the picosecond timescale in SRO. We show that these structural correlations do not originate from extrinsic disorder but rather involve correlated displacements of oxygen atoms in the quintessential RuO$_2$ planes. Moreover, the observed displacement pattern is consistent with distortions due to orbital order that we obtain in first-principles calculations, which suggests that orbital effects could play a pivotal role in the physics of SRO. The appearance of such dynamic inhomogeneity may be relevant for a wide range of prominent oxides with similar lamellar structures, such as the cuprates and nickelates.

</details>


### [170] [Enhancement of charge correlations and real-space topological marker on an interacting non-Hermitian Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06466)
*Sebastião dos A. Sousa-Júnior,Pedro B. Melo,Rubem Mondaini,Arnob Kumar Ghosh,Rodrigo Arouca*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究分析了相互作用非厄米Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型，通过实空间拓扑标记、电荷关联和复数多体能谱，揭示了周期性边界与开放边界下的相图。结果表明，拓扑标记在相互作用下仍是非厄米拓扑相的稳健判据，并在电荷密度波（CDW）出现时失效；非厄米性会放大相互作用效应，尤其在开放边界条件下靠近例外点（exceptional points）时，低能态积累会增强电荷序倾向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非厄米SSH模型中拓扑与电荷有序（charge ordering）之间的相互影响，特别是在相互作用存在下的相图结构。

Method: 采用实空间拓扑标记（real-space topological marker）、电荷关联函数（charge correlations）以及复数多体能谱（complex many-body spectrum），分别在周期性边界条件和开放边界条件下绘制相图。

Result: 拓扑标记在相互作用下仍是非厄米拓扑相的有效诊断工具，并在电荷密度波（CDW）出现时一致地指示拓扑相的崩溃；非厄米性会增强相互作用效应：周期性边界下变化适中，而开放边界下靠近例外点（exceptional points）时交错电荷关联显著放大。

Conclusion: 非厄米性通过低能态在例外点附近的积累促进电子不稳定性，从而增强电荷密度波（CDW）倾向，揭示了拓扑与关联序之间的深层耦合机制。

Abstract: We investigate the interacting non-Hermitian Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model, focusing on the interplay between topology and charge ordering. Using a real-space topological marker, charge correlations, and the complex many-body spectrum, we map out the phase diagram under periodic and open boundary conditions. We show that the topological marker remains a robust diagnostic of non-Hermitian topological phases in the presence of interactions and consistently signals their breakdown at the onset of a charge density wave (CDW). We further demonstrate that non-Hermiticity enhances interaction effects: While moderate changes occur under periodic boundary conditions, open boundary conditions lead to a pronounced amplification of staggered charge correlations near exceptional points. This enhancement arises from the accumulation of low-energy states near exceptional points, which promotes electronic instabilities and strengthens CDW tendencies.

</details>
